------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Douay-Rheims Bible: Psalms

<span id="an_1:1">1:1</span> Blessed is the man who hath not walked in
the counsel of the ungodly, nor stood in the way of sinners, nor sat in
the chair of pestilence.

<span id="an_1:2">1:2</span> But his will is in the law of the Lord, and
on his law he shall meditate day and night.

<span id="an_1:3">1:3</span> And he shall be like a tree which is
planted near the running waters, which shall bring forth its fruit, in
due season. And his leaf shall not fall off: and all whosoever he shall
do shall prosper.

<span id="an_1:4">1:4</span> Not so the wicked, not so: but like the
dust, which the wind driveth from the face of the earth.

<span id="an_1:5">1:5</span> Therefore the wicked shall not rise again
in judgment: nor sinners in the council of the just.

<span id="an_1:6">1:6</span> For the Lord knoweth the way of the just:
and the way of the wicked shall perish.

<span id="an_2:1">2:1</span> Why have the Gentiles raged, and the people
devised vain things?

<span id="an_2:2">2:2</span> The kings of the earth stood up, and the
princes met together, against the Lord and against his Christ.

<span id="an_2:3">2:3</span> Let us break their bonds asunder: and let
us cast away their yoke from us.

<span id="an_2:4">2:4</span> He that dwelleth in heaven shall laugh at
them: and the Lord shall deride them.

<span id="an_2:5">2:5</span> Then shall he speak to them in his anger,
and trouble them in his rage.

<span id="an_2:6">2:6</span> But I am appointed king by him over Sion
his holy mountain, preaching his commandment.

<span id="an_2:7">2:7</span> The Lord hath said to me: Thou art my son,
this day have I begotten thee.

<span id="an_2:8">2:8</span> Ask of me, and I will give thee the
Gentiles for thy inheritance, and the utmost parts of the earth for thy
possession.

<span id="an_2:9">2:9</span> Thou shalt rule them with a rod of iron,
and shalt break them in pieces like a potter's vessel.

<span id="an_2:10">2:10</span> And now, O ye kings, understand: receive
instruction, you that judge the earth.

<span id="an_2:11">2:11</span> Serve ye the Lord with fear: and rejoice
unto him with trembling.

<span id="an_2:12">2:12</span> Embrace discipline, lest at any time the
Lord be angry, and you perish from the just way.

<span id="an_2:13">2:13</span> When his wrath shall be kindled in a
short time, blessed are all they that trust in him.

<span id="an_3:1">3:1</span> The psalm of David when he fled from the
face of his son Absalom.

<span id="an_3:2">3:2</span> Why, O Lord, are they multiplied that
afflict me? many are they who rise up against me.

<span id="an_3:3">3:3</span> Many say to my soul: There is no salvation
for him in his God.

<span id="an_3:4">3:4</span> But thou, O Lord art my protector, my
glory, and the lifter up of my head.

<span id="an_3:5">3:5</span> I have cried to the Lord with my voice: and
he hath heard me from his holy hill.

<span id="an_3:6">3:6</span> I have slept and taken my rest: and I have
risen up, because the Lord hath protected me.

<span id="an_3:7">3:7</span> I will not fear thousands of the people,
surrounding me: arise, O Lord; save me, O my God.

<span id="an_3:8">3:8</span> For thou hast struck all them who are my
adversaries without cause: thou hast broken the teeth of sinners.

<span id="an_3:9">3:9</span> Salvation is of the Lord: and thy blessing
is upon thy people.

<span id="an_4:1">4:1</span> Unto the end, in verses. A psalm of David.

<span id="an_4:2">4:2</span> When I called upon him, the God of my
justice heard me: when I was in distress, thou hast enlarged me. Have
mercy on me: and hear my prayer.

<span id="an_4:3">4:3</span> O ye sons of men, how long will you be dull
of heart? why do you love vanity, and seek after lying?

<span id="an_4:4">4:4</span> Know ye also that the Lord hath made his
holy one wonderful: the Lord will hear me when I shall cry unto him.

<span id="an_4:5">4:5</span> Be angry, and sin not: the things you say
in your hearts, be sorry for them upon your beds.

<span id="an_4:6">4:6</span> Offer up the sacrifice of justice, and
trust in the Lord: many say, Who sheweth us good things?

<span id="an_4:7">4:7</span> The light of thy countenance O Lord, is
signed upon us: thou hast given gladness in my heart.

<span id="an_4:8">4:8</span> By the fruit of their corn, their wine and
oil, they are multiplied.

<span id="an_4:9">4:9</span> In peace in the selfsame I will sleep, and
I will rest:

<span id="an_4:10">4:10</span> for thou, O Lord, singularly hast settled
me in hope.

<span id="an_5:1">5:1</span> Unto the end, for her that obtaineth the
inheritance. A psalm of David.

<span id="an_5:2">5:2</span> Give ear, O Lord, to my words, understand
my cry.

<span id="an_5:3">5:3</span> Hearken to the voice of my prayer, O my
King and my God.

<span id="an_5:4">5:4</span> For to thee will I pray: O Lord, in the
morning thou shalt hear my voice.

<span id="an_5:5">5:5</span> In the morning I will stand before thee,
and will see: because thou art not a God that willest iniquity.

<span id="an_5:6">5:6</span> Neither shall the wicked dwell near thee:
nor shall the unjust abide before thy eyes.

<span id="an_5:7">5:7</span> Thou hatest all the workers of iniquity:
Thou wilt destroy all that speak a lie. The bloody and the deceitful man
the Lord will abhor.

<span id="an_5:8">5:8</span> But as for me in the multitude of thy
mercy, I will come into thy house; I will worship towards thy holy
temple, in thy fear.

<span id="an_5:9">5:9</span> Conduct me, O Lord, in thy justice: because
of my enemies, direct my way in thy sight.

<span id="an_5:10">5:10</span> for there is no truth in their mouth;
their heart is vain.

<span id="an_5:11">5:11</span> Their throat is an open sepulchre: they
dealt deceitfully with their tongues: judge them, O God. Let them fall
from their devices: according to the multitude of their wickedness cast
them out: for they have provoked thee, O Lord.

<span id="an_5:12">5:12</span> But let all them be glad that hope in
thee: they shall rejoice for ever, and thou shalt dwell in them. And all
they that love thy name shall glory in thee:

<span id="an_5:13">5:13</span> For thou wilt bless the just. O Lord,
thou hast crowned us, as with a shield of thy good will.

<span id="an_6:1">6:1</span> Unto the end, in verses, a psalm for David,
for the octave.

<span id="an_6:2">6:2</span> O Lord, rebuke me not in thy indignation,
nor chastise me in thy wrath.

<span id="an_6:3">6:3</span> Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I am weak:
heal me, O Lord, for my bones are troubled.

<span id="an_6:4">6:4</span> And my soul is troubled exceedingly: but
thou, O Lord, how long?

<span id="an_6:5">6:5</span> Turn to me, O Lord, and deliver my soul: O
save me for thy mercy's sake.

<span id="an_6:6">6:6</span> For there is no one in death, that is
mindful of thee: and who shall confess to thee in hell?

<span id="an_6:7">6:7</span> I have laboured in my groanings, every
night I will wash my bed: I will water my couch with my tears.

<span id="an_6:8">6:8</span> My eye is troubled through indignation: I
have grown old amongst all my enemies.

<span id="an_6:9">6:9</span> Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity:
for the Lord hath heard the voice of my weeping.

<span id="an_6:10">6:10</span> The Lord hath heard my supplication: the
Lord hath received my prayer.

<span id="an_6:11">6:11</span> Let all my enemies be ashamed, and be
very much troubled: let them be turned back, and be ashamed very
speedily.

<span id="an_7:1">7:1</span> The psalm of David which he sung to the
Lord for the words of Chusi the son of Jemini. \[2 Kings 16.\]

<span id="an_7:2">7:2</span> O Lord my God, in thee have I put my trust:
save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me.

<span id="an_7:3">7:3</span> Lest at any time he seize upon my soul like
a lion, while there is no one to redeem me, nor to save.

<span id="an_7:4">7:4</span> O Lord my God, if I have done this thing,
if there be iniquity in my hands:

<span id="an_7:5">7:5</span> If I have rendered to them that repaid me
evils, let me deservedly fall empty before my enemies.

<span id="an_7:6">7:6</span> Let the enemy pursue my soul, and take it,
and tread down my life on the earth, and bring down my glory to the
dust.

<span id="an_7:7">7:7</span> Rise up, O Lord, in thy anger: and be thou
exalted in the borders of my enemies. And arise, O Lord my God, in the
precept which thou hast commanded:

<span id="an_7:8">7:8</span> and a congregation of people shall surround
thee. And for their sakes return thou on high.

<span id="an_7:9">7:9</span> The Lord judgeth the people. Judge me, O
Lord, according to my justice, and according to my innocence in me.

<span id="an_7:10">7:10</span> The wickedness of sinners shall be
brought to nought: and thou shalt direct the just: the searcher of
hearts and reins is God.

<span id="an_7:11">7:11</span> Just is my help from the Lord: who saveth
the upright of heart.

<span id="an_7:12">7:12</span> God is a just judge, strong and patient:
is he angry every day?

<span id="an_7:13">7:13</span> Except you will be converted, he will
brandish his sword: he hath bent his bow and made it ready.

<span id="an_7:14">7:14</span> And in it he hath prepared the
instruments of death, he hath made ready his arrows for them that burn.

<span id="an_7:15">7:15</span> Behold he hath been in labour with
injustice; he hath conceived sorrow, and brought forth iniquity.

<span id="an_7:16">7:16</span> He hath opened a pit and dug it; and he
is fallen into the hole he made.

<span id="an_7:17">7:17</span> His sorrow shall be turned on his own
head: and his iniquity shall comedown upon his crown.

<span id="an_7:18">7:18</span> I will give glory to the Lord according
to his justice: and will sing to the name of the Lord the most high.

<span id="an_8:1">8:1</span> Unto the end, for the presses: a psalm of
David.

<span id="an_8:2">8:2</span> O Lord our Lord, how admirable is thy name
in the whole earth! For thy magnificence is elevated above the heavens.

<span id="an_8:3">8:3</span> Out of the mouth of infants and of
sucklings thou hast perfected praise, because of thy enemies, that thou
mayst destroy the enemy and the avenger.

<span id="an_8:4">8:4</span> For I will behold thy heavens, the works of
thy fingers: the moon and the stars which thou hast founded.

<span id="an_8:5">8:5</span> What is man that thou art mindful of him?
or the son of man that thou visitest him?

<span id="an_8:6">8:6</span> Thou hast made him a little less than the
angels, thou hast crowned him with glory and honour:

<span id="an_8:7">8:7</span> and hast set him over the works of thy
hands.

<span id="an_8:8">8:8</span> Thou hast subjected all things under his
feet, all sheep and oxen: moreover the beasts also of the fields.

<span id="an_8:9">8:9</span> The birds of the air, and the fishes of the
sea, that pass through the paths of the sea.

<span id="an_8:10">8:10</span> O Lord our Lord, how admirable is thy
name in all the earth!

<span id="an_9:1">9:1</span> Unto the end, for the hidden things of the
Son. A psalm for David.

<span id="an_9:2">9:2</span> I will give praise to thee, O Lord, with my
whole heart: I will relate all thy wonders.

<span id="an_9:3">9:3</span> I will be glad and rejoice in thee: I will
sing to thy name, O thou most high.

<span id="an_9:4">9:4</span> When my enemy shall be turned back: they
shall be weakened and perish before thy face.

<span id="an_9:5">9:5</span> For thou hast maintained my judgment and my
cause: thou hast sat on the throne, who judgest justice.

<span id="an_9:6">9:6</span> Thou hast rebuked the Gentiles, and the
wicked one hath perished: thou hast blotted out their name for ever and
ever.

<span id="an_9:7">9:7</span> The swords of the enemy have failed unto
the end: and their cities thou hast destroyed. Their memory hath
perished with a noise.

<span id="an_9:8">9:8</span> but the Lord remaineth for ever. He hath
prepared his throne in judgment:

<span id="an_9:9">9:9</span> and he shall judge the world in equity, he
shall judge the people in justice.

<span id="an_9:10">9:10</span> And the Lord is become a refuge for the
poor: a helper in due time in tribulation.

<span id="an_9:11">9:11</span> And let them trust in thee who know thy
name: for thou hast not forsaken them that seek thee, O Lord.

<span id="an_9:12">9:12</span> Sing ye to the Lord, who dwelleth in
Sion: declare his ways among the Gentiles:

<span id="an_9:13">9:13</span> For requiring their blood he hath
remembered the: he hath not forgotten the cry of the poor.

<span id="an_9:14">9:14</span> Have mercy on me, O Lord: see my
humiliation which I suffer from my enemies.

<span id="an_9:15">9:15</span> Thou that liftest me up from the gates of
death, that I may declare all thy praises in the gates of the daughter
of Sion.

<span id="an_9:16">9:16</span> I will rejoice in thy salvation: the
Gentiles have stuck fast in the destruction which they have prepared.
Their foot hath been taken in the very snare which they hid.

<span id="an_9:17">9:17</span> The Lord shall be known when he executeth
judgments: the sinner hath been caught in the works of his own hands.

<span id="an_9:18">9:18</span> The wicked shall be turned into hell, all
the nations that forget God.

<span id="an_9:19">9:19</span> For the poor man shall not be forgotten
to the end: the patience of the poor shall not perish for ever.

<span id="an_9:20">9:20</span> Arise, O Lord, let not man be
strengthened: let the Gentiles be judged in thy sight.

<span id="an_9:21">9:21</span> Appoint, O Lord, a lawgiver over them:
that the Gentiles may know themselves to be but men.

<span id="an_10:1">10:1</span> Why, O Lord, hast thou retired afar off?
why dost thou slight us in our wants, in the time of trouble?

<span id="an_10:2">10:2</span> Whilst the wicked man is proud, the poor
is set on fire: they are caught in the counsels which they devise.

<span id="an_10:3">10:3</span> For the sinner is praised in the desires
of his soul: and the unjust man is blessed.

<span id="an_10:4">10:4</span> The sinner hath provoked the Lord
according to the multitude of his wrath he will not seek him:

<span id="an_10:5">10:5</span> God is not before his eyes: his ways are
filthy at all times. Thy judgments are removed from his sight: he shall
rule over all his enemies.

<span id="an_10:6">10:6</span> For he hath said in his heart: I shall
not be moved from generation to generation, and shall be without evil.

<span id="an_10:7">10:7</span> His mouth is full of cursing, and of
bitterness, and of deceit: under his tongue are labour and sorrow.

<span id="an_10:8">10:8</span> He sitteth in ambush with the rich in
private places, that he may kill the innocent.

<span id="an_10:9">10:9</span> His eyes are upon the poor man: He lieth
in wait in secret like a lion in his den. He lieth in ambush that he may
catch the poor man: to catch the poor, whilst he draweth him to him.

<span id="an_10:10">10:10</span> In his net he will bring him down, he
will crouch and fall, when he shall have power over the poor.

<span id="an_10:11">10:11</span> For he hath said in his heart: God hath
forgotten, he hath turned away his face not to see to the end.

<span id="an_10:12">10:12</span> Arise, O Lord God, let thy hand be
exalted: forget not the poor.

<span id="an_10:13">10:13</span> Wherefore hath the wicked provoked God?
for he hath said in his heart: He will not require it.

<span id="an_10:14">10:14</span> Thou seest it, for thou considerest
labour and sorrow: that thou mayst deliver them into thy hands. To thee
is the poor man left: thou wilt be a helper to the orphan.

<span id="an_10:15">10:15</span> Break thou the arm of the sinner and of
the malignant: his sin shall be sought, and shall not be found.

<span id="an_10:16">10:16</span> The Lord shall reign to eternity, yea,
for ever and ever: ye Gentiles shall perish from his land.

<span id="an_10:17">10:17</span> The Lord hath heard the desire of the
poor: thy ear hath heard the preparation of their heart.

<span id="an_10:18">10:18</span> To judge for the fatherless and for the
humble, that man may no more presume to magnify himself upon earth.

<span id="an_10:19">10:19</span> Unto the end. A psalm for David.

<span id="an_10:20">10:20</span> In the Lord I put my trust: how then do
you say to my soul: Get thee away from hence to the mountain like a
sparrow?

<span id="an_10:21">10:21</span> For, lo, the wicked have bent their
bow; they have prepared their arrows in the quiver; to shoot in the dark
the upright of heart.

<span id="an_10:22">10:22</span> For they have destroyed the things
which thou hast made: but what has the just man done?

<span id="an_10:23">10:23</span> The Lord is in his holy temple, the
Lord's throne is in heaven. His eyes look on the poor man: his eyelids
examine the sons of men.

<span id="an_10:24">10:24</span> The Lord trieth the just and the
wicked: but he that loveth iniquity hateth his own soul.

<span id="an_10:25">10:25</span> He shall rain snares upon sinners: fire
and brimstone and storms of winds shall be the portion of their cup.

<span id="an_10:26">10:26</span> For the Lord is just, and hath loved
justice: his countenance hath beheld righteousness.

<span id="an_11:1">11:1</span> Unto the end; for the octave, a psalm for
David.

<span id="an_11:2">11:2</span> Save me, O Lord, for there is now no
saint: truths are decayed from among the children of men.

<span id="an_11:3">11:3</span> They have spoken vain things every one to
his neighbour: with deceitful lips, and with a double heart have they
spoken.

<span id="an_11:4">11:4</span> May the Lord destroy all deceitful lips,
and the tongue that speaketh proud things.

<span id="an_11:5">11:5</span> Who have said: We will magnify our
tongue; our lips are our own; who is Lord over us?

<span id="an_11:6">11:6</span> By reason of the misery of the needy, and
the groans of the poor, now will I arise, saith the Lord. I win set him
in safety; I will deal confidently in his regard.

<span id="an_11:7">11:7</span> The words of the Lord are pure words: as
silver tried by the fire, purged from the earth refined seven times.

<span id="an_11:8">11:8</span> Thou, O Lord, wilt preserve us.: and keep
us from this generation for ever.

<span id="an_11:9">11:9</span> The wicked walk round about: according to
thy highness, thou best multiplied the children of men.

<span id="an_12:1">12:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David. How
long, O Lord, wilt thou forget me unto the end? how long dost thou turn
away thy face from me?

<span id="an_12:2">12:2</span> How long shall I take counsels in my
soul, sorrow in my heart all the day?

<span id="an_12:3">12:3</span> How long shall my enemy be exalted over
me?

<span id="an_12:4">12:4</span> Consider, and hear me, O Lord my God.
Enlighten my eyes that I never sleep in death:

<span id="an_12:5">12:5</span> lest at any time my enemy say: I have
prevailed against him. They that trouble me will rejoice when I am
moved:

<span id="an_12:6">12:6</span> but I have trusted in thy mercy. My heart
shall rejoice in thy salvation: I will sing to the Lord, who giveth me
good things: yea I will sing to the name of the Lord the most high.

<span id="an_13:1">13:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David. The fool
hath said in his heart: There is no God, They are corrupt, and are
become abominable in their ways: there is none that doth good, no not
one.

<span id="an_13:2">13:2</span> The Lord hath looked down from heaven
upon the children of men, to see if there be any that understand and
seek God.

<span id="an_13:3">13:3</span> They are all gone aside, they are become
unprofitable together: there is none that doth good, no not one. Their
throat is an open sepulchre: with their tongues they acted deceitfully;
the poison of asps is under their lips. Their mouth is full of cursing
and bitterness; their feet are swift to shed blood. Destruction and
unhappiness in their ways: and the way of peace they have not known:
there is no fear of God before their eyes.

<span id="an_13:4">13:4</span> Shall not all they know that work
iniquity, who devour my people as they eat bread ?

<span id="an_13:5">13:5</span> They have not called upon the Lord: there
have they trembled for fear, where there was no fear.

<span id="an_13:6">13:6</span> For the Lord is in the just generation:
you have confounded the counsel of the poor man, but the Lord is his
hope.

<span id="an_13:7">13:7</span> Who shall give out of Sion the salvation
of Israel? when the Lord shall have turned away the captivity of his
people, Jacob shall rejoice and Israel shall be glad.

<span id="an_14:1">14:1</span> A psalm of David. Lord, who shall dwell
in thy tabernacle? or who shall rest in thy holy hill?

<span id="an_14:2">14:2</span> He that walketh without blemish, and
worketh justice:

<span id="an_14:3">14:3</span> He that speaketh truth in his heart, who
hath not used deceit in his tongue: Nor hath done evil to his neighbour:
nor taken up a reproach against his neighbours.

<span id="an_14:4">14:4</span> In his sight the malignant is brought to
nothing: but he glorifieth them that fear the Lord. He that sweareth to
his neighbour, and deceiveth not;

<span id="an_14:5">14:5</span> he that hath not put out his money to
usury, nor taken bribes against the innocent: He that doth these things
shall not be moved for ever.

<span id="an_15:1">15:1</span> The inscription of a title to David
himself. Preserve me, O Lord, for I have put trust in thee.

<span id="an_15:2">15:2</span> I have said to the Lord, thou art my God,
for thou hast no need of my goods.

<span id="an_15:3">15:3</span> To the saints, who are in his land, he
hath made wonderful all my desires in them.

<span id="an_15:4">15:4</span> Their infirmities were multiplied:
afterwards they made haste. I will not gather together their meetings
for blood offerings: nor will I be mindful of their names by my lips.

<span id="an_15:5">15:5</span> The Lord is the portion of my inheritance
and of my cup: it is thou that wilt restore my inheritance to me.

<span id="an_15:6">15:6</span> The lines are fallen unto me in goodly
places: for my inheritance is goodly to me.

<span id="an_15:7">15:7</span> I will bless the Lord, who hath given me
understanding: moreover my reins also have corrected me even till night.

<span id="an_15:8">15:8</span> I set the Lord always in my sight: for he
is at my right hand, that I be not moved.

<span id="an_15:9">15:9</span> Therefore my heart hath been glad, and my
tongue hath rejoiced: moreover my flesh also shall rest in hope.

<span id="an_15:10">15:10</span> Because thou wilt not leave my soul in
hell; nor wilt then give thy holy one to see corruption.

<span id="an_15:11">15:11</span> Thou hast made known to me the ways of
life, thou shalt fill me with joy with thy countenance: at thy right
hand are delights even to the end.

<span id="an_16:1">16:1</span> The prayer of David. Hear, O Lord, my
justice: attend to my supplication. Give ear unto my prayer, which
proceedeth not from deceitful lips.

<span id="an_16:2">16:2</span> Let my judgment come forth from thy
countenance: let thy eyes behold the things that are equitable.

<span id="an_16:3">16:3</span> Thou hast proved my heart, and visited it
by night, thou hast tried me by fire: and iniquity hath not been found
in me.

<span id="an_16:4">16:4</span> That my mouth may not speak the works of
men: for the sake of the words of thy lips, I have kept hard ways.

<span id="an_16:5">16:5</span> Perfect thou my goings in thy paths: that
my footsteps be not moved.

<span id="an_16:6">16:6</span> I have cried to thee, for thou, O God,
hast heard me: O incline thy ear unto me, and hear my words.

<span id="an_16:7">16:7</span> Shew forth thy wonderful mercies; thou
who savest them that trust in thee.

<span id="an_16:8">16:8</span> From them that resist thy right hand keep
me, as the apple of thy eye. Protect me under the shadow of thy wings.

<span id="an_16:9">16:9</span> From the face of the wicked who have
afflicted me. My enemies have surrounded my soul:

<span id="an_16:10">16:10</span> they have shut up their fat: their
mouth hath spoken proudly.

<span id="an_16:11">16:11</span> They have cast me forth and now they
have surrounded me: they have set their eyes bowing down to the earth.

<span id="an_16:12">16:12</span> They have taken me, as a lion prepared
for the prey; and as a young lion dwelling in secret places.

<span id="an_16:13">16:13</span> Arise, O Lord, disappoint him and
supplant him; deliver my soul from the wicked one: thy sword

<span id="an_16:14">16:14</span> from the enemies of thy hand. O Lord,
divide them from the few of the earth in their life: their belly is
filled from thy hidden stores. They are full of children: and they have
left to their little ones the rest of their substance.

<span id="an_16:15">16:15</span> But as for me, I will appear before thy
sight in justice: I shall be satisfied when thy glory shall appear.

<span id="an_17:1">17:1</span> Unto the end, for David the servant of
the Lord, who spoke to the Lord the words of this canticle, in the day
that the Lord delivered him from the hands of all his enemies, and from
the hand of Saul. \[2 Kings 22.\]

<span id="an_17:2">17:2</span> I will love thee, O Lord, my strength:

<span id="an_17:3">17:3</span> The Lord is my firmament, my refuge, and
my deliverer. My God is my helper, and in him will I put my trust. My
protector and the horn of my salvation, and my support.

<span id="an_17:4">17:4</span> Praising I will call upon the Lord: and I
shall be saved from my enemies.

<span id="an_17:5">17:5</span> The sorrows of death surrounded me: and
the torrents of iniquity troubled me.

<span id="an_17:6">17:6</span> The sorrows of hell encompassed me: and
the snares of death prevented me.

<span id="an_17:7">17:7</span> In my affliction I called upon the Lord,
and I cried to my God: And he heard my voice from his holy temple: and
my cry before him came into his ears.

<span id="an_17:8">17:8</span> The earth shook and trembled: the
foundations of the mountains were troubled and were moved, because he
was angry with them.

<span id="an_17:9">17:9</span> There went up a smoke in his wrath: and a
fire flamed from his face: coals were kindled by it.

<span id="an_17:10">17:10</span> He bowed the heavens, and came down:
and darkness was under his feet.

<span id="an_17:11">17:11</span> And he ascended upon the cherubim, and
he flew; he flew upon the wings of the winds.

<span id="an_17:12">17:12</span> And he made darkness his covert, his
pavilion round about him: dark waters in the clouds of the air.

<span id="an_17:13">17:13</span> At the brightness that was before him
the clouds passed, hail and coals of fire.

<span id="an_17:14">17:14</span> And the Lord thundered from heaven, and
the highest gave his voice: hail and coals of fire.

<span id="an_17:15">17:15</span> And he sent forth his arrows, and he
scattered them: he multiplied lightnings, and troubled them.

<span id="an_17:16">17:16</span> Then the fountains of waters appeared,
and the foundations of the world were discovered: At thy rebuke, O Lord,
at the blast of the spirit of thy wrath.

<span id="an_17:17">17:17</span> He sent from on high, and took me: and
received me out of many waters.

<span id="an_17:18">17:18</span> He delivered me from my strongest
enemies, and from them that hated me: for they were too strong for me.

<span id="an_17:19">17:19</span> They prevented me in the day of my
affliction: and the Lord became my protector.

<span id="an_17:20">17:20</span> And he brought me forth into a large
place: he saved me, because he was well pleased with me.

<span id="an_17:21">17:21</span> And the Lord will reward me according
to my justice; and will repay me according to the cleanness of my hands:

<span id="an_17:22">17:22</span> Because I have kept the ways of the
Lord; and have not done wickedly against my God.

<span id="an_17:23">17:23</span> For till his judgments are in my sight:
and his justices I have not put away from me.

<span id="an_17:24">17:24</span> And I shall be spotless with him: and
shall keep myself from my iniquity.

<span id="an_17:25">17:25</span> And the Lord will reward me according
to my justice; and according to the cleanness of my hands before his
eyes.

<span id="an_17:26">17:26</span> With the holy, thou wilt be holy; and
with the innocent man thou wilt be innocent.

<span id="an_17:27">17:27</span> And with the elect thou wilt be elect:
and with the perverse thou wilt be perverted.

<span id="an_17:28">17:28</span> For thou wilt save the humble people;
but wilt bring down the eyes of the proud.

<span id="an_17:29">17:29</span> For thou lightest my lamp, O Lord: O my
God enlighten my darkness.

<span id="an_17:30">17:30</span> For by thee I shall be delivered from
temptation; and through my God I shall go over a wall.

<span id="an_17:31">17:31</span> As for my God, his way is undefiled:
the words of the Lord are fire tried: he is the protector of all that
trust in him.

<span id="an_17:32">17:32</span> For who is God but the Lord? or who is
God but our God?

<span id="an_17:33">17:33</span> God who hath girt me with strength; and
made my way blameless.

<span id="an_17:34">17:34</span> Who hath made my feet like the feet of
harts: and who setteth me upon high places.

<span id="an_17:35">17:35</span> Who teacheth my hands to war: and thou
hast made my arms like a brazen bow.

<span id="an_17:36">17:36</span> And thou hast given me the protection
of thy salvation: and thy right hand hath held me up: And thy discipline
hath corrected me unto the end: and thy discipline, the same shall teach
me.

<span id="an_17:37">17:37</span> Thou hast enlarged my steps under me;
and my feet are not weakened.

<span id="an_17:38">17:38</span> I will pursue after my enemies, and
overtake them: and I will not turn again till they are consumed.

<span id="an_17:39">17:39</span> I will break them, and they shall not
be able to stand: they shall fall under my feet.

<span id="an_17:40">17:40</span> And thou hast girded me with strength
unto battle; and hast subdued under me them that rose up against me.

<span id="an_17:41">17:41</span> And thou hast made my enemies turn
their back upon me, and hast destroyed them that hated me.

<span id="an_17:42">17:42</span> They cried, but there was none to save
them, to the Lord: but he heard them not.

<span id="an_17:43">17:43</span> And I shall beat them as small as the
dust before the wind; I shall bring them to nought, like the dirt in the
streets.

<span id="an_17:44">17:44</span> Thou wilt deliver me from the
contradictions of the people: thou wilt make me head of the Gentiles.

<span id="an_17:45">17:45</span> A people, which I knew not, hath served
me: at the hearing of the ear they have obeyed me.

<span id="an_17:46">17:46</span> The children that are strangers have
lied to me, strange children have faded away, and have halted from their
paths.

<span id="an_17:47">17:47</span> The Lord liveth, and blessed be my God,
and let the God of my salvation be exalted :

<span id="an_17:48">17:48</span> O God, who avengest me, and subduest
the people under me, my deliverer from my enemies.

<span id="an_17:49">17:49</span> And thou wilt lift me up above them
that rise up against me: from the unjust man thou wilt deliver me.

<span id="an_17:50">17:50</span> Therefore will I give glory to thee, O
Lord, among the nations, and I will sing a psalm to thy name.

<span id="an_17:51">17:51</span> Giving great deliverance to his king,
and shewing mercy to David his anointed : and to his seed for ever.

<span id="an_18:1">18:1</span> Unto the end. A psalm for David.

<span id="an_18:2">18:2</span> The heavens shew forth the glory of God,
and the firmament declareth the work of his hands.

<span id="an_18:3">18:3</span> Day to day uttereth speech, and night to
night sheweth knowledge.

<span id="an_18:4">18:4</span> There are no speeches nor languages,
where their voices are not heard.

<span id="an_18:5">18:5</span> Their sound hath gone forth into all the
earth: and their words unto the ends of the world.

<span id="an_18:6">18:6</span> He hath set his tabernacle in the sun:
and he, as a bridegroom coming out of his bride chamber, Hath rejoiced
as a giant to run the way:

<span id="an_18:7">18:7</span> His going out is from the end of heaven,
And his circuit even to the end thereof: and there is no one that can
hide himself from his heat.

<span id="an_18:8">18:8</span> The law of the Lord is unspotted,
converting souls: the testimony of the Lord is faithful, giving wisdom
to little ones.

<span id="an_18:9">18:9</span> The justices of the Lord are right,
rejoicing hearts: the commandment of the Lord is lightsome, enlightening
the eyes.

<span id="an_18:10">18:10</span> The fear of the Lord is holy, enduring
for ever and ever: the judgments of the Lord are true, justified in
themselves.

<span id="an_18:11">18:11</span> More to be desired than gold and many
precious stones: and sweeter than honey and the honeycomb.

<span id="an_18:12">18:12</span> For thy servant keepeth them, and in
keeping them there is a great reward.

<span id="an_18:13">18:13</span> Who can understand sins? from my secret
ones cleanse me, O Lord:

<span id="an_18:14">18:14</span> and from those of others spare thy
servant. If they shall have no dominion over me, then shall I be without
spot: and I shall be cleansed from the greatest sin.

<span id="an_18:15">18:15</span> And the words of my mouth shall be such
as may please: and the meditation of my heart always in thy sight. O
Lord, my helper, and my redeemer.

<span id="an_19:1">19:1</span> Unto the end. A psalm for David.

<span id="an_19:2">19:2</span> May the Lord hear thee in the day of
tribulation: may the name of the God of Jacob protect thee.

<span id="an_19:3">19:3</span> May he send thee help from the sanctuary:
and defend thee out of Sion.

<span id="an_19:4">19:4</span> May he be mindful of all thy sacrifices:
and may thy whole burnt offering be made fat.

<span id="an_19:5">19:5</span> May he give thee according to thy own
heart; and confirm all thy counsels.

<span id="an_19:6">19:6</span> We will rejoice in thy salvation; and in
the name of our God we shall be exalted.

<span id="an_19:7">19:7</span> The Lord fulfil all thy petitions: now
have I known that the Lord hath saved his anointed. He will hear him
from his holy heaven: the salvation of his right hand is in powers.

<span id="an_19:8">19:8</span> Some trust in chariots, and some in
horses: but we will call upon the name of the Lord our God.

<span id="an_19:9">19:9</span> They are bound, and have fallen; but we
are risen, and are set upright. O Lord, save the king: and hear us in
the day that we shall call upon thee.

<span id="an_20:1">20:1</span> Unto the end. A psalm for David.

<span id="an_20:2">20:2</span> In thy strength, O Lord, the king shall
joy; and in thy salvation he shall rejoice exceedingly.

<span id="an_20:3">20:3</span> Thou hast given him his heart's desire:
end hast not withholden from him the will of his lips.

<span id="an_20:4">20:4</span> For thou hast prevented him with
blessings of sweetness: thou hast set on his head a crown of precious
stones.

<span id="an_20:5">20:5</span> He asked life of thee: and thou hast
given him length of days for ever and ever.

<span id="an_20:6">20:6</span> His glory is great in thy salvation:
glory and great beauty shalt thou lay upon him.

<span id="an_20:7">20:7</span> For thou shalt give him to be a blessing
for ever and ever: thou shalt make him joyful in gladness with thy
countenance.

<span id="an_20:8">20:8</span> For the king hopeth in the Lord: and
through the mercy of the most High he shall not be moved.

<span id="an_20:9">20:9</span> Let thy hand be found by all thy enemies:
let thy right hand find out all them that hate thee.

<span id="an_20:10">20:10</span> Thou shalt make them as an oven of
fire, in the time of thy anger: the Lord shall trouble them in his
wrath, and fire shall devour them.

<span id="an_20:11">20:11</span> Their fruit shalt thou destroy from the
earth: and their seed from among the children of men.

<span id="an_20:12">20:12</span> For they have intended evils against
thee: they have devised counsels which they have not been able to
establish.

<span id="an_20:13">20:13</span> For thou shalt make them turn their
back: in thy remnants thou shalt prepare their face.

<span id="an_20:14">20:14</span> Be thou exalted, O Lord, in thy own
strength: we will sing and praise thy power.

<span id="an_21:1">21:1</span> Unto the end, for the morning protection,
a psalm for David.

<span id="an_21:2">21:2</span> O God my God, look upon me: why hast thou
forsaken me? Far from my salvation are the words of my sins.

<span id="an_21:3">21:3</span> O my God, I shall cry by day, and thou
wilt not hear: and by night, and it shall not be reputed as folly in me.

<span id="an_21:4">21:4</span> But thou dwellest in the holy place, the
praise of Israel.

<span id="an_21:5">21:5</span> In thee have our fathers hoped: they have
hoped, and thou hast delivered them.

<span id="an_21:6">21:6</span> They cried to thee, and they were saved:
they trusted in thee, and were not confounded.

<span id="an_21:7">21:7</span> But I am a worm, and no man: the reproach
of men, and the outcast of the people.

<span id="an_21:8">21:8</span> All they that saw me have laughed me to
scorn: they have spoken with the lips, and wagged the head.

<span id="an_21:9">21:9</span> He hoped in the Lord, let him deliver
him: let him save him, seeing he delighteth in him.

<span id="an_21:10">21:10</span> For thou art he that hast drawn me out
of the womb: my hope from the breasts of my mother.

<span id="an_21:11">21:11</span> I was cast upon thee from the womb.
From my mother's womb thou art my God,

<span id="an_21:12">21:12</span> depart not from me. For tribulation is
very near: for there is none to help me.

<span id="an_21:13">21:13</span> Many calves have surrounded me: fat
bulls have besieged me.

<span id="an_21:14">21:14</span> They have opened their mouths against
me, as a lion ravening and roaring.

<span id="an_21:15">21:15</span> I am poured out like water; and all my
bones are scattered. My heart is become like wax melting in the midst of
my bowels.

<span id="an_21:16">21:16</span> My strength is dried up like a
potsherd, and my tongue hath cleaved to my jaws: and thou hast brought
me down into the dust of death.

<span id="an_21:17">21:17</span> For many dogs have encompassed me: the
council of the malignant hath besieged me. They have dug my hands and
feet.

<span id="an_21:18">21:18</span> They have numbered all my bones. And
they have looked and stared upon me.

<span id="an_21:19">21:19</span> They parted my garments amongst them;
and upon my vesture they cast lots.

<span id="an_21:20">21:20</span> But thou, O Lord, remove not thy help
to a distance from me; look towards my defence.

<span id="an_21:21">21:21</span> Deliver, O God, my soul from the sword:
my only one from the hand of the dog.

<span id="an_21:22">21:22</span> Save me from the lion's mouth; and my
lowness from the horns of the unicorns.

<span id="an_21:23">21:23</span> I will declare thy name to my brethren:
in the midst of the church will I praise thee.

<span id="an_21:24">21:24</span> Ye that fear the Lord, praise him: all
ye the seed of Jacob, glorify him.

<span id="an_21:25">21:25</span> Let all the seed of Israel fear him:
because he hath not slighted nor despised the supplication of the poor
man. Neither hath he turned away his face from me: and when I cried to
him he heard me.

<span id="an_21:26">21:26</span> With thee is my praise in a great
church: I will pay my vows in the sight of them that fear him.

<span id="an_21:27">21:27</span> The poor shall eat and shall be filled:
and they shall praise the Lord that seek him: their hearts shall live
for ever and ever.

<span id="an_21:28">21:28</span> All the ends of the earth shall
remember, and shall be converted to the Lord: And all the kindreds of
the Gentiles shall adore in his sight.

<span id="an_21:29">21:29</span> For the kingdom is the Lord's; and he
shall have dominion over the nations.

<span id="an_21:30">21:30</span> All the fat ones of the earth have
eaten and have adored: all they that go down to the earth shall fall
before him.

<span id="an_21:31">21:31</span> And to him my soul shall live: and my
seed shall serve him.

<span id="an_21:32">21:32</span> There shall be declared to the Lord a
generation to come: and the heavens shall shew forth his justice to a
people that shall be born, which the Lord hath made.

<span id="an_22:1">22:1</span> A psalm for David. The Lord ruleth me:
and I shall want nothing.

<span id="an_22:2">22:2</span> He hath set me in a place of pasture. He
hath brought me up, on the water of refreshment:

<span id="an_22:3">22:3</span> he hath converted my soul. He hath led me
on the paths of justice, for his own name's sake.

<span id="an_22:4">22:4</span> For though I should walk in the midst of
the shadow of death, I will fear no evils, for thou art with me. Thy rod
and thy staff, they have comforted me.

<span id="an_22:5">22:5</span> Thou hast prepared a table before me
against them that afflict me. Thou hast anointed my head with oil; and
my chalice which inebriateth me, how goodly is it!

<span id="an_22:6">22:6</span> And thy mercy will follow me all the days
of my life. And that I may dwell in the house of the Lord unto length of
days.

<span id="an_23:1">23:1</span> On the first day of the week, a psalm for
David. The earth is the Lord's and the fulness thereof: the world, and
all they that dwell therein.

<span id="an_23:2">23:2</span> For he hath founded it upon the seas; and
hath prepared it upon the rivers.

<span id="an_23:3">23:3</span> Who shall ascend into the mountain of the
Lord: or who shall stand in his holy place?

<span id="an_23:4">23:4</span> The innocent in hands, and clean of
heart, who hath not taken his soul in vain, nor sworn deceitfully to his
neighbour.

<span id="an_23:5">23:5</span> He shall receive a blessing from the
Lord, and mercy from God his Saviour.

<span id="an_23:6">23:6</span> This is the generation of them that seek
him, of them that seek the face of the God of Jacob.

<span id="an_23:7">23:7</span> Lift up your gates, O ye princes, and be
ye lifted up, O eternal gates: and the King of Glory shall enter in.

<span id="an_23:8">23:8</span> Who is this King of Glory? the Lord who
is strong and mighty: the Lord mighty in battle.

<span id="an_23:9">23:9</span> Lift up your gates, O ye princes, and be
ye lifted up, O eternal gates: and the King of Glory shall enter in.

<span id="an_23:10">23:10</span> Who is this King of Glory? the Lord of
hosts, he is the King of Glory.

<span id="an_24:1">24:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David. To thee,
O Lord, have I lifted up my soul.

<span id="an_24:2">24:2</span> In thee, O my God, I put my trust; let me
not be ashamed.

<span id="an_24:3">24:3</span> Neither let my enemies laugh at me: for
none of them that wait on thee shall be confounded.

<span id="an_24:4">24:4</span> Let all them be confounded that act
unjust things without cause. Shew, O Lord, thy ways to me, and teach me
thy paths.

<span id="an_24:5">24:5</span> Direct me in thy truth, and teach me; for
thou art God my Saviour; and on thee have I waited all the day long.

<span id="an_24:6">24:6</span> Remember, O Lord, thy bowels of
compassion; and thy mercies that are from the beginning of the world.

<span id="an_24:7">24:7</span> The sins of my youth and my ignorances do
not remember. According to thy mercy remember thou me: for thy goodness'
sake, O Lord.

<span id="an_24:8">24:8</span> The Lord is sweet and righteous:
therefore he will give a law to sinners in the way.

<span id="an_24:9">24:9</span> He will guide the mild in judgment: he
will teach the meek his ways.

<span id="an_24:10">24:10</span> All the ways of the Lord are mercy and
truth, to them that seek after his covenant and his testimonies.

<span id="an_24:11">24:11</span> For thy name's sake, O Lord, thou wilt
pardon my sin: for it is great.

<span id="an_24:12">24:12</span> Who is the man that feareth the Lord?
He hath appointed him a law in the way he hath chosen.

<span id="an_24:13">24:13</span> His soul shall dwell in good things:
and his seed shall inherit the land.

<span id="an_24:14">24:14</span> The Lord is a firmament to them that
fear him: and his covenant shall be made manifest to them.

<span id="an_24:15">24:15</span> My eyes are ever towards the Lord: for
he shall pluck my feet out of the snare.

<span id="an_24:16">24:16</span> Look thou upon me, and have mercy on
me; for I am alone and poor.

<span id="an_24:17">24:17</span> The troubles of my heart are
multiplied: deliver me from my necessities.

<span id="an_24:18">24:18</span> See my abjection and my labour; and
forgive me all my sins.

<span id="an_24:19">24:19</span> Consider my enemies for they are
multiplied, and have hated me with an unjust hatred.

<span id="an_24:20">24:20</span> Keep thou my soul, and deliver me: I
shall not be ashamed, for I have hoped in thee.

<span id="an_24:21">24:21</span> The innocent and the upright have
adhered to me: because I have waited on thee.

<span id="an_24:22">24:22</span> Deliver Israel, O God, from all his
tribulations.

<span id="an_25:1">25:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David. Judge
me, O Lord, for I have walked in my innocence: and I have put my trust
in the Lord, and shall not be weakened.

<span id="an_25:2">25:2</span> Prove me, O Lord, and try me; burn my
reins and my heart.

<span id="an_25:3">25:3</span> For thy mercy is before my eyes; and I am
well pleased with thy truth.

<span id="an_25:4">25:4</span> I have not sat with the council of
vanity: neither will I go in with the doers of unjust things.

<span id="an_25:5">25:5</span> I have hated the assembly of the
malignant; and with the wicked I will not sit.

<span id="an_25:6">25:6</span> I will wash my hands among the innocent;
and will compass thy altar, O Lord:

<span id="an_25:7">25:7</span> That I may hear the voice of thy praise:
and tell of all thy wondrous works.

<span id="an_25:8">25:8</span> I have loved, O Lord, the beauty of thy
house; and the place where thy glory dwelleth.

<span id="an_25:9">25:9</span> Take not away my soul, O God, with the
wicked: nor my life with bloody men:

<span id="an_25:10">25:10</span> In whose hands are iniquities: their
right hand is filled with gifts.

<span id="an_25:11">25:11</span> But as for me, I have walked in my
innocence: redeem me, and have mercy on me.

<span id="an_25:12">25:12</span> My foot hath stood in the direct way:
in the churches I will bless thee, O Lord.

<span id="an_26:1">26:1</span> The psalm of David before he was
anointed. The Lord is my light and my salvation, whom shall I fear? The
Lord is the protector of my life: of whom shall I be afraid?

<span id="an_26:2">26:2</span> Whilst the wicked draw near against me,
to eat my flesh. My enemies that trouble me, have themselves been
weakened, and have fallen.

<span id="an_26:3">26:3</span> If armies in camp should stand together
against me, my heart shall not fear. If a battle should rise up against
me, in this will I be confident.

<span id="an_26:4">26:4</span> One thing I have asked of the Lord, this
will I seek after; that I may dwell in the house of the Lord all the
days of my life. That I may see the delight of the Lord, and may visit
his temple.

<span id="an_26:5">26:5</span> For he hath hidden me in his tabernacle;
in the day of evils, he hath protected me in the secret place of his
tabernacle.

<span id="an_26:6">26:6</span> He hath exalted me upon a rock: and now
he hath lifted up my head above my enemies. I have gone round, and have
offered up in his tabernacle a sacrifice of jubilation: I will sing, and
recite a psalm to the Lord.

<span id="an_26:7">26:7</span> Hear, O Lord, my voice, with which I have
cried to thee: have mercy on me and hear me.

<span id="an_26:8">26:8</span> My heart hath said to thee: My face hath
sought thee: thy face, O Lord, will I still seek.

<span id="an_26:9">26:9</span> Turn not away thy face from me; decline
not in thy wrath from thy servant. Be thou my helper, forsake me not; do
not thou despise me, O God my Saviour.

<span id="an_26:10">26:10</span> For my father and my mother have left
me: but the Lord hath taken me up.

<span id="an_26:11">26:11</span> Set me, O Lord, a law in thy way, and
guide me in the right path, because of my enemies.

<span id="an_26:12">26:12</span> Deliver me not over to the will of them
that trouble me; for unjust witnesses have risen up against me; and
iniquity hath lied to itself.

<span id="an_26:13">26:13</span> I believe to see the good things of the
Lord in the land of the living.

<span id="an_26:14">26:14</span> Expect the Lord, do manfully, and let
thy heart take courage, and wait thou for the Lord.

<span id="an_27:1">27:1</span> A psalm for David himself. Unto thee will
I cry, O Lord: O my God, be not thou silent to me: lest thou be silent
to me, I become like them that go down into the pit.

<span id="an_27:2">27:2</span> Hear, O Lord, the voice of my
supplication, when I pray to thee; when I lift up my hands to thy holy
temple.

<span id="an_27:3">27:3</span> Draw me not away together with the
wicked; and with the workers of iniquity destroy me not: Who speak peace
with their neighbour, but evils are in their hearts.

<span id="an_27:4">27:4</span> Give them according to their works, and
according to the wickedness of their inventions. According to the works
of their hands give thou to them: render to them their reward.

<span id="an_27:5">27:5</span> Because they have not understood the
works of the Lord, and the operations of his hands: thou shalt destroy
them, and shalt not build them up.

<span id="an_27:6">27:6</span> Blessed be the Lord, for he hath heard
the voice of my supplication.

<span id="an_27:7">27:7</span> The Lord is my helper and my protector:
in him hath my heart confided, and I have been helped. And my flesh hath
flourished again, and with my will I will give praise to him.

<span id="an_27:8">27:8</span> The Lord is the strength of his people,
and the protector of the salvation of his anointed.

<span id="an_27:9">27:9</span> Save, O Lord, thy people, and bless thy
inheritance: and rule them and exalt them for ever.

<span id="an_28:1">28:1</span> A psalm for David, at the finishing of
the tabernacle. Bring to the Lord, O ye children of God: bring to the
Lord the offspring of rams.

<span id="an_28:2">28:2</span> Bring to the Lord glory and honour: bring
to the Lord glory to his name: adore ye the Lord in his holy court.

<span id="an_28:3">28:3</span> The voice of the Lord is upon the waters;
the God of majesty hath thundered, The Lord is upon many waters.

<span id="an_28:4">28:4</span> The voice of the Lord is in power; the
voice of the Lord in magnificence.

<span id="an_28:5">28:5</span> The voice of the Lord breaketh the
cedars: yea, the Lord shall break the cedars of Libanus.

<span id="an_28:6">28:6</span> And shall reduce them to pieces, as a
calf of Libanus, and as the beloved son of unicorns.

<span id="an_28:7">28:7</span> The voice of the Lord divideth the flame
of fire:

<span id="an_28:8">28:8</span> The voice of the Lord shaketh the desert:
and the Lord shall shake the desert of Cades.

<span id="an_28:9">28:9</span> The voice of the Lord prepareth the
stags: and he will discover the thick woods: and in his temple all shall
speak his glory.

<span id="an_28:10">28:10</span> The Lord maketh the hood to dwell: and
the Lord shall sit king for ever. The Lord will give strength to his
people: the Lord will bless his people with peace.

<span id="an_29:1">29:1</span> A psalm of a canticle, at the dedication
of David's house.

<span id="an_29:2">29:2</span> I will extol thee, O Lord, for thou hast
upheld me: and hast not made my enemies to rejoice over me.

<span id="an_29:3">29:3</span> O Lord my God, I have cried to thee, and
then hast healed me.

<span id="an_29:4">29:4</span> Thou hast brought forth, O Lord, my soul
from hell: thou hast saved me from them that go down into the pit.

<span id="an_29:5">29:5</span> Sing to the Lord, O ye his saints: and
give praise to the memory of his holiness.

<span id="an_29:6">29:6</span> For wrath is in his indignation; and life
in his good will. In the evening weeping shall have place, and in the
morning gladness.

<span id="an_29:7">29:7</span> And in my abundance I said: I shall never
be moved.

<span id="an_29:8">29:8</span> O Lord, in thy favour, thou gavest
strength to my beauty. Thou turnedst away thy face from me, and I became
troubled.

<span id="an_29:9">29:9</span> To thee, O Lord, will I cry: and I will
make supplication to my God.

<span id="an_29:10">29:10</span> What profit is there in my blood,
whilst I go down to corruption? Shall dust confess to thee, or declare
thy truth?

<span id="an_29:11">29:11</span> The Lord hath heard, and hath had mercy
on me: the Lord became my helper.

<span id="an_29:12">29:12</span> Thou hast turned for me my mourning
into joy: thou hast cut my sackcloth, and hast compassed me with
gladness:

<span id="an_29:13">29:13</span> To the end that my glory may sing to
thee, and I may not regret: O Lord my God, I will give praise to thee
for ever.

<span id="an_30:1">30:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David, in an
ecstasy.

<span id="an_30:2">30:2</span> In thee, O Lord, have I hoped, Iet me
never be confounded: deliver me in thy justice.

<span id="an_30:3">30:3</span> Bow down thy ear to me: make haste to
deliver me. Be thou unto me a God, a protector, and a house of refuge,
to save me.

<span id="an_30:4">30:4</span> For thou art my strength and my refuge;
and for thy name's sake thou wilt lead me, and nourish me.

<span id="an_30:5">30:5</span> Thou wilt bring me out of this snare,
which they have hidden for me: for thou art my protector.

<span id="an_30:6">30:6</span> Into thy hands I commend my spirit: thou
hast redeemed me, O Lord, the God of truth.

<span id="an_30:7">30:7</span> Thou hast hated them that regard
vanities, to no purpose. But I have hoped in the Lord:

<span id="an_30:8">30:8</span> I will be glad and rejoice in thy mercy.
For thou best regarded my humility, thou hast saved my soul out of
distresses.

<span id="an_30:9">30:9</span> And thou hast not shut me up in the hands
of the enemy: thou hast set my feet in a spacious place.

<span id="an_30:10">30:10</span> Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I am
afflicted: my eye is troubled with wrath, my soul, and my belly:

<span id="an_30:11">30:11</span> For my life is wasted with grief: and
my years in sighs. My strength is weakened through poverty and my bones
are disturbed.

<span id="an_30:12">30:12</span> I am become a reproach among all my
enemies, and very much to my neighbours; and a fear to my acquaintance.
They that saw me without fled from me.

<span id="an_30:13">30:13</span> I am forgotten as one dead from the
heart. I am become as a vessel that is destroyed.

<span id="an_30:14">30:14</span> For I have heard the blame of many that
dwell round about. While they assembled together against me, they
consulted to take away my life.

<span id="an_30:15">30:15</span> But I have put my trust in thee, O
Lord: I said: Thou art my God.

<span id="an_30:16">30:16</span> My lots are in thy hands. Deliver me
out of the hands of my enemies; and from them that persecute me.

<span id="an_30:17">30:17</span> Make thy face to shine upon thy
servant; save me in thy mercy.

<span id="an_30:18">30:18</span> Let me not be confounded, O Lord, for I
have called upon thee. Let the wicked be ashamed, and be brought down to
hell.

<span id="an_30:19">30:19</span> Let deceitful lips be made dumb. Which
speak iniquity against the just, with pride and abuse.

<span id="an_30:20">30:20</span> O how great is the multitude of thy
sweetness, O Lord, which thou hast hidden for them that fear thee! Which
thou hast wrought for them that hope in thee, in the sight of the sons
of men.

<span id="an_30:21">30:21</span> Thou shalt hide them in the secret of
thy face, from the disturbance of men. Thou shalt protect them in thy
tabernacle from the contradiction of tongues.

<span id="an_30:22">30:22</span> Blessed be the Lord, for he hath shewn
his wonderful mercy to me in a fortified city.

<span id="an_30:23">30:23</span> But I said in the excess of my mind: I
am cast away from before thy eyes. Therefore thou hast heard the voice
of my prayer, when I cried to thee.

<span id="an_30:24">30:24</span> O love the Lord, all ye his saints: for
the Lord will require truth, and will repay them abundantly that act
proudly.

<span id="an_30:25">30:25</span> Do ye manfully, and let your heart be
strengthened, all ye that hope in the Lord.

<span id="an_31:1">31:1</span> To David himself, understanding. Blessed
are they whose iniquities are forgiven, and whose sins are covered.

<span id="an_31:2">31:2</span> Blessed is the man to whom the Lord hath
not imputed sin, and in whose spirit there is no guile.

<span id="an_31:3">31:3</span> Because I was silent my bones grew old;
whilst I cried out all the day long.

<span id="an_31:4">31:4</span> For day and night thy hand was heavy upon
me: I am turned in my anguish, whilst the thorn is fastened.

<span id="an_31:5">31:5</span> I have acknowledged my sin to thee, and
my injustice I have not concealed. I said I will confess against myself
my injustice to the Lord: and thou hast forgiven the wickedness of my
sin.

<span id="an_31:6">31:6</span> For this shall every one that is holy
pray to thee in a seasonable time. And yet in a flood of many waters,
they shall not come nigh unto him.

<span id="an_31:7">31:7</span> Thou art my refuge from the trouble which
hath encompassed me: my joy, deliver me from them that surround me.

<span id="an_31:8">31:8</span> I will give thee understanding, and I
will instruct thee in this way, in which thou shalt go: I will fix my
eyes upon thee.

<span id="an_31:9">31:9</span> Do not become like the horse and the
mule, who have no understanding. With bit and bridle bind fast their
jaws, who come not near unto thee.

<span id="an_31:10">31:10</span> Many are the scourges of the sinner,
but mercy shall encompass him that hopeth in the Lord.

<span id="an_31:11">31:11</span> Be glad in the Lord, and rejoice, ye
just, and glory, all ye right of heart.

<span id="an_32:1">32:1</span> A psalm for David. Rejoice in the Lord, O
ye just: praise becometh the upright.

<span id="an_32:2">32:2</span> Give praise to the Lord on the harp; sing
to him with the psaltery, the instrument of ten strings.

<span id="an_32:3">32:3</span> Sing to him a new canticle, sing well
unto him with a loud noise.

<span id="an_32:4">32:4</span> For the word of the Lord is right, and
all his works are done with faithfulness.

<span id="an_32:5">32:5</span> He loveth mercy and judgment; the earth
is full of the mercy of the Lord.

<span id="an_32:6">32:6</span> By the word of the Lord the heavens were
established; and all the power of them by the spirit of his mouth:

<span id="an_32:7">32:7</span> Gathering together the waters of the sea,
as in a vessel; laying up the depths in storehouses.

<span id="an_32:8">32:8</span> Let all the earth fear the Lord, and let
all the inhabitants of the world be in awe of him.

<span id="an_32:9">32:9</span> For he spoke and they were made: he
commanded and they were created.

<span id="an_32:10">32:10</span> The Lord bringeth to naught the
counsels of nations; and he rejecteth the devices of people, and casteth
away the counsels of princes.

<span id="an_32:11">32:11</span> But the counsel of the Lord standeth
for ever: the thoughts of his heart to all generations.

<span id="an_32:12">32:12</span> Blessed is the nation whose God is the
Lord: the people whom he hath chosen for his inheritance.

<span id="an_32:13">32:13</span> The Lord hath looked from heaven: he
hath beheld all the sons of men.

<span id="an_32:14">32:14</span> From his habitation which he hath
prepared, he hath looked upon all that dwell on the earth.

<span id="an_32:15">32:15</span> He who hath made the hearts of every
one of them: who understandeth all their works.

<span id="an_32:16">32:16</span> The king is not saved by a great army:
nor shall the giant be saved by his own great strength.

<span id="an_32:17">32:17</span> Vain is the horse for safety: neither
shall he be saved by the abundance of his strength.

<span id="an_32:18">32:18</span> Behold the eyes of the Lord are on them
that fear him: and on them that hope in his mercy.

<span id="an_32:19">32:19</span> To deliver their souls from death; and
feed them in famine.

<span id="an_32:20">32:20</span> Our soul waiteth for the Lord: for he
is our helper and protector.

<span id="an_32:21">32:21</span> For in him our heart shall rejoice: and
in his holy name we have trusted.

<span id="an_32:22">32:22</span> Let thy mercy, O Lord, be upon us, as
we have hoped in thee.

<span id="an_33:1">33:1</span> For David, when he changed his
countenance before Achimelech, who dismissed him, and he went his way.
\[1 Kings 21.\]

<span id="an_33:2">33:2</span> I will bless the Lord at all times, his
praise shall be always in my mouth.

<span id="an_33:3">33:3</span> In the Lord shall my soul be praised: let
the meek hear and rejoice.

<span id="an_33:4">33:4</span> O magnify the Lord with me; and let us
extol his name together.

<span id="an_33:5">33:5</span> I sought the Lord, and he heard me; and
he delivered me from all my troubles.

<span id="an_33:6">33:6</span> Come ye to him and be enlightened: and
your faces shall not be confounded.

<span id="an_33:7">33:7</span> This poor man cried, and the Lord heard
him: and saved him out of all his troubles.

<span id="an_33:8">33:8</span> The angel of the Lord shall encamp round
about them that fear him: and shall deliver them.

<span id="an_33:9">33:9</span> O taste, and see that the Lord is sweet:
blessed is the man that hopeth in him.

<span id="an_33:10">33:10</span> Fear the Lord, all ye his saints: for
there is no want to them that fear him.

<span id="an_33:11">33:11</span> The rich have wanted, and have suffered
hunger: but they that seek the Lord shall not be deprived of any good.

<span id="an_33:12">33:12</span> Come, children, hearken to me: I will
teach you the fear of the Lord.

<span id="an_33:13">33:13</span> Who is the man that desireth life: who
loveth to see good days?

<span id="an_33:14">33:14</span> Keep thy tongue from evil, and thy lips
from speaking guile.

<span id="an_33:15">33:15</span> Turn away from evil and do good: seek
after peace and pursue it.

<span id="an_33:16">33:16</span> The eyes of the Lord are upon the just:
and his ears unto their prayers.

<span id="an_33:17">33:17</span> But the countenance of the Lord is
against them that do evil things: to cut off the remembrance of them
from the earth.

<span id="an_33:18">33:18</span> The just cried, and the Lord heard
them: and delivered them out of all their troubles.

<span id="an_33:19">33:19</span> The Lord is nigh unto them that are of
a contrite heart: and he will save the humble of spirit.

<span id="an_33:20">33:20</span> Many are the afflictions of the just;
but out of them all will the Lord deliver them.

<span id="an_33:21">33:21</span> The Lord keepeth all their bones, not
one of them shall be broken.

<span id="an_33:22">33:22</span> The death of the wicked is very evil:
and they that hate the just shall be guilty.

<span id="an_33:23">33:23</span> The Lord will redeem the souls of his
servants: and none of them that trust in him shall offend.

<span id="an_34:1">34:1</span> For David himself. Judge thou, O Lord,
them that wrong me : overthrow them that fight against me.

<span id="an_34:2">34:2</span> Take hold of arms and shield : and rise
up to help me.

<span id="an_34:3">34:3</span> Bring out the sword, and shut up the way
against them that persecute me : say to my soul : I am thy salvation.

<span id="an_34:4">34:4</span> Let them be confounded and ashamed that
seek after my soul. Let them be turned back and be confounded that
devise against me.

<span id="an_34:5">34:5</span> Let them become as dust before the wind :
and let the angel of the Lord straiten them.

<span id="an_34:6">34:6</span> Let their way become dark and slippery;
and let the angel of the Lord pursue them.

<span id="an_34:7">34:7</span> For without cause they have hidden their
net for me unto destruction : without cause they have upbraided my soul.

<span id="an_34:8">34:8</span> Let the snare which he knoweth not come
upon him : and let the net which he hath hidden catch him : and let the
net which he hath hidden catch him : and into that very snare let them
fall.

<span id="an_34:9">34:9</span> But my soul shall rejoice in the Lord;
and shall be delighted in his salvation.

<span id="an_34:10">34:10</span> All my bones shall say : Lord, who is
like to thee? Who deliverest the poor from the hand of them that are
stronger than he; the needy and the poor from them that strip him.

<span id="an_34:11">34:11</span> Unjust witnesses rising up have asked
me things I knew not.

<span id="an_34:12">34:12</span> They repaid me evil for good : to the
depriving me of my soul.

<span id="an_34:13">34:13</span> But as for me, when they were
troublesome to me, I was clothed with haircloth. I humbled my soul with
fasting; and my prayer shall be turned into my bosom.

<span id="an_34:14">34:14</span> As a neighbour and as an own brother,
so did I please : as one mourning and sorrowful so was I humbled.

<span id="an_34:15">34:15</span> But they rejoiced against me, and came
together : scourges were gathered together upon me, and I knew not.

<span id="an_34:16">34:16</span> They were separated, and repented not :
they tempted me, they scoffed at me with scorn : they gnashed upon me
with their teeth.

<span id="an_34:17">34:17</span> Lord, when wilt thou look upon me?
rescue thou soul from their malice : my only one from the lions.

<span id="an_34:18">34:18</span> I will give thanks to thee in a great
church; I will praise thee in a strong people.

<span id="an_34:19">34:19</span> Let not them that are my enemies
wrongfully rejoice over me : who have hated me without cause, and wink
with the eyes.

<span id="an_34:20">34:20</span> For they spoke indeed peaceably to me;
and speaking in the anger of the earth they devised guile.

<span id="an_34:21">34:21</span> And they opened their mouth wide
against me; they said : Well done, well done, our eyes have seen it.

<span id="an_34:22">34:22</span> Thou hast seen, O Lord, be not thou
silent : O Lord, depart not from me.

<span id="an_34:23">34:23</span> Arise, and be attentive to my judgment
: to my cause, my God, and my Lord.

<span id="an_34:24">34:24</span> Judge me, O Lord my God according to
thy justice, and let them not rejoice over me.

<span id="an_34:25">34:25</span> Let them not say in their hearts : It
is well, it is well, to our mind : neither let them say : We have
swallowed him up.

<span id="an_34:26">34:26</span> Let them blush : and be ashamed
together, who rejoice at my evils. Let them be clothed with confusion
and shame, who speak great things against me.

<span id="an_34:27">34:27</span> Let them rejoice and be glad, who are
well pleased with my justice, and let them say always : The Lord be
magnified, who delights in the peace of his servant.

<span id="an_34:28">34:28</span> Any my tongue shall meditate thy
justice, thy praise all the day long.

<span id="an_35:1">35:1</span> Unto the end, for the servant of God,
David himself.

<span id="an_35:2">35:2</span> The unjust hath said within himself, that
he would sin : there is no fear of God before his eyes.

<span id="an_35:3">35:3</span> For in his sight he hath done
deceitfully, that his iniquity may be found unto hatred.

<span id="an_35:4">35:4</span> The words of his mouth are iniquity and
guile : he would not understand that he might do well.

<span id="an_35:5">35:5</span> He hath devised iniquity on his bed, he
hath set himself on every way that is not good : but evil he hath not
hated.

<span id="an_35:6">35:6</span> O Lord, thy mercy is in heaven, and thy
truth reacheth, even to the clouds.

<span id="an_35:7">35:7</span> Thy justice is as the mountains of God,
thy judgments are a great deep. Men and beasts thou wilt preserve, O
Lord :

<span id="an_35:8">35:8</span> O how hast thou multiplied thy mercy, O
God! But the children of men shall put their trust under the covert of
thy wings.

<span id="an_35:9">35:9</span> They shall be inebriated with the plenty
of thy house; and thou shalt make them drink of the torrent of thy
pleasure.

<span id="an_35:10">35:10</span> For with thee is the fountain of life;
and in thy light we shall see light.

<span id="an_35:11">35:11</span> Extend thy mercy to them that know
thee, and thy justice to them that are right in heart.

<span id="an_35:12">35:12</span> Let not the foot of pride come to me,
and let not the hand of the sinner move me.

<span id="an_35:13">35:13</span> There the workers of iniquity are
fallen, they are cast out, and could not stand.

<span id="an_36:1">36:1</span> A psalm for David himself. Be not emulous
of evildoers; nor envy them that work iniquity.

<span id="an_36:2">36:2</span> For they shall shortly wither away as
grass, and as the green herbs shall quickly fall.

<span id="an_36:3">36:3</span> Trust in the Lord, and do good, and dwell
in the land, and thou shalt be fed with its riches.

<span id="an_36:4">36:4</span> Delight in the Lord, and he will give
thee the requests of thy heart.

<span id="an_36:5">36:5</span> Commit thy way to the Lord, and trust in
him, and he will do it.

<span id="an_36:6">36:6</span> And he will bring forth thy justice as
the light, and thy judgment as the noonday.

<span id="an_36:7">36:7</span> Be subject to the Lord and pray to him
Envy not the man who prospereth in his way; the man who doth unjust
things.

<span id="an_36:8">36:8</span> Cease from anger, and leave rage; have no
emulation to do evil.

<span id="an_36:9">36:9</span> For the evildoers shall be cut off : but
they that wait upon the Lord shall inherit the land.

<span id="an_36:10">36:10</span> For yet a little while, and the wicked
shall not be : and thou shalt seek his place, and shalt not find it.

<span id="an_36:11">36:11</span> But the meek shall inherit the land,
and shall delight in abundance of peace.

<span id="an_36:12">36:12</span> The sinner shall watch the just man :
and shall gnash upon him with his teeth.

<span id="an_36:13">36:13</span> But the Lord shall laugh at him : for
he foreseeth that his day shall come.

<span id="an_36:14">36:14</span> The wicked have drawn out the sword :
they have bent their bow. To cast down the poor and needy, to kill the
upright of heart.

<span id="an_36:15">36:15</span> Let their sword enter into their own
hearts, and let their bow be broken.

<span id="an_36:16">36:16</span> Better is a little to the just, than
the great riches of the wicked.

<span id="an_36:17">36:17</span> For the arms of the wicked shall be
broken in pieces; but the Lord strengtheneth the just.

<span id="an_36:18">36:18</span> The Lord knoweth the days of undefiled;
and their inheritance shall be for ever.

<span id="an_36:19">36:19</span> They shall not be confounded in the
evil time; and in the days of famine they shall be filled :

<span id="an_36:20">36:20</span> because the wicked shall perish. And
the enemies of the Lord, presently after they shall be honoured and
exalted, shall come to nothing and vanish like smoke.

<span id="an_36:21">36:21</span> The sinner shall borrow, and not pay
again; but the just sheweth mercy and shall give.

<span id="an_36:22">36:22</span> For such as bless him shall inherit the
land : but such as curse him shall perish.

<span id="an_36:23">36:23</span> With the Lord shall the steps of a man
be directed, and he shall like well his way.

<span id="an_36:24">36:24</span> When he shall fall he shall not be
bruised, for the Lord putteth his hand under him.

<span id="an_36:25">36:25</span> I have been young, and now am old; and
I have not seen the just forsaken, nor his seed seeking bread.

<span id="an_36:26">36:26</span> He sheweth mercy, and lendeth all the
day long; and his seed shall be in blessing.

<span id="an_36:27">36:27</span> Decline from evil and do good, and
dwell for ever and ever.

<span id="an_36:28">36:28</span> For the Lord loveth judgment, and will
not forsake his saints : they shall be preserved for ever. The unjust
shall be punished, and the seed of the wicked shall perish.

<span id="an_36:29">36:29</span> But the just shall inherit the land,
and shall dwell therein for evermore.

<span id="an_36:30">36:30</span> The mouth of the just shall meditate
wisdom : and his tongue shall speak judgment.

<span id="an_36:31">36:31</span> The law of his God is in his heart, and
his steps shall not be supplanted.

<span id="an_36:32">36:32</span> The wicked watcheth the just man, and
seeketh to put him to death,

<span id="an_36:33">36:33</span> But the Lord will not leave in his
hands; nor condemn him when he shall be judged.

<span id="an_36:34">36:34</span> Expect the Lord and keep his way : and
he will exalt thee to inherit the land : when the sinners shall perish
thou shalt see.

<span id="an_36:35">36:35</span> I have seen the wicked highly exalted,
and lifted up like the cedars of Libanus.

<span id="an_36:36">36:36</span> And I passed by, and lo, he was not :
and I sought him and his place was not found.

<span id="an_36:37">36:37</span> Keep innocence, and behold justice :
for there are remnants for the peaceable man.

<span id="an_36:38">36:38</span> But the unjust shall be destroyed
together : the remnants of the wicked shall perish.

<span id="an_36:39">36:39</span> But the salvation of the just is from
the Lord, and he is their protector in the time of trouble.

<span id="an_36:40">36:40</span> And the Lord will help them and deliver
them : and he will rescue them from the wicked, and save them, because
they have hoped in him.

<span id="an_37:1">37:1</span> A psalm for David, for a remembrance of
the sabbath.

<span id="an_37:2">37:2</span> Rebuke me not, O Lord, in thy
indignation; nor chastise me in thy wrath.

<span id="an_37:3">37:3</span> For thy arrows are fastened in me : and
thy hand hath been strong upon me.

<span id="an_37:4">37:4</span> There is no health in my flesh, because
of thy wrath : there is no peace for my bones, because of my sins.

<span id="an_37:5">37:5</span> For my iniquities are gone over my head :
and as a heavy burden are become heavy upon me.

<span id="an_37:6">37:6</span> My sores are putrified and corrupted,
because of my foolishness.

<span id="an_37:7">37:7</span> I am become miserable, and am bowed down
even to the end : I walked sorrowful all the day long.

<span id="an_37:8">37:8</span> For my loins are filled with illusions;
and there is no health in my flesh.

<span id="an_37:9">37:9</span> I am afflicted and humbled exceedingly :
I roared with the groaning of my heart.

<span id="an_37:10">37:10</span> Lord, all my desire is before thee, and
my groaning is not hidden from thee.

<span id="an_37:11">37:11</span> My heart is troubled, my strength hath
left me, and the light of my eyes itself is not with me.

<span id="an_37:12">37:12</span> My friends and my neighbours have drawn
near, and stood against me. And they that were near me stood afar off :

<span id="an_37:13">37:13</span> And they that sought my soul used
violence. And they that sought evils to me spoke vain things, and
studied deceits all the day long.

<span id="an_37:14">37:14</span> But I, as a deaf man, heard not : and
as a dumb man not opening his mouth.

<span id="an_37:15">37:15</span> And I became as a man that heareth not
: and that hath no reproofs in his mouth.

<span id="an_37:16">37:16</span> For in thee, O Lord, have I hoped :
thou wilt hear me, O Lord my God.

<span id="an_37:17">37:17</span> For I said: Lest at any time my enemies
rejoice over me : and whilst my feet are moved, they speak great things
against me.

<span id="an_37:18">37:18</span> For I am ready for scourges : and my
sorrow is continually before me.

<span id="an_37:19">37:19</span> For I will declare my inequity : and I
will think for my sin.

<span id="an_37:20">37:20</span> But my enemies live, and are stronger
that I : and they hate me wrongfully are multiplied.

<span id="an_37:21">37:21</span> They that render evil for good, have
detracted me, because I followed goodness.

<span id="an_37:22">37:22</span> Forsake me not, O Lord my God : do not
thou depart from me.

<span id="an_37:23">37:23</span> Attend unto my help, O Lord, the God of
my salvation.

<span id="an_38:1">38:1</span> Unto the end, for Idithun himself, a
canticle of David.

<span id="an_38:2">38:2</span> I said: I will take heed to my ways :
that I sin not with my tongue. I have set guard to my mouth, when the
sinner stood against me.

<span id="an_38:3">38:3</span> I was dumb, and was humbled, and kept
silence from good things : and my sorrow was renewed.

<span id="an_38:4">38:4</span> My heart grew hot within me : and in my
meditation a fire shall flame out.

<span id="an_38:5">38:5</span> I spoke with my tongue : O Lord, make me
know my end. And what is the number of my days : that I may know what is
wanting to me.

<span id="an_38:6">38:6</span> Behold thou hast made my days measurable
: and my substance is as nothing before thee. And indeed all things are
vanity : every man living.

<span id="an_38:7">38:7</span> Surely man passeth as an image : yea, and
he is disquieted in vain. He storeth up : and he knoweth not for whom he
shall gather these things.

<span id="an_38:8">38:8</span> And now what is my hope? is it not the
Lord? and my substance is with thee.

<span id="an_38:9">38:9</span> Deliver thou me from all my iniquities :
thou hast made me a reproach to the fool.

<span id="an_38:10">38:10</span> I was dumb, and I opened not my mouth,
because thou hast done it.

<span id="an_38:11">38:11</span> Remove thy scourges from me. The
strength of thy hand hath made me faint in rebukes:

<span id="an_38:12">38:12</span> thou hast corrected man for iniquity.
And thou hast made his soul to waste away like a spider : surely in vain
is any man disquieted.

<span id="an_38:13">38:13</span> Hear my prayer, O Lord, and my
supplication : give ear to my tears. Be not silent : for I am a stranger
with thee, and a sojourner as all my fathers were.

<span id="an_38:14">38:14</span> O forgive me, that I may be refreshed,
before I go hence, and be no more.

<span id="an_39:1">39:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David himself.

<span id="an_39:2">39:2</span> With expectation I have waited for the
Lord, and he was attentive to me.

<span id="an_39:3">39:3</span> And he heard my prayers, and brought me
out of the pit of misery and the mire of dregs. And he set my feet upon
a rock, and directed my steps.

<span id="an_39:4">39:4</span> And he put a new canticle into my mouth,
a song to our God. Many shall see, and shall fear : and they shall hope
in the Lord.

<span id="an_39:5">39:5</span> Blessed is the man whose trust is in the
name of the Lord; and who hath not had regard to vanities, and lying
follies.

<span id="an_39:6">39:6</span> Thou hast multiplied thy wonderful works,
