O Lord my God : and in thy thoughts there is no one like to thee. I have
declared and I have spoken they are multiplied above number.

<span id="an_39:7">39:7</span> Sacrifice and oblation thou didst not
desire; but thou hast pierced ears for me. Burnt offering and sin
offering thou didst not require :

<span id="an_39:8">39:8</span> then said I, Behold I come. In the head
of the book it is written of me

<span id="an_39:9">39:9</span> that I should do thy will : O my God, I
have desired it, and thy law in the midst of my heart.

<span id="an_39:10">39:10</span> I have declared thy justice in a great
church, lo, I will not restrain my lips : O Lord, thou knowest it.

<span id="an_39:11">39:11</span> I have not hid thy justice within my
heart : I have declared thy truth and thy salvation. I have not
concealed thy mercy and thy truth from a great council.

<span id="an_39:12">39:12</span> Withhold not thou, O Lord, thy tender
mercies from me : thy mercy and thy truth have always upheld me.

<span id="an_39:13">39:13</span> For evils without number have
surrounded me; my iniquities have overtaken me, and I was not able to
see. They are multiplied above the hairs of my head : and my heart hath
forsaken me.

<span id="an_39:14">39:14</span> Be pleased, O Lord, to deliver me, look
down, O Lord, to help me.

<span id="an_39:15">39:15</span> Let them be confounded and ashamed
together, that seek after my soul to take it away. Let them be turned
backward and be ashamed that desire evils to me.

<span id="an_39:16">39:16</span> Let them immediately bear their
confusion, that say to me : 'T is well, 't is well.

<span id="an_39:17">39:17</span> Let all that seek thee rejoice and be
glad in thee : and let such as love thy salvation say always : The Lord
be magnified.

<span id="an_39:18">39:18</span> But I am a beggar and poor : the Lord
is careful for me. Thou art my helper and my protector : O my God, be
not slack.

<span id="an_40:1">40:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David himself.

<span id="an_40:2">40:2</span> Blessed is he that understandeth
concerning the needy and the poor : the Lord will deliver him in the
evil day.

<span id="an_40:3">40:3</span> The Lord preserve him and give him life,
and make him blessed upon the earth : and deliver him not up to the will
of his enemies.

<span id="an_40:4">40:4</span> The Lord help him on his bed of sorrow :
thou hast turned all his couch in his sickness.

<span id="an_40:5">40:5</span> I said: O Lord, be thou merciful to me :
heal my soul, for I have sinned against thee.

<span id="an_40:6">40:6</span> My enemies have spoken evils against me:
when shall he die and his name perish?

<span id="an_40:7">40:7</span> And if he came in to see me, he spoke
vain things : his heart gathered together iniquity to itself. He went
out and spoke to the same purpose.

<span id="an_40:8">40:8</span> All my enemies whispered together against
me : they devised evils to me.

<span id="an_40:9">40:9</span> They determined against me an unjust word
: shall he that sleepeth rise again no more?

<span id="an_40:10">40:10</span> For even the man of peace, in whom I
trusted, who ate my bread, hath greatly supplanted me.

<span id="an_40:11">40:11</span> But thou, O Lord, have mercy on me, and
raise me up again : and I will requite them.

<span id="an_40:12">40:12</span> By this I know, that thou hast had a
good will for me : because my enemy shall not rejoice over me.

<span id="an_40:13">40:13</span> But thou hast upheld me by reason of my
innocence : and hast established me in thy sight for ever.

<span id="an_40:14">40:14</span> Blessed by the Lord the God of Israel
from eternity to eternity. So be it. So be it.

<span id="an_41:1">41:1</span> Unto the end, understanding for the sons
of Core.

<span id="an_41:2">41:2</span> As the hart panteth after the fountains
of water; so my soul panteth after thee, O God.

<span id="an_41:3">41:3</span> My soul hath thirsted after the strong
living God; when shall I come and appear before the face of God?

<span id="an_41:4">41:4</span> My tears have been any bread day and
night, whilst it is said to me daily : Where is thy God?

<span id="an_41:5">41:5</span> These things I remembered, and poured out
my soul in me : for I shall go over into the place of the wonderful
tabernacle, even to the house of God : With the voice of joy and praise;
the noise of one feasting.

<span id="an_41:6">41:6</span> Why art thou sad, O my soul? and why dost
thou trouble me? Hope in God, for I will still give praise to him : the
salvation of my countenance,

<span id="an_41:7">41:7</span> and my God. My soul is troubled within
myself : therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan and
Hermoniim, from the little hill.

<span id="an_41:8">41:8</span> Deep calleth on deep, at the noise of thy
flood-gates. All thy heights and thy billows have passed over me.

<span id="an_41:9">41:9</span> In the daytime the Lord hath commanded
his mercy; and a canticle to him in the night. With me is prayer to the
God of my life.

<span id="an_41:10">41:10</span> I will say to God : Thou art my
support. Why hast thou forgotten me? and why go I mourning, whilst my
enemy afflicteth me?

<span id="an_41:11">41:11</span> Whilst my bones are broken, my enemies
who trouble me have reproached me; Whilst they say to me day be day :
Where is thy God?

<span id="an_41:12">41:12</span> Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and
why dost thou disquiet me? Hope thou in God, for I will still give
praise to him : the salvation of my countenance, and my God.

<span id="an_42:1">42:1</span> A psalm for David. Judge me, O God, and
distinguish my cause from the nation that is not holy : deliver me from
the unjust and deceitful man.

<span id="an_42:2">42:2</span> For thou art God my strength : why hast
thou cast me off? and why do I go sorrowful whilst the enemy afflicteth
me?

<span id="an_42:3">42:3</span> Send forth thy light and thy truth : they
have conducted me, and brought me unto thy holy hill, and into thy
tabernacles.

<span id="an_42:4">42:4</span> And I will go in to the altar of God : to
God who giveth joy to my youth.

<span id="an_42:5">42:5</span> To thee, O God my God, I will give praise
upon the harp : why art thou sad, O my soul? and why dost thou disquiet
me?

<span id="an_42:6">42:6</span> Hope in God, for I will still give praise
to him : the salvation of my countenance, and my God.

<span id="an_43:1">43:1</span> Unto the end, for the sons of Core, to
give understanding.

<span id="an_43:2">43:2</span> We have heard, O God, with our ears : our
fathers have declared to us, The work, thou hast wrought in their days,
and in the days of old.

<span id="an_43:3">43:3</span> Thy hand destroyed the Gentiles, and thou
plantedst them : thou didst afflict the people and cast them out.

<span id="an_43:4">43:4</span> For they got not the possession of the
land by their own sword : neither did their own arm save them. But thy
right hand and thy arm, and the light of thy countenance : because thou
wast pleased with them.

<span id="an_43:5">43:5</span> Thou art thyself my king and my God, who
commandest the saving of Jacob.

<span id="an_43:6">43:6</span> Through thee we will push down our
enemies with the horn : and through thy name we will despise them that
rise up against us.

<span id="an_43:7">43:7</span> For I will not trust in my bow : neither
shall my sword save me.

<span id="an_43:8">43:8</span> But thou hast saved us from them that
afflict us : and hast put them to shame that hate us.

<span id="an_43:9">43:9</span> In God shall we glory all the day long :
and in thy name we will give praise for ever.

<span id="an_43:10">43:10</span> But now thou hast cast us off, and put
us to shame : and thou, O God, wilt not go out with our armies.

<span id="an_43:11">43:11</span> Thou hast made us turn our back to our
enemies : and they that hated us plundered for themselves.

<span id="an_43:12">43:12</span> Thou hast given us up like sheep to be
eaten : thou hast scattered us among the nations.

<span id="an_43:13">43:13</span> Thou hast sold thy people for no price
: and there was no reckoning in the exchange of them.

<span id="an_43:14">43:14</span> Thou hast made us a reproach to our
neighbours, a scoff and derision to them that are round about us.

<span id="an_43:15">43:15</span> Thou hast made us a byword among the
Gentiles : a shaking of the head among the people.

<span id="an_43:16">43:16</span> All the day long my shame is before me
: and the confusion of my face hath covered me,

<span id="an_43:17">43:17</span> At the voice of him that reproacheth
and detracteth me : at the face of the enemy and persecutor.

<span id="an_43:18">43:18</span> All these things have come upon us, yet
we have not forgotten thee : and we have not done wickedly in they
covenant.

<span id="an_43:19">43:19</span> And our heart hath not turned back :
neither hast thou turned aside our steps from thy way.

<span id="an_43:20">43:20</span> For thou hast humbled us in the place
of affliction : and the shadow of death hath covered us.

<span id="an_43:21">43:21</span> If we have forgotten the name of our
God, and if we have spread forth our hands to a strange god :

<span id="an_43:22">43:22</span> Shall not God search out these things :
for he knoweth the secrets of the heart. Because for thy sake we are
killed all the day long : we are counted as sheep for the slaughter.

<span id="an_43:23">43:23</span> Arise, why sleepest thou, O Lord?
arise, and cast us not off to the end.

<span id="an_43:24">43:24</span> Why turnest thou face away? and
forgettest our want and our trouble?

<span id="an_43:25">43:25</span> For our soul is humbled down to the
dust : our belly cleaveth to the earth.

<span id="an_43:26">43:26</span> Arise, O Lord, help us and redeem us
for thy name's sake.

<span id="an_44:1">44:1</span> Unto the end, for them that shall be
changed, for the sons of Core, for understanding. A canticle for the
Beloved.

<span id="an_44:2">44:2</span> My heart hath uttered a good word I speak
my works to the king; My tongue is the pen of a scrivener that writeth
swiftly.

<span id="an_44:3">44:3</span> Thou art beautiful above the sons of men:
grace is poured abroad in thy lips; therefore hath God blessed thee for
ever

<span id="an_44:4">44:4</span> Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O thou
most mighty.

<span id="an_44:5">44:5</span> With thy comeliness and thy beauty set
out, proceed prosperously, and reign. Because of truth and meekness and
justice: and thy right hand shall conduct thee wonderfully.

<span id="an_44:6">44:6</span> Thy arrows are sharp: under thee shall
people fall, into the hearts of the king's enemies.

<span id="an_44:7">44:7</span> Thy throne, O God, is for ever and ever:
the sceptre of thy kingdom is a sceptre of uprightness.

<span id="an_44:8">44:8</span> Thou hast loved justice, and hated
iniquity: therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of
gladness above thy fellows.

<span id="an_44:9">44:9</span> Myrrh and stacte and cassia perfume thy
garments, from the ivory houses: out of which

<span id="an_44:10">44:10</span> the daughters of kings have delighted
thee in thy glory. The queen stood on thy right hand, in gilded
clothing; surrounded with variety.

<span id="an_44:11">44:11</span> Hearken, O daughter, and see, and
incline thy ear: and forget thy people and thy father's house.

<span id="an_44:12">44:12</span> And the king shall greatly desire thy
beauty; for he is the Lord thy God, and him they shall adore.

<span id="an_44:13">44:13</span> And the daughters of Tyre with gifts,
yea, all the rich among the people, shall entreat thy countenance.

<span id="an_44:14">44:14</span> All the glory of the king's daughter is
within in golden borders,

<span id="an_44:15">44:15</span> clothed round about with varieties.
After her shall virgins be brought to the king: her neighbours shall be
brought to thee.

<span id="an_44:16">44:16</span> They shall be brought with gladness and
rejoicing: they shall be brought into the temple of the king.

<span id="an_44:17">44:17</span> Instead of thy fathers, sons are born
to thee: thou shalt make them princes over all the earth.

<span id="an_44:18">44:18</span> They shall remember thy name throughout
all generations. Therefore shall people praise thee for ever; yea, for
ever and ever.

<span id="an_45:1">45:1</span> Unto the end, for the sons of Core, for
the hidden.

<span id="an_45:2">45:2</span> Our God is our refuge and strength: a
helper in troubles, which have found us exceedingly.

<span id="an_45:3">45:3</span> Therefore we will not fear, when the
earth shall be troubled; and the mountains shall be removed into the
heart of the sea.

<span id="an_45:4">45:4</span> Their waters roared and were troubled:
the mountains were troubled with his strength.

<span id="an_45:5">45:5</span> The stream of the river maketh the city
of God joyful: the most High hath sanctified his own tabernacle.

<span id="an_45:6">45:6</span> God is in the midst thereof, it shall not
be moved: God will help it in the morning early.

<span id="an_45:7">45:7</span> Nations were troubled, and kingdoms were
bowed down: he uttered his voice, the earth trembled.

<span id="an_45:8">45:8</span> The Lord of armies is with us: the God of
Jacob is our protector.

<span id="an_45:9">45:9</span> Come and behold ye the works of the Lord:
what wonders he hath done upon earth,

<span id="an_45:10">45:10</span> making wars to cease even to the end of
the earth. He shall destroy the bow, and break the weapons: and the
shield he shall burn in the fire.

<span id="an_45:11">45:11</span> Be still and see that I am God; I will
be exalted among the nations, and I will be exalted in the earth.

<span id="an_45:12">45:12</span> The Lord of armies is with us: the God
of Jacob is our protector.

<span id="an_46:1">46:1</span> Unto the end, for the sons of Core.

<span id="an_46:2">46:2</span> O clap your hands, all ye nations: shout
unto God with the voice of Joy,

<span id="an_46:3">46:3</span> For the Lord is high, terrible: a great
king over all the earth.

<span id="an_46:4">46:4</span> He hath subdued the people under us; and
the nations under our feet.

<span id="an_46:5">46:5</span> He hath chosen for us his inheritance the
beauty of Jacob which he hath loved.

<span id="an_46:6">46:6</span> God is ascended with jubilee, and the
Lord with the sound of trumpet.

<span id="an_46:7">46:7</span> Sing praises to our God, sing ye: sing
praises to our king, sing ye.

<span id="an_46:8">46:8</span> For God is the king of all the earth:
sing ye wisely.

<span id="an_46:9">46:9</span> God shall reign over the nations: God
sitteth on his holy throne.

<span id="an_46:10">46:10</span> The princes of the people are gathered
together, with the God of Abraham: for the strong gods of the earth are
exceedingly exalted.

<span id="an_47:1">47:1</span> A psalm of a canticle, for the sons of
Core, on the second day of the week.

<span id="an_47:2">47:2</span> Great is the Lord, and exceedingly to be
praised in the city of our God, in his holy mountain.

<span id="an_47:3">47:3</span> With the joy of the whole earth is mount
Sion founded, on the sides of the north, the city of the great king.

<span id="an_47:4">47:4</span> In her houses shall God be known, when he
shall protect her.

<span id="an_47:5">47:5</span> For behold the kings of the earth
assembled themselves: they gathered together.

<span id="an_47:6">47:6</span> So they saw, and they wondered, they were
troubled, they were moved:

<span id="an_47:7">47:7</span> trembling took hold of them. There were
pains as of a woman in labour.

<span id="an_47:8">47:8</span> With a vehement wind thou shalt break in
pieces the ships of Tharsis.

<span id="an_47:9">47:9</span> As we have heard, so have we seen, in the
city of the Lord of hosts, in the city of our God: God hath founded it
for ever.

<span id="an_47:10">47:10</span> We have received thy mercy, O God, in
the midst of thy temple.

<span id="an_47:11">47:11</span> According to thy name, O God, so also
is thy praise unto the ends of the earth: thy right hand is full of
justice.

<span id="an_47:12">47:12</span> Let mount Sion rejoice, and the
daughters of Juda be glad; because of thy judgments, O Lord.

<span id="an_47:13">47:13</span> Surround Sion, and encompass her: tell
ye in her towers.

<span id="an_47:14">47:14</span> Set your hearts on her strength; and
distribute her houses, that ye may relate it in another generation.

<span id="an_47:15">47:15</span> For this is God, our God unto eternity,
and for ever and ever: he shall rule us for evermore.

<span id="an_48:1">48:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for the sons of
Core.

<span id="an_48:2">48:2</span> Hear these things, all ye nations: give
ear, all ye inhabitants of the world.

<span id="an_48:3">48:3</span> All you that are earthborn, and you sons
of men: both rich and poor together.

<span id="an_48:4">48:4</span> My mouth shall speak wisdom: and the
meditation of my heart understanding.

<span id="an_48:5">48:5</span> I will incline my ear to a parable; I
will open my proposition on the psaltery.

<span id="an_48:6">48:6</span> Why shall I fear in the evil day? the
iniquity of my heel shall encompass me.

<span id="an_48:7">48:7</span> They that trust in their own strength,
and glory in the multitude of their riches,

<span id="an_48:8">48:8</span> No brother can redeem, nor shall man
redeem: he shall not give to God his ransom,

<span id="an_48:9">48:9</span> Nor the price of the redemption of his
soul: and shall labour for ever,

<span id="an_48:10">48:10</span> and shall still live unto the end.

<span id="an_48:11">48:11</span> He shall not see destruction, when he
shall see the wise dying: the senseless and the fool shall perish
together: And they shall leave their riches to strangers:

<span id="an_48:12">48:12</span> and their sepulchres shall be their
houses for ever. Their dwelling places to all generations: they have
called their lands by their names.

<span id="an_48:13">48:13</span> And man when he was in honour did not
understand; he is compared to senseless beasts, and is become like to
them.

<span id="an_48:14">48:14</span> This way of theirs is a stumblingblock
to them: and afterwards they shall delight in their mouth.

<span id="an_48:15">48:15</span> They are laid in hell like sheep: death
shall feed upon them. And the just shall have dominion over them in the
morning; and their help shall decay in hell from their glory.

<span id="an_48:16">48:16</span> But God will redeem my soul from the
hand of hell, when he shall receive me.

<span id="an_48:17">48:17</span> Be not thou afraid, when a man shall be
made rich, and when the glory of his house shall be increased.

<span id="an_48:18">48:18</span> For when he shall die he shall take
nothing away; nor shall his glory descend with him.

<span id="an_48:19">48:19</span> For in his lifetime his soul will be
blessed: and he will praise thee when thou shalt do well to him.

<span id="an_48:20">48:20</span> He shall go in to the generations of
his fathers: and he shall never see light.

<span id="an_48:21">48:21</span> Man when he was in honour did not
understand: he hath been compared to senseless beasts, and made like to
them.

<span id="an_49:1">49:1</span> A psalm for Asaph. The God of gods, the
Lord hath spoken: and he hath called the earth. From the rising of the
sun, to the going down thereof:

<span id="an_49:2">49:2</span> out of Sion the loveliness of his beauty.

<span id="an_49:3">49:3</span> God shall come manifestly: our God shall
come, and shall not keep silence. A fire shall burn before him: and a
mighty tempest shall be round about him.

<span id="an_49:4">49:4</span> He shall call heaven from above, and the
earth, to judge his people.

<span id="an_49:5">49:5</span> Gather ye together his saints to him: who
set his covenant before sacrifices.

<span id="an_49:6">49:6</span> And the heavens shall declare his
justice: for God is judge.

<span id="an_49:7">49:7</span> Hear, O my people, and I will speak: O
Israel, and I will testify to thee: I am God, thy God.

<span id="an_49:8">49:8</span> I will not reprove thee for thy
sacrifices: and thy burnt offerings are always in my sight.

<span id="an_49:9">49:9</span> I will not take calves out of thy house:
nor he goats out of thy flocks.

<span id="an_49:10">49:10</span> For all the beasts of the woods are
mine: the cattle on the hills, and the oxen.

<span id="an_49:11">49:11</span> I know all the fowls of the air: and
with me is the beauty of the field.

<span id="an_49:12">49:12</span> If I should be hungry, I would not tell
thee: for the world is mine, and the fulness thereof.

<span id="an_49:13">49:13</span> Shall I eat the flesh of bullocks? or
shall I drink the blood of goats?

<span id="an_49:14">49:14</span> Offer to God the sacrifice of praise:
and pay thy vows to the most High.

<span id="an_49:15">49:15</span> And call upon me in the day of trouble:
I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me.

<span id="an_49:16">49:16</span> But to the sinner God hath said: Why
dost thou declare my justices, and take my covenant in thy mouth ?

<span id="an_49:17">49:17</span> Seeing thou hast hated discipline: and
hast cast my words behind thee.

<span id="an_49:18">49:18</span> If thou didst see a thief thou didst
run with him: and with adulterers thou hast been a partaker.

<span id="an_49:19">49:19</span> Thy mouth hath abounded with evil, and
thy tongue framed deceits.

<span id="an_49:20">49:20</span> Sitting thou didst speak against thy
brother, and didst lay a scandal against thy mother's son:

<span id="an_49:21">49:21</span> these things hast thou done, and I was
silent. Thou thoughtest unjustly that I should be like to thee: but I
will reprove thee, and set before thy face.

<span id="an_49:22">49:22</span> Understand these things, you that
forget God; lest he snatch you away, and there be none to deliver you.

<span id="an_49:23">49:23</span> The sacrifice of praise shall glorify
me: and there is the way by which I will shew him the salvation of God.

<span id="an_50:1">50:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm of David,

<span id="an_50:2">50:2</span> when Nathan the prophet came to him after
he had sinned with Bethsabee.

<span id="an_50:3">50:3</span> Have mercy on me, O God, according to thy
great mercy. And according to the multitude of thy tender mercies blot
out my iniquity.

<span id="an_50:4">50:4</span> Wash me yet more from my iniquity, and
cleanse me from my sin.

<span id="an_50:5">50:5</span> For I know my iniquity, and my sin is
always before me.

<span id="an_50:6">50:6</span> To thee only have I sinned, and have done
evil before thee: that thou mayst be justified in thy words and mayst
overcome when thou art judged.

<span id="an_50:7">50:7</span> For behold I was conceived in iniquities;
and in sins did my mother conceive me.

<span id="an_50:8">50:8</span> For behold thou hast loved truth: the
uncertain and hidden things of thy wisdom thou hast made manifest to me.

<span id="an_50:9">50:9</span> Thou shalt sprinkle me with hyssop, and I
shall be cleansed: thou shalt wash me, and I shall be made whiter than
snow.

<span id="an_50:10">50:10</span> To my hearing thou shalt give joy and
gladness: and the bones that have been humbled shall rejoice.

<span id="an_50:11">50:11</span> Turn away thy face from my sins, and
blot out all my iniquities.

<span id="an_50:12">50:12</span> Create a clean heart in me, O God: and
renew a right spirit within my bowels.

<span id="an_50:13">50:13</span> Cast me not away from thy face; and
take not thy holy spirit from me.

<span id="an_50:14">50:14</span> Restore unto me the joy of thy
salvation, and strengthen me with a perfect spirit.

<span id="an_50:15">50:15</span> I will teach the unjust thy ways: and
the wicked shall be converted to thee.

<span id="an_50:16">50:16</span> Deliver me from blood, O God, thou God
of my salvation: and my tongue shall extol thy justice.

<span id="an_50:17">50:17</span> O Lord, thou wilt open my lips: and my
mouth shall declare thy praise.

<span id="an_50:18">50:18</span> For if thou hadst desired sacrifice, I
would indeed have given it: with burnt offerings thou wilt not be
delighted.

<span id="an_50:19">50:19</span> A sacrifice to God is an afflicted
spirit: a contrite and humbled heart, O God, thou wilt not despise.

<span id="an_50:20">50:20</span> Deal favourably, O Lord, in thy good
will with Sion; that the walls of Jerusalem may be built up.

<span id="an_50:21">50:21</span> Then shalt thou accept the sacrifice of
justice, oblations and whole burnt offerings: then shall they lay calves
upon thy altar.

<span id="an_51:1">51:1</span> Unto the end, understanding for David,

<span id="an_51:2">51:2</span> when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul
David went to the house of Achimelech

<span id="an_51:3">51:3</span> Why dost thou glory in malice, thou that
art mighty in iniquity?

<span id="an_51:4">51:4</span> All the day long thy tongue hath devised
injustice: as a sharp razor, thou hast wrought deceit.

<span id="an_51:5">51:5</span> Thou hast loved malice more than
goodness: and iniquity rather than to speak righteousness.

<span id="an_51:6">51:6</span> Thou hast loved all the words of ruin, O
deceitful tongue.

<span id="an_51:7">51:7</span> Therefore will God destroy thee for ever:
he will pluck thee out, and remove thee from thy dwelling place: and thy
root out of the land of the living.

<span id="an_51:8">51:8</span> The just shall see and fear, and shall
laugh at him, and say:

<span id="an_51:9">51:9</span> Behold the man that made not God his
helper: But trusted in the abundance of his riches: and prevailed in his
vanity.

<span id="an_51:10">51:10</span> But I, as a fruitful olive tree in the
house of God, have hoped in the mercy of God for ever, yea for ever and
ever.

<span id="an_51:11">51:11</span> I will praise thee for ever, because
thou hast done it: and I will wait on thy name, for it is good in the
sight of thy saints.

<span id="an_52:1">52:1</span> Unto the end, for Maeleth, understandings
to David. The fool said in his hear t: There is no God.

<span id="an_52:2">52:2</span> They are corrupted, and become abominable
in iniquities: there is none that doth good.

<span id="an_52:3">52:3</span> God looked down from heaven on the
children of men: to see if there were any that did understand, or did
seek God.

<span id="an_52:4">52:4</span> All have gone aside, they are become
unprofitable together, there is none that doth good, no not one.

<span id="an_52:5">52:5</span> Shall not all the workers of iniquity
know, who eat up my people as they eat bread?

<span id="an_52:6">52:6</span> They have not called upon God: there have
they trembled for fear, where there was no fear. For God hath scattered
the bones of them that please men: they have been confounded, because
God hath despised them.

<span id="an_52:7">52:7</span> Who will give out of Sion the salvation
of Israel? when God shall bring back the captivity of his people, Jacob
shall rejoice, and Israel shall be glad.

<span id="an_53:1">53:1</span> Unto the end, In verses, understanding
for David.

<span id="an_53:2">53:2</span> When the men of Ziph had come and said to
Saul: Is not David hidden with us?

<span id="an_53:3">53:3</span> Save me, O God, by thy name, and judge me
in thy strength.

<span id="an_53:4">53:4</span> O God, hear my prayer: give ear to the
words of my mouth.

<span id="an_53:5">53:5</span> For strangers have risen up against me;
and the mighty have sought after my soul: and they have not set God
before their eyes.

<span id="an_53:6">53:6</span> For behold God is my helper: and the Lord
is the protector of my soul.

<span id="an_53:7">53:7</span> Turn back the evils upon my enemies; and
cut them off in thy truth.

<span id="an_53:8">53:8</span> I will freely sacrifice to thee, and will
give praise, O God, to thy name: because it is good:

<span id="an_53:9">53:9</span> For thou hast delivered me out of all
trouble: and my eye hath looked down upon my enemies.

<span id="an_54:1">54:1</span> Unto the end, in verses, understanding
for David.

<span id="an_54:2">54:2</span> Hear, O God, my prayer, and despise not
my supplication:

<span id="an_54:3">54:3</span> be attentive to me and hear me. I am
grieved in my exercise; and am troubled,

<span id="an_54:4">54:4</span> at the voice of the enemy, and at the
tribulation of the sinner. For they have cast iniquities upon me: and in
wrath they were troublesome to me.

<span id="an_54:5">54:5</span> My heart is troubled within me: and the
fear of death is fallen upon me.

<span id="an_54:6">54:6</span> Fear and trembling are come upon me: and
darkness hath covered me.

<span id="an_54:7">54:7</span> And I said: Who will give me wings like a
dove, and I will fly and be at rest?

<span id="an_54:8">54:8</span> Lo, I have gone far off flying away; and
I abode in the wilderness.

<span id="an_54:9">54:9</span> I waited for him that hath saved me from
pusillanimity of spirit, and a storm.

<span id="an_54:10">54:10</span> Cast down, O Lord, and divide their
tongues; for I have seen iniquity and contradiction in the city.

<span id="an_54:11">54:11</span> Day and night shall iniquity surround
it upon its walls: and in the midst thereof are labour,

<span id="an_54:12">54:12</span> and injustice. And usury and deceit
have not departed from its streets.

<span id="an_54:13">54:13</span> For if my enemy had reviled me, I would
verily have borne with it. And if he that hated me had spoken great
things against me, I would perhaps have hidden myself from him.

<span id="an_54:14">54:14</span> But thou a man of one mind, my guide,
and my familiar,

<span id="an_54:15">54:15</span> Who didst take sweetmeats together with
me: in the house of God we walked with consent.

<span id="an_54:16">54:16</span> Let death come upon them, and let them
go down alive into hell. For there is wickedness in their dwellings: in
the midst of them.

<span id="an_54:17">54:17</span> But I have cried to God: and the Lord
will save me.

<span id="an_54:18">54:18</span> Evening and morning, and at noon I will
speak and declare: and he shall hear my voice.

<span id="an_54:19">54:19</span> He shall redeem my soul in peace from
them that draw near to me: for among many they were with me.

<span id="an_54:20">54:20</span> God shall hear, and the Eternal shall
humble them. For there is no change with them, and they have not feared
God:

<span id="an_54:21">54:21</span> he hath stretched forth his hand to
repay. They have defiled his covenant,

<span id="an_54:22">54:22</span> they are divided by the wrath Of his
countenance, and his heart hath drawn near. His words are smoother than
oil, and the same are darts.

<span id="an_54:23">54:23</span> Cast thy care upon the Lord, and he
shall sustain thee: he shall not suffer the just to waver for ever.

<span id="an_54:24">54:24</span> But thou, O God, shalt bring them down
into the pit of destruction. Bloody and deceitful men shall not live out
half their days; but I will trust in thee, O Lord.

<span id="an_55:1">55:1</span> Unto the end, for a people that is
removed at a distance from the sanctuary for David, for an inscription
of a title (or pillar ) when the Philistines held him in Geth.

<span id="an_55:2">55:2</span> Have mercy on me, O God, for man hath
trodden me under foot; all the day long he hath afflicted me fighting
against me.

<span id="an_55:3">55:3</span> My enemies have trodden on me all the day
long; for they are many that make war against me.

<span id="an_55:4">55:4</span> From the height of the day I shall fear:
but I will trust in thee.

<span id="an_55:5">55:5</span> In God I will praise my words, in God I
have put my trust: I will not fear what flesh can do against me.

<span id="an_55:6">55:6</span> All the day long they detested my words:
all their thoughts were against me unto evil.

<span id="an_55:7">55:7</span> They will dwell and hide themselves: they
will watch my heel. As they have waited for my soul,

<span id="an_55:8">55:8</span> for nothing shalt thou save them: in thy
anger thou shalt break the people in pieces, O God,

<span id="an_55:9">55:9</span> I have declared to thee my life: thou
hast set my tears in thy sight, As also in thy promise.

<span id="an_55:10">55:10</span> Then shall my enemies be turned back.
In what day soever I shall call upon thee, behold I know thou art my
God.

<span id="an_55:11">55:11</span> In God will I praise the word, in the
Lord will I praise his speech. In God have I hoped, I will not fear what
man can do to me.

<span id="an_55:12">55:12</span> In me, O God, are vows to thee, which I
will pay, praises to thee:

<span id="an_55:13">55:13</span> Because thou hast delivered my soul
from death, my feet from falling: that I may please in the sight of God,
in the light of the living.

<span id="an_56:1">56:1</span> Unto the end, destroy not, for David, for
an inscription of a title, when he fled from Saul into the cave

<span id="an_56:2">56:2</span> Have mercy on me, O God, have mercy on
me: for my soul trusteth in thee. And in the shadow of thy wings will I
hope, until iniquity pass away.

<span id="an_56:3">56:3</span> I will cry to God the most High; to God
who hath done good to me.

<span id="an_56:4">56:4</span> He hath sent from heaven and delivered
me: he hath made them a reproach that trod upon me. God hath sent his
mercy and his truth,

<span id="an_56:5">56:5</span> and he hath delivered my soul from the
midst of the young lions. I slept troubled. The sons of men, whose teeth
are weapons and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword.

<span id="an_56:6">56:6</span> Be thou exalted, O God, above the
heavens, and thy glory above all the earth.

<span id="an_56:7">56:7</span> They prepared a snare for my feet; and
they bowed down my soul. They dug a pit before my face, and they are
fallen into it.

<span id="an_56:8">56:8</span> My heart is ready, O God, my heart is
ready: I will Sing, and rehearse a psalm.

<span id="an_56:9">56:9</span> Arise, O my glory, arise psaltery and
harp: I will arise early.

<span id="an_56:10">56:10</span> I will give praise to thee, O Lord,
among the people: I will sing a psalm to thee among the nations.

<span id="an_56:11">56:11</span> For thy mercy is magnified even to the
heavens: and thy truth unto the clouds.

<span id="an_56:12">56:12</span> Be thou exalted, O God, above the l
heavens: and thy glory above all the earth.

<span id="an_57:1">57:1</span> Unto the end, destroy not, for David, for
an inscription of a title.

<span id="an_57:2">57:2</span> If in very deed you speak justice: judge
right things, ye sons of men.

<span id="an_57:3">57:3</span> For in your heart you work iniquity: your
hands forge injustice in the earth.

<span id="an_57:4">57:4</span> The wicked are alienated from the womb;
they have gone astray from the womb: they have spoken false things.

<span id="an_57:5">57:5</span> Their madness is according to the
likeness of a serpent: like the deaf asp that stoppeth her ears:

<span id="an_57:6">57:6</span> Which will not hear the voice of the
charmers; nor of the wizard that charmeth wisely.

<span id="an_57:7">57:7</span> God shall break in pieces their teeth in
their mouth: the Lord shall break the grinders of the lions.

<span id="an_57:8">57:8</span> They shall come to nothing, like water
running down; he hath bent his bow till they be weakened.

<span id="an_57:9">57:9</span> Like wax that melteth they shall be taken
away: fire hath fallen on them, and they shall not see the sun.

<span id="an_57:10">57:10</span> Before your thorns could know the
brier; he swalloweth them up, as alive, in his wrath.

<span id="an_57:11">57:11</span> The just shall rejoice when he shall
see the revenge: he shall wash his hands in the blood of the sinner.

<span id="an_57:12">57:12</span> And man shall say: If indeed there be
fruit to the just: there is indeed a God that judgeth them on the earth.

<span id="an_58:1">58:1</span> Unto the end, destroy not, for David for
an inscription of It title, when Saul sent and watched his house to kill
him.

<span id="an_58:2">58:2</span> Deliver me from my enemies, O my God; and
defend me from them that rise up against me.

<span id="an_58:3">58:3</span> Deliver me from them that work iniquity,
and save me from bloody men.

<span id="an_58:4">58:4</span> For behold they have caught my soul: the
mighty have rushed in upon me:

<span id="an_58:5">58:5</span> Neither is it my iniquity, nor my sin, O
Lord: without iniquity have I run, and directed my steps.

<span id="an_58:6">58:6</span> Rise up thou to meet me, and behold: even
thou, O Lord, the God of hosts, the God of Israel. Attend to visit all
the nations: have no mercy on all them that work iniquity.

<span id="an_58:7">58:7</span> They shall return at evening, and shall
suffer hunger like dogs: and shall go round about the city.

<span id="an_58:8">58:8</span> Behold they shall speak with their mouth,
and a sword is in their lips: for who, say they, hath heard us ?

<span id="an_58:9">58:9</span> But thou, O Lord, shalt laugh at them:
thou shalt bring all the nations to nothing.

<span id="an_58:10">58:10</span> I will keep my strength to thee: for
thou art my protector:

<span id="an_58:11">58:11</span> my God, his mercy shall prevent me.

<span id="an_58:12">58:12</span> God shall let me see over my enemies:
slay them not, lest at any time my people forget. Scatter them by thy
power; and bring them down, O Lord, my protector:

<span id="an_58:13">58:13</span> For the sin of their mouth, and the
word of their lips: and let them be taken in their pride. And for their
cursing and lying they shall be talked of,

<span id="an_58:14">58:14</span> when they are consumed: when they are
consumed by thy wrath, and they shall be no more. And they shall know
that God will rule Jacob, and all the ends of the earth.

<span id="an_58:15">58:15</span> They shall return at evening and shall
suffer hunger like dogs: and shall go round about the city.

<span id="an_58:16">58:16</span> They shall be scattered abroad to eat,
and shall murmur if they be not filled.

<span id="an_58:17">58:17</span> But I will sing thy strength: and will
extol thy mercy in the morning. For thou art become my support, and my
refuge, in the day of my trouble.

<span id="an_58:18">58:18</span> Unto thee, O my helper, will I sing,
for thou art God my defence: my God my mercy.

<span id="an_59:1">59:1</span> Unto the end, for them that shall be
changed, for the inscription of a title, to David himself, for doctrine,

<span id="an_59:2">59:2</span> when he set fire to Mesopotamia of Syria
and Sobal and Joab returned and slew of Edom, in the vale of the
saltpits, twelve thousand men.

<span id="an_59:3">59:3</span> O God, thou hast cast us off, and hast
destroyed us; thou hast been angry, and hast had mercy on us.

<span id="an_59:4">59:4</span> Thou hast moved the earth, and hast
troubled it: heal thou the breaches thereof, for it has been moved.

<span id="an_59:5">59:5</span> Thou hast shewn thy people hard things;
thou hast made us drink wine of sorrow.

<span id="an_59:6">59:6</span> Thou hast given a warning to them that
fear thee: that they may flee from before the bow: That thy beloved may
be delivered.

<span id="an_59:7">59:7</span> Save me with thy right hand, and hear me.

<span id="an_59:8">59:8</span> God hath spoken in his holy place: I will
rejoice, and I will divide Sichem; and will mete out the vale of
tabernacles.

<span id="an_59:9">59:9</span> Galaad is mine, and Manasses is mine: and
Ephraim is the strength of my head. Juda is my king:

<span id="an_59:10">59:10</span> Moab is the pot of my hope. Into Edom
will I stretch out my shoe: to me the foreigners are made subject.

<span id="an_59:11">59:11</span> Who will bring me into the strong city?
who will lead me into Edom?

<span id="an_59:12">59:12</span> Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us
off? and wilt not thou, O God, go out with our armies?

<span id="an_59:13">59:13</span> Give us help from trouble: for vain is
the salvation of man.

<span id="an_59:14">59:14</span> Through God we shall do mightily: and
he shall bring to nothing them that afflict us.

<span id="an_60:1">60:1</span> Unto the end, in hymns, for David.

<span id="an_60:2">60:2</span> Hear, O God, my supplication: be
attentive to my prayer,

<span id="an_60:3">60:3</span> To thee have I cried from the ends of the
earth: when my heart was in anguish, thou hast exalted me on a rock.
Thou hast conducted me;

<span id="an_60:4">60:4</span> for thou hast been my hope; a tower of
strength against the face of the enemy.

<span id="an_60:5">60:5</span> In thy tabernacle I shall dwell for ever:
I shall be protected under the covert of thy wings.

<span id="an_60:6">60:6</span> For thou, my God, hast heard my prayer:
thou hast given an inheritance to them that fear thy name.

<span id="an_60:7">60:7</span> Thou wilt add days to the days of the
king: his years even to generation and generation.

<span id="an_60:8">60:8</span> He abideth for ever in the sight of God:
his mercy and truth who shall search ?

<span id="an_60:9">60:9</span> So will I sing a psalm to thy name for
ever and ever: that I may pay my vows from day to day.

<span id="an_61:1">61:1</span> Unto the end, for Idithun, a psalm of
David.

<span id="an_61:2">61:2</span> Shall not my soul be subject to God? for
from him is my salvation.

<span id="an_61:3">61:3</span> For he is my God and my saviour: he is my
protector, I shall be moved no more.

<span id="an_61:4">61:4</span> How long do you rush in upon a man? you
all kill, as if you were thrusting down a leaning wall, and a tottering
fence.

<span id="an_61:5">61:5</span> But they have thought to cast away my
price; I ran in thirst: they blessed with their mouth, but cursed with
their heart.

<span id="an_61:6">61:6</span> But be thou, O my soul, subject to God:
for from him is my patience.

<span id="an_61:7">61:7</span> For he is my God and my saviour: he is my
helper, I shall not be moved.

<span id="an_61:8">61:8</span> In God is my salvation and my glory: he
is the God of my help, and my hope is in God.

<span id="an_61:9">61:9</span> Trust in him, all ye congregation of
people: pour out your hearts before him. God is our helper for ever.

<span id="an_61:10">61:10</span> But vain are the sons of men, the sons
of men are liars in the balances: that by vanity they may together
deceive.

<span id="an_61:11">61:11</span> Trust not in iniquity, and cover not
robberies: if riches abound, set not your heart upon them.

<span id="an_61:12">61:12</span> God hath spoken once, these two things
have I heard, that power belongeth to God,

<span id="an_61:13">61:13</span> and mercy to thee, O Lord; for thou
wilt render to every man according to his works.

<span id="an_62:1">62:1</span> A psalm of David when he was in the
desert of Edom.

<span id="an_62:2">62:2</span> O God, my God, to thee do I watch at
break of day. For thee my soul hath thirsted; for thee my flesh, O how
many ways!

<span id="an_62:3">62:3</span> In a desert land, and where there is no
way, and no water: so in the sanctuary have I come before thee, to see
thy power and thy glory.

<span id="an_62:4">62:4</span> For thy mercy is better than lives: thee
my lips shall praise.

<span id="an_62:5">62:5</span> Thus will I bless thee all my life long:
and in thy name I will lift up my hands.

<span id="an_62:6">62:6</span> Let my soul be filled as with marrow and
fatness: and my mouth shall praise thee with joyful lips.

<span id="an_62:7">62:7</span> If I have remembered thee upon my bed, I
will meditate on thee in the morning:

<span id="an_62:8">62:8</span> because thou hast been my helper. And I
will rejoice under the covert of thy wings:

<span id="an_62:9">62:9</span> my soul hath stuck close to thee: thy
right hand hath received me.

<span id="an_62:10">62:10</span> But they have sought my soul in vain,
they shall go into the lower parts of the earth:

<span id="an_62:11">62:11</span> They shall be delivered into the hands
of the sword, they shall be the portions of foxes.

<span id="an_62:12">62:12</span> But the king shall rejoice in God, all
they shall be praised that swear by him: because the mouth is stopped of
them that speak wicked things.

<span id="an_63:1">63:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David.

<span id="an_63:2">63:2</span> Hear, O God, my prayer, when I make
supplication to thee : deliver my soul from the fear of the enemy.

<span id="an_63:3">63:3</span> Thou hast protected me from the assembly
of the malignant; from the multitude of the workers of iniquity.

<span id="an_63:4">63:4</span> For they have whetted their tongues like
a sword; they have bent their bow a bitter thing,

<span id="an_63:5">63:5</span> to shoot in secret the undefiled.

<span id="an_63:6">63:6</span> They will shoot at him on a sudden, and
will not fear: they are resolute in wickedness. They have talked of
hiding snares; they have said: Who shall see them?

<span id="an_63:7">63:7</span> They have searched after iniquities: they
have failed in their search. Man shall come to a deep heart:

<span id="an_63:8">63:8</span> and God shall be exalted. The arrows of
children are their wounds:

<span id="an_63:9">63:9</span> and their tongues against them are made
weak. All that saw them were troubled;

<span id="an_63:10">63:10</span> and every man was afraid. And they
declared the works of God: and understood his doings.

<span id="an_63:11">63:11</span> The just shall rejoice in the Lord, and
shall hope in him: and all the upright in heart shall be praised.

<span id="an_64:1">64:1</span> To the end, a psalm of David. The
canticle of Jeremias and Ezechiel to the people of the captivity, when
they began to go out.

<span id="an_64:2">64:2</span> A Hymn, O God, becometh thee in Sion: and
a vow shall be paid to thee in Jerusalem.

<span id="an_64:3">64:3</span> O hear my prayer: all flesh shall come to
thee.

<span id="an_64:4">64:4</span> The words of the wicked have prevailed
over us: and thou wilt pardon our transgressions.

<span id="an_64:5">64:5</span> Blessed is he whom thou hast chosen and
taken to thee: he shall dwell in thy courts. We shall be filled with the
good things of thy house; holy is thy temple,

<span id="an_64:6">64:6</span> wonderful in justice. Hear us, O God our
saviour, who art the hope of all the ends of the earth, and in the sea
afar off.

<span id="an_64:7">64:7</span> Thou who preparest the mountains by thy
strength, being girded with power:

<span id="an_64:8">64:8</span> who troublest the depth of the sea, the
noise of its waves. The Gentiles shall be troubled,

<span id="an_64:9">64:9</span> and they that dwell in the uttermost
borders shall be afraid at thy signs: thou shalt make the outgoings of
the morning and of the evening to be joyful.

<span id="an_64:10">64:10</span> Thou hast visited the earth, and hast
plentifully watered it; thou hast many ways enriched it. The river of
God is filled with water, thou hast prepared their food: for so is its
preparation.

<span id="an_64:11">64:11</span> Fill up plentifully the streams
thereof, multiply its fruits; it shall spring up and rejoice in its
showers.

<span id="an_64:12">64:12</span> Thou shalt bless the crown of the year
of thy goodness: and thy fields shall be filled with plenty.

<span id="an_64:13">64:13</span> The beautiful places of the wilderness
shall grow fat: and the hills shall be girded about with joy,

<span id="an_64:14">64:14</span> The rams of the flock are clothed, and
the vales shall abound with corn: they shall shout, yea they shall sing
a hymn.

<span id="an_65:1">65:1</span> Unto the end, a canticle of a psalm of
the resurrection. Shout with joy to God, all the earth,

<span id="an_65:2">65:2</span> sing ye a psalm to his name; give glory
to his praise.

<span id="an_65:3">65:3</span> Say unto God, How terrible are thy works,
O Lord! in the multitude of thy strength thy enemies shall lie to thee.

<span id="an_65:4">65:4</span> Let all the earth adore thee, and sing to
thee: let it sing a psalm to thy name.

<span id="an_65:5">65:5</span> Come and see the works of God; who is
terrible in his counsels over the sons of men.

<span id="an_65:6">65:6</span> Who turneth the sea into dry land, in the
river they shall pass on foot: there shall we rejoice in him.

<span id="an_65:7">65:7</span> Who by his power ruleth for ever: his
eyes behold the nations; let not them that provoke him he exalted in
themselves.

<span id="an_65:8">65:8</span> O bless our God, ye Gentiles: and make
the voice of his praise to be heard.

<span id="an_65:9">65:9</span> Who hath set my soul to live: and hath
not suffered my feet to be moved:

<span id="an_65:10">65:10</span> For thou, O God, hast proved us: thou
hast tried us by fire, as silver is tried.

<span id="an_65:11">65:11</span> Thou hast brought us into a net, thou
hast laid afflictions on our back:

<span id="an_65:12">65:12</span> thou hast set men over our heads. We
have passed through tire and water, and thou hast brought us out into a
refreshment.

<span id="an_65:13">65:13</span> I will go into thy house with burnt
offerings: I will pay thee my vows,

<span id="an_65:14">65:14</span> which my lips have uttered, And my
mouth hath spoken, when I was in trouble.

<span id="an_65:15">65:15</span> I will offer up to thee holocausts full
of marrow, with burnt offerings of rams: I will offer to thee bullocks
with goats.

<span id="an_65:16">65:16</span> Come and hear, all ye that fear God,
and I will tell you what great things he hath done for my soul.

<span id="an_65:17">65:17</span> I cried to him with my mouth: and I
extolled him with my tongue.

<span id="an_65:18">65:18</span> If I have looked at iniquity in my
heart, the Lord will not hear me.

<span id="an_65:19">65:19</span> Therefore hath God heard me, and hath
attended to the voice of my supplication.

<span id="an_65:20">65:20</span> Blessed be God, who hath not turned
away my prayer, nor his mercy from me.

<span id="an_66:1">66:1</span> Unto the end, in, hymns, a psalm of a
canticle for David.

<span id="an_66:2">66:2</span> May God have mercy on us, and bless us:
may he cause the light of his countenance to shine upon us, and may he
have mercy on us.

<span id="an_66:3">66:3</span> That we may know thy way upon earth: thy
salvation in all nations.

<span id="an_66:4">66:4</span> Let people confess to thee, O God: let
all people give praise to thee.

<span id="an_66:5">66:5</span> Let the nations be glad and rejoice: for
thou judgest the people with justice, and directest the nations upon
earth.

<span id="an_66:6">66:6</span> Let the people, O God, confess to thee:
let all the people give praise to thee:

<span id="an_66:7">66:7</span> the earth hath yielded her fruit. May
God, our God bless us,

<span id="an_66:8">66:8</span> may God bless us: and all the ends of the
earth fear him.

<span id="an_67:1">67:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm of a canticle for
David himself.

<span id="an_67:2">67:2</span> Let God arise, and let his enemies be
scattered: and let them that hate him flee from before his face.

<span id="an_67:3">67:3</span> As smoke vanisheth, so let them vanish
away: as wax melteth before the fire, so let the wicked perish at the
presence of God.

<span id="an_67:4">67:4</span> And let the just feast, and rejoice
before God: and be delighted with gladness.

<span id="an_67:5">67:5</span> Sing ye to God, sing a psalm to his name,
make a way for him who ascendeth upon the west: the Lord is his name.
Rejoice ye before him: but the wicked shall be troubled at his presence,

<span id="an_67:6">67:6</span> who is the father of orphans, and the
judge of widows. God in his holy place:

<span id="an_67:7">67:7</span> God who maketh men of one manner to dwell
in a house: Who bringeth out them that were bound in strength; in like
manner them that provoke, that dwell in sepulchres.

<span id="an_67:8">67:8</span> O God, when thou didst go forth in the
sight of thy people, when thou didst pass through the desert:

<span id="an_67:9">67:9</span> The earth was moved, and the heavens
dropped at the presence of the God of Sina, at the presence of the God
of Israel.

<span id="an_67:10">67:10</span> Thou shalt set aside for thy
inheritance a free rain, O God: and it was weakened, but thou hast made
it perfect.

<span id="an_67:11">67:11</span> In it shall thy animals dwell; in thy
sweetness, O God, thou hast provided for the poor.

<span id="an_67:12">67:12</span> The Lord shall give the word to them
that preach good tidings with great power.

<span id="an_67:13">67:13</span> The king of powers is of the beloved,
of the beloved; and the beauty of the house shall divide spoils.

<span id="an_67:14">67:14</span> If you sleep among the midst of lots,
you shall be as the wings of a dove covered with silver, and the hinder
parts of her back with the paleness of gold.

<span id="an_67:15">67:15</span> When he that is in heaven appointeth
kings over her, they shall be whited with snow in Selmon.

<span id="an_67:16">67:16</span> The mountain of God is a fat mountain.
A curdled mountain, a fat mountain.

<span id="an_67:17">67:17</span> Why suspect, ye curdled mountains? A
mountain in which God is well pleased to dwell: for there the Lord shall
dwell unto the end.

<span id="an_67:18">67:18</span> The chariot of God is attended by ten
thousands; thousands of them that rejoice: the Lord is among them in
Sina, in the holy place.

<span id="an_67:19">67:19</span> Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast
led captivity captive; thou hast received gifts in men. Yea for those
also that do not believe, the dwelling of the Lord God.

<span id="an_67:20">67:20</span> Blessed be the Lord day by day: the God
of our salvation will make our journey prosperous to us.

<span id="an_67:21">67:21</span> Our God is the God of salvation: and of
the Lord, of the Lord are the issues from death.

<span id="an_67:22">67:22</span> But God shall break the heads of his
enemies: the hairy crown of them that walk on in their sins.

<span id="an_67:23">67:23</span> The Lord said: I will turn them from
Basan, I will turn them into the depth of the sea:

<span id="an_67:24">67:24</span> That thy foot may be dipped in the
blood of thy enemies; the tongue of thy dogs be red with the same.

<span id="an_67:25">67:25</span> They have seen thy goings, O God, the
goings of my God: of my king who is in his sanctuary.

<span id="an_67:26">67:26</span> Princes went before joined with
singers, in the midst of young damsels playing on timbrels.

<span id="an_67:27">67:27</span> In the churches bless ye God the Lord,
from the fountains of Israel.

<span id="an_67:28">67:28</span> There is Benjamin a youth, in ecstasy
of mind. The princes of Juda are their leaders: the princes of Zabulon,
the princes of Nephthali.

<span id="an_67:29">67:29</span> Command thy strength, O God: confirm, O
God, what thou hast wrought in us.

<span id="an_67:30">67:30</span> From thy temple in Jerusalem, kings
shall offer presents to thee.

<span id="an_67:31">67:31</span> Rebuke the wild beasts of the reeds,
the congregation of bulls with the kine of the people; who seek to
exclude them who are tried with silver. Scatter thou the nations that
delight in wars:

<span id="an_67:32">67:32</span> ambassadors shall come out of Egypt:
Ethiopia shall soon stretch out her hands to God.

<span id="an_67:33">67:33</span> Sing to God, ye kingdoms of the earth:
sing ye to the Lord: Sing ye to God,

<span id="an_67:34">67:34</span> who mounteth above the heaven of
heavens, to the east. Behold he will give to his voice the voice of
power:

<span id="an_67:35">67:35</span> give ye glory to God for Israel, his
magnificence, and his power is in the clouds.

<span id="an_67:36">67:36</span> God is wonderful in his saints: the God
of Israel is he who will give power and strength to his people. Blessed
be God.

<span id="an_68:1">68:1</span> Unto the end, for them that shall be
changed; for David.

<span id="an_68:2">68:2</span> Save me, O God: for the waters are come
in even unto my soul.

<span id="an_68:3">68:3</span> I stick fast in the mire of the deep: and
there is no sure standing. I am come into the depth of the sea: and a
tempest hath overwhelmed me.

<span id="an_68:4">68:4</span> I have laboured with crying; my jaws are
become hoarse: my eyes have failed, whilst I hope in my God.

<span id="an_68:5">68:5</span> They are multiplied above the hairs of my
head, who hate me without cause. My enemies are grown strong who have
wrongfully persecuted me: then did I pay that which I took not away.

<span id="an_68:6">68:6</span> O God, thou knowest my foolishness; and
my offences are not hidden from thee:

<span id="an_68:7">68:7</span> Let not them be ashamed for me, who look
for thee, O Lord, the Lord of hosts. Let them not be confounded on my
account, who seek thee, O God of Israel.

<span id="an_68:8">68:8</span> Because for thy sake I have borne
reproach; shame hath covered my face.

<span id="an_68:9">68:9</span> I am become a stranger to my brethren,
and an alien to the sons of my mother.

<span id="an_68:10">68:10</span> For the zeal of thy house hath eaten me
up: and the reproaches of them that reproached thee are fallen upon me.

<span id="an_68:11">68:11</span> And I covered my soul in fasting: and
it was made a reproach to me.

<span id="an_68:12">68:12</span> And I made haircloth my garment: and I
became a byword to them.

<span id="an_68:13">68:13</span> They that sat in the gate spoke against
me: and they that drank wine made me their song.

<span id="an_68:14">68:14</span> But as for me, my prayer is to thee, O
Lord; for the time of thy good pleasure, O God. In the multitude of thy
mercy hear me, in the truth of thy salvation.

<span id="an_68:15">68:15</span> Draw me out of the mire, that I may not
stick fast: deliver me from them that hate me, and out of the deep
waters.

<span id="an_68:16">68:16</span> Let not the tempest of water drown me,
nor the deep swallow me up: and let not the pit shut her mouth upon me.

<span id="an_68:17">68:17</span> Hear me, O Lord, for thy mercy is kind;
look upon me according to the multitude of thy tender mercies.

<span id="an_68:18">68:18</span> And turn not away thy face from thy
servant: for I am in trouble, hear me speedily.

<span id="an_68:19">68:19</span> Attend to my soul, and deliver it: save
me because of my enemies.

<span id="an_68:20">68:20</span> Thou knowest my reproach, and my
confusion, and my shame.

<span id="an_68:21">68:21</span> In thy sight are all they that afflict
me; my heart hath expected reproach and misery. And I looked for one
that would grieve together with me, but there was none: and for one that
would comfort me, and I found none.

<span id="an_68:22">68:22</span> And they gave me gall for my food, and
in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.

<span id="an_68:23">68:23</span> Let their table become as a snare
before them, and a recompense, and a stumblingblock.

<span id="an_68:24">68:24</span> Let their eyes be darkened that they
see not; and their back bend thou down always.

<span id="an_68:25">68:25</span> Pour out thy indignation upon them: and
let thy wrathful anger take hold of them.

<span id="an_68:26">68:26</span> Let their habitation be made desolate:
and let there be none to dwell in their tabernacles.

<span id="an_68:27">68:27</span> Because they have persecuted him whom
thou hast smitten; and they have added to the grief of my wounds.

<span id="an_68:28">68:28</span> Add thou iniquity upon their iniquity:
and let them not come into thy justice.

<span id="an_68:29">68:29</span> Let them be blotted out of the book of
the living; and with the just let them not be written.

<span id="an_68:30">68:30</span> But I am poor and sorrowful: thy
salvation, O God, hath set me up.

<span id="an_68:31">68:31</span> I will praise the name of God with a
canticle: and I will magnify him with praise.

<span id="an_68:32">68:32</span> And it shall please God better than a
young calf, that bringeth forth horns and hoofs.

<span id="an_68:33">68:33</span> Let the poor see and rejoice: seek ye
God, and your soul shall live.

<span id="an_68:34">68:34</span> For the Lord hath heard the poor: and
hath not despised his prisoners.

<span id="an_68:35">68:35</span> Let the heavens and the earth praise
him; the sea, and every thing that creepeth therein.

<span id="an_68:36">68:36</span> For God will save Sion, and the cities
of Juda shall be built up. And they shall dwell there, and acquire it by
inheritance.

<span id="an_68:37">68:37</span> And the seed of his servants shall
possess it; and they that love his name shall dwell therein.

<span id="an_69:1">69:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David, to bring
to remembrance that the Lord saved him.

<span id="an_69:2">69:2</span> O God, come to my assistance; O Lord,
make haste to help me.

<span id="an_69:3">69:3</span> Let them be confounded and ashamed that
seek my soul:

<span id="an_69:4">69:4</span> Let them be turned backward, and blush
for shame that desire evils to me: Let them be presently turned away
blushing for shame that say to me: 'T is well, 't is well.

<span id="an_69:5">69:5</span> Let all that seek thee rejoice and be
glad in thee; and let such as love thy salvation say always: The Lord be
magnified.

<span id="an_69:6">69:6</span> But I am needy and poor; O God, help me.
Thou art my helper and my deliverer: O Lord, make no delay.

<span id="an_70:1">70:1</span> A psalm for David. Of the sons of
Jonadab, and the former captives. In thee, O Lord, I have hoped, let me
never be put to confusion:

<span id="an_70:2">70:2</span> deliver me in thy justice, and rescue me.
Incline thy ear unto me, and save me.

<span id="an_70:3">70:3</span> Be thou unto me a God, a protector, and a
place of strength: that thou mayst make me safe. For thou art my
firmament and my refuge.

<span id="an_70:4">70:4</span> Deliver me, O my God, out of the hand of
the sinner, and out of the hand of the transgressor of the law and of
the unjust.

<span id="an_70:5">70:5</span> For thou art my patience, O Lord: my
hope, O Lord, from my youth;

<span id="an_70:6">70:6</span> By thee have I been confirmed from the
womb: from my mother's womb thou art my protector. Of thee shall I
continually sing:

<span id="an_70:7">70:7</span> I run become unto many as a wonder, but
thou art a strong helper.

<span id="an_70:8">70:8</span> Let my mouth be filled with praise, that
I may sing thy glory; thy greatness all the day long.

<span id="an_70:9">70:9</span> Cast me not off in the time of old age:
when my strength shall fail, do not thou forsake me.

<span id="an_70:10">70:10</span> For my enemies have spoken against me;
and they that watched my soul have consulted together,

<span id="an_70:11">70:11</span> Saying: God hath forsaken him: pursue
and take him, for there is none to deliver him.

<span id="an_70:12">70:12</span> O God, be not thou far from me: O my
God, make haste to my help.

<span id="an_70:13">70:13</span> Let them be confounded and come to
nothing that detract my soul; let them be covered with confusion and
shame that seek my hurt.

<span id="an_70:14">70:14</span> But I will always hope; and will add to
all thy praise.

<span id="an_70:15">70:15</span> My mouth shall shew forth thy justice;
thy salvation all the day long. Because I have not knows learning,

<span id="an_70:16">70:16</span> I will enter into the powers of the
Lord: O Lord, I will be mindful of thy justice alone.

<span id="an_70:17">70:17</span> Thou hast taught me, O God, from my
youth: and till now I will declare thy wonderful works.

<span id="an_70:18">70:18</span> And unto old age and grey hairs: O God,
forsake me not, Until I shew forth thy arm to all the generation that is
to come: Thy power,

<span id="an_70:19">70:19</span> and thy justice, O God, even to the
highest great things thou hast done: O God, who is like to thee?

<span id="an_70:20">70:20</span> How great troubles hast thou shewn me,
many and grievous: and turning thou hast brought me to life, and hast
brought me back again from the depths of the earth :

<span id="an_70:21">70:21</span> Thou hast multiplied thy magnificence;
and turning to me thou hast comforted me.

<span id="an_70:22">70:22</span> For I will also confess to thee thy
truth with the instruments of psaltery: O God, I will sing to thee with
the harp, thou holy one of Israel.

<span id="an_70:23">70:23</span> My lips shall greatly rejoice, when I
shall sing to thee; and my soul which thou hast redeemed.

<span id="an_70:24">70:24</span> Yea and my tongue shall meditate on thy
justice all the day; when they shall be confounded and put to shame that
seek evils to me.

<span id="an_71:1">71:1</span> A psalm on Solomon.

<span id="an_71:2">71:2</span> Give to the king thy judgment, O God: and
to the king's son thy justice: To judge thy people with justice, and thy
poor with judgment.

<span id="an_71:3">71:3</span> Let the mountains receive peace for the
people: and the hills justice.

<span id="an_71:4">71:4</span> He shall judge the poor of the people,
and he shall save the children of the poor: and he shall humble the
oppressor.

<span id="an_71:5">71:5</span> And he shall continue with the sun, and
before the moon, throughout all generations.

<span id="an_71:6">71:6</span> He shall come down like rain upon the
fleece; and as showers falling gently upon the earth.

<span id="an_71:7">71:7</span> In his days shall justice spring up, and
abundance of peace, till the moon be taken sway.

<span id="an_71:8">71:8</span> And he shall rule from sea to sea, and
from the river unto the ends of the earth.

<span id="an_71:9">71:9</span> Before him the Ethiopians shall fall
down: and his enemies shall lick the ground.

<span id="an_71:10">71:10</span> The kings of Tharsis and the islands
shall offer presents: the kings of the Arabians and of Saba shall bring
gifts:

<span id="an_71:11">71:11</span> And all kings of the earth shall adore
him: all nations shall serve him.

<span id="an_71:12">71:12</span> For he shall deliver the poor from the
mighty: and the needy that had no helper.

<span id="an_71:13">71:13</span> He shall spare the poor and needy: and
he shall save the souls of the poor.

<span id="an_71:14">71:14</span> He shall redeem their souls from
usuries and iniquity: and their names shall be honourable in his sight.

<span id="an_71:15">71:15</span> And he shall live, and to him shall be
given of the gold of Arabia, for him they shall always adore: they shall
bless him all the day.

<span id="an_71:16">71:16</span> And there shall be a firmament on the
earth on the tops of mountains, above Libanus shall the fruit thereof be
exalted : and they of the city shall flourish like the grass of the
earth.

<span id="an_71:17">71:17</span> Let his name be blessed for evermore :
his name continueth before the sun. And in him shall all the tribes of
the earth be blessed: all nations shall magnify him.

<span id="an_71:18">71:18</span> Blessed be the Lord, the God of Israel,
who alone doth wonderful things.

<span id="an_71:19">71:19</span> And blessed be the name of his majesty
for ever: and the whole earth shall be filled with his majesty. So be
it. So be it.

<span id="an_71:20">71:20</span> The praises of David, the son of Jesse,
are ended.

<span id="an_72:1">72:1</span> A psalm for Asaph. How good is God to
Israel, to them that are of a right heart!

<span id="an_72:2">72:2</span> But my feet were almost moved; my steps
had well nigh slipped.

<span id="an_72:3">72:3</span> Because I had a zeal on occasion of the
wicked, seeing the prosperity of sinners.

<span id="an_72:4">72:4</span> For there is no regard to their death,
nor is there strength in their stripes.

<span id="an_72:5">72:5</span> They are not in the labour of men:
neither shall they be scourged like other men.

<span id="an_72:6">72:6</span> Therefore pride hath held them fast: they
are covered with their iniquity and their wickedness.

<span id="an_72:7">72:7</span> Their iniquity hath come forth, as it
were from fatness: they have passed into the affection of the heart.

<span id="an_72:8">72:8</span> They have thought and spoken wickedness:
they have spoken iniquity on high.

<span id="an_72:9">72:9</span> They have set their mouth against heaven:
and their tongue hath passed through the earth.

<span id="an_72:10">72:10</span> Therefore will my people return here
and full days shall be found in them.

<span id="an_72:11">72:11</span> And they said: How doth God know? and
is there knowledge in the most High?

<span id="an_72:12">72:12</span> Behold these are sinners; and yet
abounding in the world they have obtained riches.

<span id="an_72:13">72:13</span> And I said: Then have I in vain
justified my heart, and washed my hands among the innocent.

<span id="an_72:14">72:14</span> And I have been scourged all the day;
and my chastisement hath been in the mornings.

<span id="an_72:15">72:15</span> If I said: I will speak thus; behold I
should condemn the generation of thy children.

<span id="an_72:16">72:16</span> I studied that I might know this thing,
it is a labour in my sight:

<span id="an_72:17">72:17</span> Until I go into the sanctuary of God,
and understand concerning their last ends.

<span id="an_72:18">72:18</span> But indeed for deceits thou hast put it
to them: when they were lifted up thou hast cast them down.

<span id="an_72:19">72:19</span> How are they brought to desolation?
they have suddenly ceased to be: they have perished by reason of their
iniquity.

<span id="an_72:20">72:20</span> As the dream of them that awake, O
Lord; so in thy city thou shalt bring their image to nothing.

<span id="an_72:21">72:21</span> For my heart hath been inflamed, and my
reins have been changed:

<span id="an_72:22">72:22</span> and I am brought to nothing, and I knew
not.

<span id="an_72:23">72:23</span> I am become as a beast before thee: and
I am always with thee.

<span id="an_72:24">72:24</span> Thou hast held me by my right hand; and
by thy will thou hast conducted me, and with thy glory thou hast
received me.

<span id="an_72:25">72:25</span> For what have I in heaven? and besides
thee what do I desire upon earth?

<span id="an_72:26">72:26</span> For thee my flesh and my heart hath
fainted away: thou art the God of my heart, and the God that is my
portion for ever.

<span id="an_72:27">72:27</span> For behold they that go far from thee
shall perish: thou hast destroyed all them that are disloyal to thee.

<span id="an_72:28">72:28</span> But it is good for me to adhere to my
God, to put my hope in the Lord God: That I may declare all thy praises,
in the gates of the daughter of Sion.

<span id="an_73:1">73:1</span> Understanding for Asaph. O God, why hast
thou cast us off unto the end: why is thy wrath enkindled against the
sheep of thy pasture?

<span id="an_73:2">73:2</span> Remember thy congregation, which thou
hast possessed from the beginning. The sceptre of thy inheritance which
thou hast redeemed: mount Sion in which thou hast dwelt.

<span id="an_73:3">73:3</span> Lift up thy hands against their pride
unto the end; see what things the enemy hath done wickedly in the
sanctuary.

<span id="an_73:4">73:4</span> And they that hate thee have made their
boasts, in the midst of thy solemnity. They have set up their ensigns
for signs,

<span id="an_73:5">73:5</span> and they knew not both in the going out
and on the highest top. As with axes in a wood of trees,

<span id="an_73:6">73:6</span> they have cut down at once the gates
thereof, with axe and hatchet they have brought it down.

<span id="an_73:7">73:7</span> They have set fire to thy sanctuary: they
have defiled the dwelling place of thy name on the earth.

<span id="an_73:8">73:8</span> They said in their heart, the whole
kindred of them together: Let us abolish all the festival days of God
from the land.

<span id="an_73:9">73:9</span> Our signs we have not seen, there is now
no prophet: and he will know us no more.

<span id="an_73:10">73:10</span> How long, O God, shall the enemy
reproach: is the adversary to provoke thy name for ever?

<span id="an_73:11">73:11</span> Why dost thou turn away thy hand: and
thy right hand out of the midst of thy bosom for ever ?

<span id="an_73:12">73:12</span> But God is our king before ages: he
hath wrought salvation in the midst of the earth.

<span id="an_73:13">73:13</span> Thou by thy strength didst make the sea
firm: thou didst crush the heads of the dragons in the waters.

<span id="an_73:14">73:14</span> Thou hast broken the heads of the
dragon: thou hast given him to be meat for the people of the Ethiopians.

<span id="an_73:15">73:15</span> Thou hast broken up the fountains and
the torrents: thou hast dried up the Ethan rivers.

<span id="an_73:16">73:16</span> Thine is the day, and thine is the
night: thou hast made the morning light and the sun.

<span id="an_73:17">73:17</span> Thou hast made all the borders of the
earth: the summer and the spring were formed by thee.

<span id="an_73:18">73:18</span> Remember this, the enemy hath
reproached the Lord: and a foolish people hath provoked thy name.

<span id="an_73:19">73:19</span> Deliver not up to beasts the souls that
confess to thee: and forget not to the end the souls of thy poor.

<span id="an_73:20">73:20</span> Have regard to thy covenant: for they
that are the obscure of the earth have been filled with dwellings of
iniquity.

<span id="an_73:21">73:21</span> Let not the humble be turned away with
confusion: the poor and needy shall praise thy name.

<span id="an_73:22">73:22</span> Arise, O God, judge thy own cause:
remember thy reproaches with which the foolish man hath reproached thee
all the day.

<span id="an_73:23">73:23</span> Forget not the voices of thy enemies:
the pride of them that hate thee ascendeth continually.

<span id="an_74:1">74:1</span> Unto the end, corrupt not, a psalm of a
canticle for Asaph.

<span id="an_74:2">74:2</span> We will praise thee, O God: we will
praise, and we will call upon thy name. We will relate thy wondrous
works:

<span id="an_74:3">74:3</span> when I shall take a time, I will judge
justices.

<span id="an_74:4">74:4</span> The earth is melted, and all that dwell
therein: I have established the pillars thereof.

<span id="an_74:5">74:5</span> I said to the wicked: Do not act
wickedly: and to the sinners: Lift not up the horn.

<span id="an_74:6">74:6</span> Lift not up your horn on high: speak not
iniquity against God.

<span id="an_74:7">74:7</span> For neither from the east, nor from the
west, nor from the desert hills:

<span id="an_74:8">74:8</span> for God is the judge. One he putteth
down, and another he lifteth up:

<span id="an_74:9">74:9</span> for in the hand of the Lord there is a
cup of strong wine full of mixture. And he hath poured it out from this
to that: but the dregs thereof are not emptied: all the sinners of the
earth shall drink.

<span id="an_74:10">74:10</span> But I will declare for ever: I will
sing to the God of Jacob.

<span id="an_74:11">74:11</span> And I will break all the horns of
sinners: but the horns of the just shall be exalted.

<span id="an_75:1">75:1</span> Unto the end, in praises, a psalm for
Asaph: a canticle to the Assyrians.

<span id="an_75:2">75:2</span> In Judea God is known: his name is great
in Israel.

<span id="an_75:3">75:3</span> And his place is in peace: and his abode
in Sion:

<span id="an_75:4">75:4</span> There hath he broken the powers of bows,
the shield, the sword, and the battie.

<span id="an_75:5">75:5</span> Thou enlightenest wonderfully from the
everlasting hills.

<span id="an_75:6">75:6</span> All the foolish of heart were troubled.
They have slept their sleep; and all the men of riches have found
nothing in their hands.

<span id="an_75:7">75:7</span> At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, they have
all slumbered that mounted on horseback.

<span id="an_75:8">75:8</span> Thou art terrible, and who shall resist
thee? from that time thy wrath.

<span id="an_75:9">75:9</span> Thou hast caused judgment to be heard
from heaven: the earth trembled and was still,

<span id="an_75:10">75:10</span> When God arose in judgment, to save all
the meek of the earth.

<span id="an_75:11">75:11</span> For the thought of man shall give
praise to thee: and the remainders of the thought shall keep holiday to
thee.

<span id="an_75:12">75:12</span> Vow ye, and pay to the Lord your God:
all you that are round about him bring presents. To him that is
terrible,

<span id="an_75:13">75:13</span> even to him who taketh away the spirit
of princes: to the terrible with the kings of the earth.

<span id="an_76:1">76:1</span> Unto the end, for Idithun, a psalm of
Asaph.

<span id="an_76:2">76:2</span> I cried to the Lord with my voice; to God
with my voice, and he gave ear to me.

<span id="an_76:3">76:3</span> In the day of my trouble I sought God,
with my hands lifted up to him in the night, and I was not deceived. My
soul refused to be comforted:

<span id="an_76:4">76:4</span> I remembered God, and was delighted, and
was exercised, and my spirit swooned away.

<span id="an_76:5">76:5</span> My eyes prevented the watches: I was
troubled, and I spoke not.

<span id="an_76:6">76:6</span> I thought upon the days of old: and I had
in my mind the eternal years.

<span id="an_76:7">76:7</span> And I meditated in the night with my own
heart: and I was exercised and I swept my spirit.

<span id="an_76:8">76:8</span> Will God then cast off for ever? or will
he never be more favourable again?

<span id="an_76:9">76:9</span> Or will he cut off his mercy for ever,
from generation to generation?

<span id="an_76:10">76:10</span> Or will God forget to shew mercy? or
will he in his anger shut up his mercies?

<span id="an_76:11">76:11</span> And I said, Now have I begun: this is
the change of the right hand of the most High.

<span id="an_76:12">76:12</span> I remembered the works of the Lord: for
I will be mindful of thy wonders from the beginning.

<span id="an_76:13">76:13</span> And I will meditate on all thy works:
and will be employed in thy inventions.

<span id="an_76:14">76:14</span> Thy way, O God, is in the holy place:
who is the great God like our God?

<span id="an_76:15">76:15</span> Thou art the God that dost wonders.
Thou hast made thy power known among the nations:

<span id="an_76:16">76:16</span> with thy arm thou hast redeemed thy
people the children of Jacob and of Joseph.

<span id="an_76:17">76:17</span> The waters saw thee, O God, the waters
saw thee: and they were afraid, and the depths were troubled.

<span id="an_76:18">76:18</span> Great was the noise of the waters: the
clouds sent out a sound. For thy arrows pass:

<span id="an_76:19">76:19</span> the voice of thy thunder in a wheel.
Thy lightnings enlightened the world: the earth shook and trembled.

<span id="an_76:20">76:20</span> Thy way is in the sea, and thy paths in
many waters: and thy footsteps shall not be known.

<span id="an_76:21">76:21</span> Thou hast conducted thy people like
sheep, by the hand of Moses and Aaron

<span id="an_77:1">77:1</span> Understanding for Asaph. Attend, O my
people, to my law: incline your ears to the words of my mouth.

<span id="an_77:2">77:2</span> I will open my mouth in parables: I will
utter propositions from the beginning.

<span id="an_77:3">77:3</span> How great things have we heard and known,
and our fathers have told us.

<span id="an_77:4">77:4</span> They have not been hidden from their
children, in another generation. Declaring the praises of the Lord, and
