his powers, and his wonders which he hath done.

<span id="an_77:5">77:5</span> And he set up a testimony in Jacob: and
made a law in Israel. How great things he commanded our fathers, that
they should make the same known to their children:

<span id="an_77:6">77:6</span> that another generation might know them.
The children that should be born and should rise up, and declare them to
their children.

<span id="an_77:7">77:7</span> That they may put their hope in God and
may not forget the works of God: and may seek his commandments.

<span id="an_77:8">77:8</span> That they may not become like their
fathers, a perverse end exasperating generation. A generation that set
not their heart aright: and whose spirit was not faithful to God.

<span id="an_77:9">77:9</span> The sons of Ephraim who bend and shoot
with the bow: they have turned back in the day of battle.

<span id="an_77:10">77:10</span> They kept not the covenant of God: and
in his law they would not walk.

<span id="an_77:11">77:11</span> And they forgot his benefits, and his
wonders that he had shewn them.

<span id="an_77:12">77:12</span> Wonderful things did he do in the sight
of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, in the field of Tanis.

<span id="an_77:13">77:13</span> He divided the sea and brought them
through: and he made the waters to stand as in a vessel.

<span id="an_77:14">77:14</span> And he conducted them with a cloud by
day: and all the night with a light of

<span id="an_77:15">77:15</span> He struck the rock in the wilderness:
and gave them to drink, as out of the great deep.

<span id="an_77:16">77:16</span> He brought forth water out of the rock:
and made streams run down as rivers.

<span id="an_77:17">77:17</span> And they added yet more sin against
him: they provoked the most High to wrath in the place without water.

<span id="an_77:18">77:18</span> And they tempted God in their hearts,
by asking meat for their desires.

<span id="an_77:19">77:19</span> And they spoke ill of God: they said:
Can God furnish a table in the wilderness?

<span id="an_77:20">77:20</span> Because he struck the rock, and the
waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed. Can he also give bread,
or provide a table for his people?

<span id="an_77:21">77:21</span> Therefore the Lord heard, and was
angry: and a fire was kindled against Jacob, and wrath came up against
Israel.

<span id="an_77:22">77:22</span> Because they believed not in God: and
trusted not in his salvation.

<span id="an_77:23">77:23</span> And he had commanded the clouds from
above, and had opened the doors of heaven.

<span id="an_77:24">77:24</span> And had rained down manna upon them to
eat, and had given them the bread of heaven.

<span id="an_77:25">77:25</span> Man ate the bread of angels: he sent
them provisions in abundance.

<span id="an_77:26">77:26</span> He removed the south wind from heaven:
and by his power brought in the southwest wind.

<span id="an_77:27">77:27</span> And he rained upon them flesh as dust:
and feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea.

<span id="an_77:28">77:28</span> And they fell in the midst of their
camp, round about their pavilions.

<span id="an_77:29">77:29</span> So they did eat, and were filled
exceedingly, and he gave them their desire:

<span id="an_77:30">77:30</span> they were not defrauded of that which
they craved. As yet their meat was in their mouth:

<span id="an_77:31">77:31</span> and the wrath of God came upon them.
And he slew the fat ones amongst them, and brought down the chosen men
of Israel.

<span id="an_77:32">77:32</span> In all these things they sinned still:
and they believed not for his wondrous works.

<span id="an_77:33">77:33</span> And their days were consumed in vanity,
and their years in haste.

<span id="an_77:34">77:34</span> When he slew them, then they sought
him: and they returned, and came to him early in the morning.

<span id="an_77:35">77:35</span> And they remembered that God was their
helper: and the most high God their redeemer.

<span id="an_77:36">77:36</span> And they loved him with their mouth:
and with their tongue they lied unto him:

<span id="an_77:37">77:37</span> But their heart was not right with him:
nor were they counted faithful in his covenant.

<span id="an_77:38">77:38</span> But he is merciful, and will forgive
their sins: and will not destroy them. And many a time did he turn away
his anger: and did not kindle all his wrath.

<span id="an_77:39">77:39</span> And he remembered that they are flesh:
a wind that goeth and returneth not.

<span id="an_77:40">77:40</span> How often did they provoke him in the
desert: and move him to wrath in the place without water?

<span id="an_77:41">77:41</span> And they turned back and tempted God:
and grieved the holy one of Israel.

<span id="an_77:42">77:42</span> They remembered not his hand, in the
day that he redeemed them from the hand of him that afflicted them:

<span id="an_77:43">77:43</span> How he wrought his signs in Egypt, and
his wonders in the field of Tanis.

<span id="an_77:44">77:44</span> And he turned their rivers into blood,
and their showers that they might, not drink.

<span id="an_77:45">77:45</span> He sent amongst them divers sores of
flies, which devoured them: and frogs which destroyed them.

<span id="an_77:46">77:46</span> And he gave up their fruits to the
blast, and their labours to the locust.

<span id="an_77:47">77:47</span> And he destroyed their vineyards with
hail, and their mulberry trees with hoarfrost.

<span id="an_77:48">77:48</span> And he gave up their cattle to the
hail, and their stock to the fire.

<span id="an_77:49">77:49</span> And he sent upon them the wrath of his
indignation: indignation and wrath and trouble, which he sent by evil
angels.

<span id="an_77:50">77:50</span> He made a way for a path to his anger:
he spared not their souls from death, and their cattle he shut up in
death.

<span id="an_77:51">77:51</span> And he killed all the firstborn in the
land of Egypt: the firstfruits of all their labour in the tabernacles of
Cham.

<span id="an_77:52">77:52</span> And he took away his own people as
sheep: and guided them in the wilderness like a flock.

<span id="an_77:53">77:53</span> And he brought them out in hope, and
they feared not: and the sea overwhelmed their enemies.

<span id="an_77:54">77:54</span> And he brought them into the mountain
of his sanctuary: the mountain which his right hand had purchased. And
he cast out the Gentiles before them: and by lot divided to them their
land by a line of distribution.

<span id="an_77:55">77:55</span> And he made the tribes of Israel to
dwell in their tabernacles.

<span id="an_77:56">77:56</span> Yet they tempted, and provoked the most
high God: and they kept not his testimonies.

<span id="an_77:57">77:57</span> And they turned away, and kept not the
covenant: even like their fathers they were turned aside as a crooked
bow.

<span id="an_77:58">77:58</span> They provoked him to anger on their
hills: and moved him to jealousy with their graven things.

<span id="an_77:59">77:59</span> God heard, and despised them, and he
reduced Israel exceedingly as it were to nothing.

<span id="an_77:60">77:60</span> And he put away the tabernacle of Silo,
his tabernacle where he dwelt among men.

<span id="an_77:61">77:61</span> And he delivered their strength into
captivity: and their beauty into the hands of the enemy.

<span id="an_77:62">77:62</span> And he shut up his people under the
sword: and he despised his inheritance.

<span id="an_77:63">77:63</span> Fire consumed their young men: and
their maidens were not lamented.

<span id="an_77:64">77:64</span> Their priests fell by the sword: and
their widows did not mourn.

<span id="an_77:65">77:65</span> And the Lord was awaked as one out of
sleep, and like a mighty man that hath been surfeited with wine.

<span id="an_77:66">77:66</span> And he smote his enemies on the hinder
parts: he put them to an everlasting reproach.

<span id="an_77:67">77:67</span> And he rejected the tabernacle of
Joseph: and chose not the tribe of Ephraim:

<span id="an_77:68">77:68</span> But he chose the tribe of Juda, mount
Sion which he loved.

<span id="an_77:69">77:69</span> And he built his sanctuary as of
unicorns, in the land which he founded for ever.

<span id="an_77:70">77:70</span> And he chose his servant David, and
took him from the hocks of sheep: he brought him from following the ewes
great with young,

<span id="an_77:71">77:71</span> To feed Jacob his servant, and Israel
his inheritance.

<span id="an_77:72">77:72</span> And he fed them in the innocence of his
heart: and conducted them by the skilfulness of his hands.

<span id="an_78:1">78:1</span> A psalm for Asaph. O God, the heathens
are come into thy inheritance, they have defiled thy holy temple: they
have made Jerusalem as a place to keep fruit.

<span id="an_78:2">78:2</span> They have given the dead bodies of thy
servants to be meat for the fowls of the air: the flesh of thy saints
for the beasts of the earth.

<span id="an_78:3">78:3</span> They have poured out their blood as
water, round about Jerusalem and there was none to bury them.

<span id="an_78:4">78:4</span> We are become a reproach to our
neighbours: a scorn and derision to them that are round about us.

<span id="an_78:5">78:5</span> How long, O Lord, wilt thou be angry for
ever: shall thy zeal be kindled like a fire?

<span id="an_78:6">78:6</span> Pour out thy wrath upon the nations that
have not known thee: and upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy
name.

<span id="an_78:7">78:7</span> Because they have devoured Jacob; and
have laid waste his place.

<span id="an_78:8">78:8</span> Remember not our former iniquities: let
thy mercies speedily prevent us, for we are become exceeding poor.

<span id="an_78:9">78:9</span> Help us, O God, our saviour: and for the
glory of thy name, O Lord, deliver us: and forgive us our sins for thy
name's sake:

<span id="an_78:10">78:10</span> Lest they should say among the
Gentiles: Where is their God? And let him be made known among the
nations before our eyes, By the revenging the blood of thy servants,
which hath been shed:

<span id="an_78:11">78:11</span> let the sighing of the prisoners come
in before thee. According to the greatness of thy arm, take possession
of the children of them that have been put to death.

<span id="an_78:12">78:12</span> And render to our neighbours sevenfold
in their bosom: the reproach wherewith they have reproached thee, O
Lord.

<span id="an_78:13">78:13</span> But we thy people, and the sheep of thy
pasture, will give thanks to thee for ever. We will shew forth thy
praise, unto generation and generation.

<span id="an_79:1">79:1</span> Unto the end, for them that shall he
changed, a testimony for Asaph, a psalm.

<span id="an_79:2">79:2</span> Give ear, O thou that rulest Israel: thou
that leadest Joseph like a sheep. Thou that sittest upon the cherubims,
shine forth

<span id="an_79:3">79:3</span> before Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasses.
Stir up thy might, and come to save us.

<span id="an_79:4">79:4</span> Convert us, O God: and shew us thy face,
and we shall be saved.

<span id="an_79:5">79:5</span> O Lord God of hosts, how long wilt thou
be angry against the prayer of thy servant?

<span id="an_79:6">79:6</span> How long wilt thou feed us with the bread
of tears: and give us for our drink tears in measure?

<span id="an_79:7">79:7</span> Thou hast made us to be a contradiction
to our neighbours: and our enemies have scoffed at us.

<span id="an_79:8">79:8</span> O God of hosts, convert us: and shew thy
face, and we shall be saved.

<span id="an_79:9">79:9</span> Thou hast brought a vineyard out of
Egypt: thou hast cast cut the Gentiles and planted it.

<span id="an_79:10">79:10</span> Thou wast the guide of its journey in
its sight: thou plantedst the roots thereof, and it filled the land.

<span id="an_79:11">79:11</span> The shadow of it covered the hills: and
the branches thereof the cedars of God.

<span id="an_79:12">79:12</span> It stretched forth its branches unto
the sea, and its boughs unto the river.

<span id="an_79:13">79:13</span> Why hast thou broken down the hedge
thereof, so that all they who pass by the way do pluck it?

<span id="an_79:14">79:14</span> The boar out of the wood hath laid it
waste: and a singular wild beast hath devoured it.

<span id="an_79:15">79:15</span> Turn again, O God of hosts, look down
from heaven, and see, and visit this vineyard:

<span id="an_79:16">79:16</span> And perfect the same which thy right
hand hath planted: and upon the son of man whom thou hast confirmed for
thyself.

<span id="an_79:17">79:17</span> Things set on fire and dug down shall
perish at the rebuke of thy countenance.

<span id="an_79:18">79:18</span> Let thy hand be upon the man of thy
right hand: and upon the son of man whom thou hast confirmed for
thyself.

<span id="an_79:19">79:19</span> And we depart not from thee, thou shalt
quicken us: and we will call upon thy name.

<span id="an_79:20">79:20</span> O Lord God of hosts, convert us: and
shew thy face, and we shall be saved.

<span id="an_80:1">80:1</span> Unto the end, for the winepresses, a
psalm for Asaph himself.

<span id="an_80:2">80:2</span> Rejoice to God our helper: sing aloud to
the God of Jacob.

<span id="an_80:3">80:3</span> Take a psalm, and bring hither the
timbrel: the pleasant psaltery with the harp.

<span id="an_80:4">80:4</span> Blow up the trumpet on the new moon, on
the noted day of your solemnity.

<span id="an_80:5">80:5</span> For it is a commandment in Israel, and a
judgment to the God of Jacob.

<span id="an_80:6">80:6</span> He ordained it for a testimony in Joseph,
when he came out of the land of Egypt: he heard a tongue which he knew
not.

<span id="an_80:7">80:7</span> He removed his back from the burdens: his
hands had served in baskets.

<span id="an_80:8">80:8</span> Thou calledst upon me in affliction, and
I delivered thee: I heard thee in the secret place of tempest: I proved
thee at the waters of contradiction.

<span id="an_80:9">80:9</span> Hear, O my people, and I will testify to
thee: O Israel, if thou wilt hearken to me,

<span id="an_80:10">80:10</span> there shall be no new god in thee:
neither shalt thou adore a strange god.

<span id="an_80:11">80:11</span> For I am the Lord thy God, who brought
thee out of the land of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it.

<span id="an_80:12">80:12</span> But my people heard not my voice: and
Israel hearkened not to me.

<span id="an_80:13">80:13</span> So I let them go according to the
desires of their heart: they shall walk in their own inventions.

<span id="an_80:14">80:14</span> If my people had heard me: if Israel
had walked in my ways:

<span id="an_80:15">80:15</span> I should soon have humbled their
enemies, and laid my hand on them that troubled them.

<span id="an_80:16">80:16</span> The enemies of the Lord have lied to
him: and their time shall be for ever.

<span id="an_80:17">80:17</span> And he fed them with the fat of wheat,
and filled them with honey out of the rock.

<span id="an_81:1">81:1</span> A psalm for Asaph. God hath stood in the
congregation of gods: and being in the midst of them he judgeth gods.

<span id="an_81:2">81:2</span> How long will you judge unjustly: and
accept the persons of the wicked?

<span id="an_81:3">81:3</span> Judge for the needy and fatherless: do
justice to the humble and the poor.

<span id="an_81:4">81:4</span> Rescue the poor; and deliver the needy
out of the hand of the sinner.

<span id="an_81:5">81:5</span> They have not known nor understood: they
walk on in darkness: all the foundations of the earth shall be moved.

<span id="an_81:6">81:6</span> I have said: You are gods and all of you
the sons of the most High.

<span id="an_81:7">81:7</span> But you like men shall die: and shall
fall like one of the princes.

<span id="an_81:8">81:8</span> Arise, O God, judge thou the earth: for
thou shalt inherit among all the nations.

<span id="an_82:1">82:1</span> A canticle of a psalm for Asaph.

<span id="an_82:2">82:2</span> O God, who shall be like to thee? hold
not thy peace, neither be thou still, O God.

<span id="an_82:3">82:3</span> For lo, thy enemies have made a noise:
and they that hate thee have lifted up the head.

<span id="an_82:4">82:4</span> They have taken a malicious counsel
against thy people, and have consulted against thy saints.

<span id="an_82:5">82:5</span> They have said: Come and let us destroy
them, so that they be not a nation: and let the name of Israel be
remembered no more.

<span id="an_82:6">82:6</span> For they have contrived with one consent:
they have made a covenant together against thee,

<span id="an_82:7">82:7</span> the tabernacles of the Edomites, and the
Ismahelites: Moab, and the Agarens,

<span id="an_82:8">82:8</span> Gebal, and Ammon and Amalec: the
Philistines, with the inhabitants of Tyre.

<span id="an_82:9">82:9</span> Yea, and the Assyrian also is joined with
them: they are come to the aid of the sons of Lot.

<span id="an_82:10">82:10</span> Do to them as thou didst to Madian and
to Sisara: as to Jabin at the brook of Cisson.

<span id="an_82:11">82:11</span> Who perished at Endor: and became as
dung for the earth.

<span id="an_82:12">82:12</span> Make their princes like Oreb, and Zeb,
and Zebee, and Salmana. All their princes,

<span id="an_82:13">82:13</span> who have said: Let us possess the
sanctuary of God for an inheritance.

<span id="an_82:14">82:14</span> O my God, make them like a wheel; and
as stubble before the wind.

<span id="an_82:15">82:15</span> As fire which burneth the wood: and as
a flame burning mountains:

<span id="an_82:16">82:16</span> So shalt thou pursue them with thy
tempest: and shalt trouble them in thy wrath.

<span id="an_82:17">82:17</span> Fill their faces with shame; and they
shall seek thy name, O Lord.

<span id="an_82:18">82:18</span> Let them be ashamed and troubled for
ever and ever: and let them be confounded and perish.

<span id="an_82:19">82:19</span> And let them know that the Lord is thy
name: thou alone art the most High over all the earth.

<span id="an_83:1">83:1</span> Unto the end, for the winepresses, a
psalm for the sons of Core.

<span id="an_83:2">83:2</span> How lovely are thy tabernacles, O Lord of
host!

<span id="an_83:3">83:3</span> my soul longeth and fainteth for the
courts of the Lord. My heart and my flesh have rejoiced in the living
God.

<span id="an_83:4">83:4</span> For the sparrow hath found herself a
house, and the turtle a nest for herself where she may lay her young
ones: Thy altars, O Lord of hosts, my king and my God.

<span id="an_83:5">83:5</span> Blessed are they that dwell in thy house,
O Lord: they shall praise thee for ever and ever.

<span id="an_83:6">83:6</span> Blessed is the man whose help is from
thee: in his heart he hath disposed to ascend by steps,

<span id="an_83:7">83:7</span> in the vale of tears, in the place which
be hath set.

<span id="an_83:8">83:8</span> For the lawgiver shall give a blessing,
they shall go from virtue to virtue: the God of gods shall be seen in
Sion.

<span id="an_83:9">83:9</span> O Lord God of hosts, hear my prayer: give
ear, O God of Jacob.

<span id="an_83:10">83:10</span> Behold, O God our protector: and look
on the face of thy Christ.

<span id="an_83:11">83:11</span> For better is one day in thy courts
above thousands. I have chosen to be an abject in the house of my God,
rather than to dwell in the tabernacles of sinners.

<span id="an_83:12">83:12</span> For God loveth mercy and truth: the
Lord will give grace and glory.

<span id="an_83:13">83:13</span> He will not deprive of good things them
that walk in innocence : O Lord of hosts, blessed is the man that
trusteth in thee.

<span id="an_84:1">84:1</span> Unto the end, for the sons of Core, a
psalm.

<span id="an_84:2">84:2</span> Lord, thou hast blessed thy land: thou
hast turned away the captivity of Jacob.

<span id="an_84:3">84:3</span> Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy
people: thou hast covered all their sins.

<span id="an_84:4">84:4</span> Thou hast mitigated all thy anger: thou
best turned away from the wrath of thy indignation.

<span id="an_84:5">84:5</span> Convert us, O God our saviour: and turn
off thy anger from us.

<span id="an_84:6">84:6</span> Wilt thou be angry with us for ever: or
wilt thou extend thy wrath from generation to generation?

<span id="an_84:7">84:7</span> Thou wilt turn, O God, and bring us to
life: and thy people shall rejoice in thee.

<span id="an_84:8">84:8</span> Shew us, O Lord, thy mercy; and grant us
thy salvation.

<span id="an_84:9">84:9</span> I will hear what the Lord God will speak
in me: for he will speak peace unto his people: And unto his saints: and
unto them that are converted to the heart.

<span id="an_84:10">84:10</span> Surely his salvation is near to them
that fear him: that glory may dwell in our land.

<span id="an_84:11">84:11</span> Mercy and truth have met each other:
justice and peace have kissed.

<span id="an_84:12">84:12</span> Truth is sprung out of the earth: and
justice hath looked down from heaven.

<span id="an_84:13">84:13</span> For the Lord will give goodness: and
our earth shall yield her fruit.

<span id="an_84:14">84:14</span> Justice shall walk before him: and
shall set his steps in the way.

<span id="an_85:1">85:1</span> A prayer for David himself. Incline thy
ear, O Lord, and hear me: for I am needy and poor.

<span id="an_85:2">85:2</span> Preserve my soul, for I am holy: save thy
servant, O my God, that trusteth in thee.

<span id="an_85:3">85:3</span> Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I have
cried to thee all the day.

<span id="an_85:4">85:4</span> Give joy to the soul of thy servant, for
to thee, O Lord, I have lifted up my soul.

<span id="an_85:5">85:5</span> For thou, O Lord, art sweet and mild: and
plenteous in mercy to all that call upon thee.

<span id="an_85:6">85:6</span> Give ear, O Lord, to my prayer: and
attend to the voice of my petition.

<span id="an_85:7">85:7</span> I have called upon thee in the day of my
trouble: because thou hast heard me.

<span id="an_85:8">85:8</span> There is none among the gods like unto
thee, O Lord: and there is none according to thy works.

<span id="an_85:9">85:9</span> All the nations thou hast made shall come
and adore before thee, O Lord: and they shall glorify thy name.

<span id="an_85:10">85:10</span> For thou art great and dost wonderful
things: thou art God alone.

<span id="an_85:11">85:11</span> Conduct me, O Lord, in thy way, and I
will walk in thy truth: let my heart rejoice that it may fear thy name.

<span id="an_85:12">85:12</span> I will praise thee, O Lord my God: with
my whole heart, and I will glorify thy name for ever:

<span id="an_85:13">85:13</span> For thy mercy is great towards me: and
thou hast delivered my soul out of the lower hell.

<span id="an_85:14">85:14</span> O God, the wicked are risen up against
me, and the assembly of the mighty have sought my soul: and they have
not set thee before their eyes.

<span id="an_85:15">85:15</span> And thou, O Lord, art a God of
compassion, and merciful, patient, and of much mercy, and true.

<span id="an_85:16">85:16</span> O look upon me, and have mercy on me:
give thy command to thy servant, and save the son of thy handmaid.

<span id="an_85:17">85:17</span> Shew me a token for good: that they who
hate me may see, and be confounded, because thou, O Lord, hast helped me
and hast comforted me.

<span id="an_86:1">86:1</span> For the sons of Core, a psalm of a
canticle. The foundations thereof are in the holy mountains:

<span id="an_86:2">86:2</span> The Lord loveth the gates of Sion above
all the tabernacles of Jacob.

<span id="an_86:3">86:3</span> Glorious things are said of thee, O city
of God.

<span id="an_86:4">86:4</span> I will be mindful of Rahab and of Babylon
knowing me. Behold the foreigners, and Tyre, and the people of the
Ethiopians, these were there.

<span id="an_86:5">86:5</span> Shall not Sion say: This man and that man
is born in her? and the Highest himself hath founded her.

<span id="an_86:6">86:6</span> The Lord shall tell in his writings of
peoples and of princes, of them that have been in her.

<span id="an_86:7">86:7</span> The dwelling in thee is as it were of all
rejoicing.

<span id="an_87:1">87:1</span> A canticle of a psalm for the sons of
Core: unto the end, for Maheleth, to answer understanding of Eman the
Ezrahite.

<span id="an_87:2">87:2</span> O Lord, the God of my salvation: I have
cried in the day, and in the night before thee.

<span id="an_87:3">87:3</span> Let my prayer come in before thee:
incline thy ear to my petition.

<span id="an_87:4">87:4</span> For my soul is filled with evils: and my
life hath drawn nigh to hell.

<span id="an_87:5">87:5</span> I am counted among them that go down to
the pit: I am become as a man without help,

<span id="an_87:6">87:6</span> free among the dead. Like the slain
sleeping in the sepulchres, whom thou rememberest no more: and they are
cast off from thy hand.

<span id="an_87:7">87:7</span> They have laid me in the lower pit: in
the dark places, and in the shadow of death.

<span id="an_87:8">87:8</span> Thy wrath is strong over me: and all thy
waves thou hast brought in upon me.

<span id="an_87:9">87:9</span> Thou hast put away my acquaintance far
from me: they have set me an abomination to themselves. I was delivered
up, and came not forth:

<span id="an_87:10">87:10</span> my eyes languished through poverty. All
the day I cried to thee, O Lord: I stretched out my hands to thee.

<span id="an_87:11">87:11</span> Wilt thou shew wonders to the dead? or
shall physicians raise to life, and give praise to thee?

<span id="an_87:12">87:12</span> Shall any one in the sepulchre declare
thy mercy: and thy truth in destruction?

<span id="an_87:13">87:13</span> Shall thy wonders be known in the dark;
and thy justice in the land of forgetfulness?

<span id="an_87:14">87:14</span> But I, O Lord, have cried to thee: and
in the morning my prayer shall prevent thee.

<span id="an_87:15">87:15</span> Lord, why castest thou off my prayer:
why turnest thou away thy face from me?

<span id="an_87:16">87:16</span> I am poor, and in labours from my
youth: and being exalted have been humbled and troubled.

<span id="an_87:17">87:17</span> Thy wrath hath come upon me: and thy
terrors have troubled me.

<span id="an_87:18">87:18</span> They have come round about me like
water all the day: they have compassed me about together.

<span id="an_87:19">87:19</span> Friend and neighbour thou hast put far
from me: and my acquaintance, because of misery.

<span id="an_88:1">88:1</span> Of understanding, for Ethan the Ezrahite.

<span id="an_88:2">88:2</span> The mercies of the Lord I will sing for
ever. I will shew forth thy truth with my mouth to generation and
generation.

<span id="an_88:3">88:3</span> For thou hast said: Mercy shall be built
up for ever in the heavens: thy truth shall be prepared in them.

<span id="an_88:4">88:4</span> I have made a covenant with my elect: I
have sworn to David my servant:

<span id="an_88:5">88:5</span> Thy seed will I settle for ever. And I
will build up thy throne unto generation and generation.

<span id="an_88:6">88:6</span> The heavens shall confess thy wonders, O
Lord: and thy truth in the church of the saints.

<span id="an_88:7">88:7</span> For who in the clouds can be compared to
the Lord: or who among the sons of God shall be like to God?

<span id="an_88:8">88:8</span> God, who is glorified in the assembly of
the saints: great and terrible above all them that are about him.

<span id="an_88:9">88:9</span> O Lord God of hosts, who is like to thee?
thou art mighty, O Lord, and thy truth is round about thee.

<span id="an_88:10">88:10</span> Thou rulest the power of the sea: and
appeasest the motion of the waves thereof.

<span id="an_88:11">88:11</span> Thou hast humbled the proud one, as one
that is slain: with the arm of thy strength thou hast scattered thy
enemies.

<span id="an_88:12">88:12</span> Thine are the heavens, and thine is the
earth: the world and the fulness thereof thou hast founded:

<span id="an_88:13">88:13</span> the north and the sea thou hast
created. Thabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name:

<span id="an_88:14">88:14</span> thy arm is with might. Let thy hand be
strengthened, and thy right hand exalted:

<span id="an_88:15">88:15</span> justice and judgment are the
preparation of thy throne. Mercy and truth shall go before thy face:

<span id="an_88:16">88:16</span> blessed is the people that knoweth
jubilation. They shall walk, O Lord, in the light of thy countenance:

<span id="an_88:17">88:17</span> and in thy name they shall rejoice all
the day, and in thy justice they shall be exalted.

<span id="an_88:18">88:18</span> For thou art the glory of their
strength: and in thy good pleasure shall our horn be exalted.

<span id="an_88:19">88:19</span> For our protection is of the Lord, and
of our king the holy one of Israel.

<span id="an_88:20">88:20</span> Then thou spokest in a vision to thy
saints, and saidst: I have laid help upon one that is mighty, and have
exalted one chosen out of my people.

<span id="an_88:21">88:21</span> I have found David my servant: with my
holy oil I have anointed him.

<span id="an_88:22">88:22</span> For my hand shall help him: and my arm
shall strengthen him.

<span id="an_88:23">88:23</span> The enemy shall have no advantage over
him: nor the son of iniquity have power to hurt him.

<span id="an_88:24">88:24</span> And I will cut down his enemies before
his face; and them that hate him I will put to flight.

<span id="an_88:25">88:25</span> And my truth and my mercy shall be with
him: and in my name shall his horn be exalted.

<span id="an_88:26">88:26</span> And I will set his hand in the sea; and
his right hand in the rivers.

<span id="an_88:27">88:27</span> He shall cry out to me: Thou art my
father: my God, and the support of my salvation.

<span id="an_88:28">88:28</span> And I will make him my firstborn, high
above the kings of the earth.

<span id="an_88:29">88:29</span> I will keep my mercy for him for ever:
and my covenant faithful to him.

<span id="an_88:30">88:30</span> And I will make his seed to endure for
evermore: and his throne as the days of heaven.

<span id="an_88:31">88:31</span> And if his children forsake my law, and
walk not in my judgments:

<span id="an_88:32">88:32</span> If they profane my justices: and keep
not my commandments:

<span id="an_88:33">88:33</span> I will visit their iniquities with a
rod: and their sins with stripes.

<span id="an_88:34">88:34</span> But my mercy I will not take away from
him: nor will I suffer my truth to fail.

<span id="an_88:35">88:35</span> Neither will I profane my covenant: and
the words that proceed from my mouth I will not make void.

<span id="an_88:36">88:36</span> Once have I sworn by my holiness: I
will not lie unto David:

<span id="an_88:37">88:37</span> his seed shall endure for ever.

<span id="an_88:38">88:38</span> And his throne as the sun before me:
and as the moon perfect for ever, and a faithful witness in heaven.

<span id="an_88:39">88:39</span> But thou hast rejected and despised:
thou hast been angry with thy anointed.

<span id="an_88:40">88:40</span> Thou hast overthrown the covenant of
thy servant: thou hast profaned his sanctuary on the earth.

<span id="an_88:41">88:41</span> Thou hast broken down all his hedges:
thou hast made his strength fear.

<span id="an_88:42">88:42</span> All that pass by the way have robbed
him: he is become a reproach to his neighbours.

<span id="an_88:43">88:43</span> Thou hast set up the right hand of them
that oppress him: thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice.

<span id="an_88:44">88:44</span> Thou hast turned away the help of his
sword; and hast not assisted him in battle.

<span id="an_88:45">88:45</span> Thou hast made his purification to
cease: and thou hast cast his throne down to the ground.

<span id="an_88:46">88:46</span> Thou hast shortened the days of his
time: thou hast covered him with confusion.

<span id="an_88:47">88:47</span> How long, O Lord, turnest thou away
unto the end? shall thy anger burn like fire?

<span id="an_88:48">88:48</span> Remember what my substance is for hast
thou made all the children of men in vain?

<span id="an_88:49">88:49</span> Who is the man that shall live, and not
see death: that shall deliver his soul from the hand of hell?

<span id="an_88:50">88:50</span> Lord, where are thy ancient mercies,
according to what thou didst swear to David in thy truth?

<span id="an_88:51">88:51</span> Be mindful, O Lord, of the reproach of
thy servants (which I have held in my bosom) of many nations:

<span id="an_88:52">88:52</span> Wherewith thy enemies have reproached,
O Lord; wherewith they have reproached the change of thy anointed.

<span id="an_88:53">88:53</span> Blessed be the Lord for evermore. So be
it. So be it.

<span id="an_89:1">89:1</span> A prayer of Moses the man of God. Lord,
thou hast been our refuge from generation to generation.

<span id="an_89:2">89:2</span> Before the mountains were made, or the
earth and the world was formed; from eternity and to eternity thou art
God.

<span id="an_89:3">89:3</span> Turn not man away to be brought low: and
thou hast said: Be converted, O ye sons of men.

<span id="an_89:4">89:4</span> For a thousand years in thy sight are as
yesterday, which is past. And as a watch in the night,

<span id="an_89:5">89:5</span> things that are counted nothing, shall
their years be.

<span id="an_89:6">89:6</span> In the morning man shall grow up like
grass; in the morning he shall flourish and pass away: in the evening he
shall fall, grow dry, and wither.

<span id="an_89:7">89:7</span> For in thy wrath we have fainted away:
and are troubled in thy indignation.

<span id="an_89:8">89:8</span> Thou hast set our iniquities before thy
eyes: our life in the light of thy countenance.

<span id="an_89:9">89:9</span> For all our days are spent; and in thy
wrath we have fainted away. Our years shall be considered spider:

<span id="an_89:10">89:10</span> the days of our years in them are
threescore and ten years. But if in the strong they be fourscore years:
and what is more of them is labour and sorrow. For mildness is come upon
us: and we shall be corrected.

<span id="an_89:11">89:11</span> Who knoweth the power of thy anger, and
for thy fear

<span id="an_89:12">89:12</span> can number thy wrath? So make thy right
hand known: and men learned in heart, in wisdom.

<span id="an_89:13">89:13</span> Return, O Lord, how long? and be
entreated in favour of thy servants.

<span id="an_89:14">89:14</span> We are filled in the morning with thy
mercy: and we have rejoiced, and are delighted all our days.

<span id="an_89:15">89:15</span> We have rejoiced for the days in which
thou hast humbled us: for the years in which we have seen evils.

<span id="an_89:16">89:16</span> Look upon thy servants and upon their
works: and direct their children.

<span id="an_89:17">89:17</span> And let the brightness of the Lord our
God be upon us: and direct thou the works of our hands over us; yea, the
work of our hands do thou direct.

<span id="an_90:1">90:1</span> The praise of a canticle for David. He
that dwelleth in the aid of the most High, shall abide under the
protection of the God of Jacob.

<span id="an_90:2">90:2</span> He shall say to the Lord: Thou art my
protector, and my refuge: my God, in him will I trust.

<span id="an_90:3">90:3</span> For he hath delivered me from the snare
of the hunters: and from the sharp word.

<span id="an_90:4">90:4</span> He will overshadow thee with his
shoulders: and under his wings thou shalt trust.

<span id="an_90:5">90:5</span> His truth shall compass thee with a
shield: thou shalt not be afraid of the terror of the night.

<span id="an_90:6">90:6</span> Of the arrow that flieth in the day, of
the business that walketh about in the dark: of invasion, or of the
noonday devil.

<span id="an_90:7">90:7</span> A thousand shall fall at thy side, and
ten thousand at thy right hand: but it shall not come nigh thee.

<span id="an_90:8">90:8</span> But thou shalt consider with thy eyes:
and shalt see the reward of the wicked.

<span id="an_90:9">90:9</span> Because thou, O Lord, art my hope: thou
hast made the most High thy refuge.

<span id="an_90:10">90:10</span> There shall no evil come to thee: nor
shall the scourge come near thy dwelling.

<span id="an_90:11">90:11</span> For he hath given his angels charge
over thee; to keep thee in all thy ways.

<span id="an_90:12">90:12</span> In their hands they shall bear thee up:
lest thou dash thy foot against a stone.

<span id="an_90:13">90:13</span> Thou shalt walk upon the asp and the
basilisk: and thou shalt trample under foot the lion and the dragon.

<span id="an_90:14">90:14</span> Because he hoped in me I will deliver
him: I will protect him because he hath known my name.

<span id="an_90:15">90:15</span> He shall cry to me, and I will hear
him: I am with him in tribulation, I will deliver him, and I will
glorify him.

<span id="an_90:16">90:16</span> I will fill him with length of days;
and I will shew him my salvation.

<span id="an_91:1">91:1</span> A psalm of a canticle on the sabbath day.

<span id="an_91:2">91:2</span> It is good to give praise to the Lord:
and to sing to thy name, O most High.

<span id="an_91:3">91:3</span> To shew forth thy mercy in the morning,
and thy truth in the night:

<span id="an_91:4">91:4</span> Upon an instrument of ten strings, upon
the psaltery: with a canticle upon the harp.

<span id="an_91:5">91:5</span> For thou hast given me, O Lord, a delight
in thy doings: and in the works of thy hands I shall rejoice.

<span id="an_91:6">91:6</span> O Lord, how great are thy works! thy
thoughts are exceeding deep.

<span id="an_91:7">91:7</span> The senseless man shall not know: nor
will the fool understand these things.

<span id="an_91:8">91:8</span> When the wicked shall spring up as grass:
and all the workers of iniquity shall appear: That they may perish for
ever and ever:

<span id="an_91:9">91:9</span> but thou, O Lord, art most high for
evermore.

<span id="an_91:10">91:10</span> For behold thy enemies, O Lord, for
behold thy enemies shall perish: and all the workers of iniquity shall
be scattered.

<span id="an_91:11">91:11</span> But my horn shall be exalted like that
of the unicorn: and my old age in plentiful mercy.

<span id="an_91:12">91:12</span> My eye also hath looked down upon my
enemies: and my ear shall hear of the downfall of the malignant that
rise up against me.

<span id="an_91:13">91:13</span> The just shall flourish like the palm
tree: he shall grow up like the cedar of Libanus.

<span id="an_91:14">91:14</span> They that are planted in the house of
the Lord shall flourish in the courts of the house of our God.

<span id="an_91:15">91:15</span> They shall still increase in a fruitful
old age: and shall be well treated,

<span id="an_91:16">91:16</span> that they may shew, That the Lord our
God is righteous, and there is no iniquity in him.

<span id="an_92:1">92:1</span> The Lord hath reigned, he is clothed with
beauty: the Lord is clothed with strength, and hath girded himself. For
he hath established the world which shall not be moved.

<span id="an_92:2">92:2</span> Thy throne is prepared from of old: thou
art from everlasting.

<span id="an_92:3">92:3</span> The floods have lifted up, O Lord: the
floods have lifted up their voice. The floods have lifted up their
waves,

<span id="an_92:4">92:4</span> with the noise of many waters. Wonderful
are the surges of the sea: wonderful is the Lord on high.

<span id="an_92:5">92:5</span> Thy testimonies are become exceedingly
credible: holiness becometh thy house, O Lord, unto length of days.

<span id="an_93:1">93:1</span> The Lord is the God to whom revenge
belongeth: the God of revenge hath acted freely.

<span id="an_93:2">93:2</span> Lift up thyself, thou that judgest the
earth: render a reward to the proud.

<span id="an_93:3">93:3</span> How long shall sinners, O Lord: how long
shall sinners glory?

<span id="an_93:4">93:4</span> Shall they utter, and speak iniquity:
shall all speak who work injustice?

<span id="an_93:5">93:5</span> Thy people, O Lord, they have brought
low: and they have afflicted thy inheritance.

<span id="an_93:6">93:6</span> They have slain the widow and the
stranger: and they have murdered the fatherless.

<span id="an_93:7">93:7</span> And they have said: The Lord shall not
see: neither shall the God of Jacob understand.

<span id="an_93:8">93:8</span> Understand, ye senseless among the
people: and, you fools, be wise at last.

<span id="an_93:9">93:9</span> He that planted the ear, shall he not
hear? or he that formed the eye, doth he not consider?

<span id="an_93:10">93:10</span> He that chastiseth nations, shall he
not rebuke: he that teacheth man knowledge?

<span id="an_93:11">93:11</span> The Lord knoweth the thoughts of men,
that they are vain.

<span id="an_93:12">93:12</span> Blessed is the man whom thou shalt
instruct, O Lord: and shalt teach him out of thy law.

<span id="an_93:13">93:13</span> That thou mayst give him rest from the
evil days: till a pit be dug for the wicked.

<span id="an_93:14">93:14</span> For the Lord will not cast off his
people: neither will he forsake his own inheritance.

<span id="an_93:15">93:15</span> Until justice be turned into judgment:
and they that are near it are all the upright in heart.

<span id="an_93:16">93:16</span> Who shall rise up for me against the
evildoers? or who shall stand with me against the workers of iniquity?

<span id="an_93:17">93:17</span> Unless the Lord had been my helper, my
soul had almost dwelt in hell.

<span id="an_93:18">93:18</span> If I said: My foot is moved: thy mercy,
O Lord, assisted me.

<span id="an_93:19">93:19</span> According to the multitude of my
sorrows in my heart, thy comforts have given joy to my soul.

<span id="an_93:20">93:20</span> Doth the seat of iniquity stick to
thee, who framest labour in commandment?

<span id="an_93:21">93:21</span> They will hunt after the soul of the
just, and will condemn innocent blood.

<span id="an_93:22">93:22</span> But the Lord is my refuge: and my God
the help of my hope.

<span id="an_93:23">93:23</span> And he will render them their iniquity:
and in their malice he will destroy them: the Lord our God will destroy
them.

<span id="an_94:1">94:1</span> Come let us praise the Lord with joy: let
us joyfully sing to God our saviour.

<span id="an_94:2">94:2</span> Let us come before his presence with
thanksgiving; and make a joyful noise to him with psalms.

<span id="an_94:3">94:3</span> For the Lord is a great God, and a great
King above all gods.

<span id="an_94:4">94:4</span> For in his hand are all the ends of the
earth: and the heights of the mountains are his.

<span id="an_94:5">94:5</span> For the sea is his, and he made it: and
his hands formed the dry land.

<span id="an_94:6">94:6</span> Come let us adore and fall down: and weep
before the Lord that made us.

<span id="an_94:7">94:7</span> For he is the Lord our God: and we are
the people of his pasture and the sheep of his hand.

<span id="an_94:8">94:8</span> To day if you shall hear his voice,
harden not your hearts:

<span id="an_94:9">94:9</span> As in the provocation, according to the
day of temptation in the wilderness: where your fathers tempted me, they
proved me, and saw my works.

<span id="an_94:10">94:10</span> Forty years long was I offended with
that generation, and I said: These always err in heart.

<span id="an_94:11">94:11</span> And these men have not known my ways:
so I swore in my wrath that they shall not enter into my rest.

<span id="an_95:1">95:1</span> A canticle for David himself, when the
house was built after the captivity. Sing ye to the Lord a new canticle:
sing to the Lord, all the earth.

<span id="an_95:2">95:2</span> Sing ye to the Lord and bless his name:
shew forth his salvation from day to day.

<span id="an_95:3">95:3</span> Declare his glory among the Gentiles: his
wonders among all people.

<span id="an_95:4">95:4</span> For the Lord is great, and exceedingly to
be praised: he is to be feared above all gods.

<span id="an_95:5">95:5</span> For all the gods of the Gentiles are
devils: but the Lord made the heavens.

<span id="an_95:6">95:6</span> Praise and beauty are before him:
holiness and majesty in his sanctuary.

<span id="an_95:7">95:7</span> Bring ye to the Lord, O ye kindreds of
the Gentiles, bring ye to the Lord glory and honour:

<span id="an_95:8">95:8</span> bring to the Lord glory unto his name.
Bring up sacrifices, and come into his courts:

<span id="an_95:9">95:9</span> adore ye the Lord in his holy court. Let
all the earth be moved at his presence.

<span id="an_95:10">95:10</span> Say ye among the Gentiles, the Lord
hath reigned. For he hath corrected the world, which shall not be moved:
he will judge the people with justice.

<span id="an_95:11">95:11</span> Let the heavens rejoice, and let the
earth be glad, let the sea be moved, and the fulness thereof:

<span id="an_95:12">95:12</span> the fields and all things that are in
them shall be joyful. Then shall all the trees of the woods rejoice

<span id="an_95:13">95:13</span> before the face of the Lord, because he
cometh: because he cometh to judge the earth. He shall judge the world
with justice, and the people with his truth.

<span id="an_96:1">96:1</span> For the same David, when his land was
restored again to him. The Lord hath reigned, let the earth rejoice: let
many islands be glad.

<span id="an_96:2">96:2</span> Clouds and darkness are round about him:
justice and judgment are the establishment of his throne.

<span id="an_96:3">96:3</span> A fire shall go before him, and shall
burn his enemies round about.

<span id="an_96:4">96:4</span> His lightnings have shone forth to the
world: the earth saw and trembled.

<span id="an_96:5">96:5</span> The mountains melted like wax, at the
presence of the Lord: at the presence of the Lord of all the earth.

<span id="an_96:6">96:6</span> The heavens declared his justice: and all
people saw his glory.

<span id="an_96:7">96:7</span> Let them be all confounded that adore
graven things, and that glory in their idols. Adore him, all you his
angels:

<span id="an_96:8">96:8</span> Sion heard, and was glad. And the
daughters of Juda rejoiced, because of thy judgments, O Lord.

<span id="an_96:9">96:9</span> For thou art the most high Lord over all
the earth: thou art exalted exceedingly above all gods.

<span id="an_96:10">96:10</span> You that love the Lord, hate evil: the
Lord preserveth the souls of his saints, he will deliver them out of the
hand of the sinner.

<span id="an_96:11">96:11</span> Light is risen to the just, and joy to
the right of heart.

<span id="an_96:12">96:12</span> Rejoice, ye just, in the Lord: and give
praise to the remembrance of his holiness.

<span id="an_97:1">97:1</span> A psalm for David himself. Sing ye to the
Lord anew canticle: because he hath done wonderful things. His right
hand hath wrought for him salvation, and his arm is holy.

<span id="an_97:2">97:2</span> The Lord hath made known his salvation:
he hath revealed his justice in the sight of the Gentiles.

<span id="an_97:3">97:3</span> He hath remembered his mercy his truth
toward the house of Israel. All the ends of the earth have seen the
salvation of our God.

<span id="an_97:4">97:4</span> Sing joyfully to God, all the earth; make
melody, rejoice and sing.

<span id="an_97:5">97:5</span> Sing praise to the Lord on the harp, on
the harp, and with the voice of a psalm:

<span id="an_97:6">97:6</span> with long trumpets, and sound of comet.
Make a joyful noise before the Lord our king:

<span id="an_97:7">97:7</span> let the sea be moved and the fulness
thereof: the world end they that dwell therein.

<span id="an_97:8">97:8</span> The rivers shall clap their hands, the
mountains shall rejoice together

<span id="an_97:9">97:9</span> at the presence of the Lord: because he
cometh to judge the earth. He shall judge the world with justice, and
the people with equity.

<span id="an_98:1">98:1</span> A psalm for David himself. The Lord hath
reigned, let the people be angry: he that sitteth on the cherubims: let
the earth be moved.

<span id="an_98:2">98:2</span> The Lord is great in Sion, and high above
all people.

<span id="an_98:3">98:3</span> Let them give praise to thy great name:
for it is terrible and holy:

<span id="an_98:4">98:4</span> and the king's honour loveth judgment.
Thou hast prepared directions: thou hast done judgment and justice in
Jacob.

<span id="an_98:5">98:5</span> Exalt ye the Lord our God, and adore his
footstool, for it is holy.

<span id="an_98:6">98:6</span> Moses and Aaron among his priests: and
Samuel among them that call upon his name. They called upon the Lord,
and he heard them:

<span id="an_98:7">98:7</span> he spoke to them in the pillar of the
cloud. They kept his testimonies, and the commandment which he gave
them.

<span id="an_98:8">98:8</span> Thou didst hear them, O Lord our God:
thou wast a merciful God to them, and taking vengeance on all their
inventions.

<span id="an_98:9">98:9</span> Exalt ye the Lord our God, and adore at
his holy mountain: for the Lord our God is holy.

<span id="an_99:1">99:1</span> A psalm of praise.

<span id="an_99:2">99:2</span> Sing joyfully to God, all the earth:
serve ye the Lord with gladness. Come in before his presence with
exceeding great joy.

<span id="an_99:3">99:3</span> Know ye that the Lord he is God: he made
us, and not we ourselves. We are his people and the sheep of his
pasture.

<span id="an_99:4">99:4</span> Go ye into his gates with praise, into
his courts with hymns: and give glory to him. Praise ye his name:

<span id="an_99:5">99:5</span> for the Lord is sweet, his mercy endureth
for ever, and his truth to generation and generation.

<span id="an_100:1">100:1</span> A psalm for David himself. Mercy and
judgment I will sing to thee, O Lord: I will sing,

<span id="an_100:2">100:2</span> and I will understand in the unspotted
way, when thou shalt come to me. I walked in the innocence of my heart,
in the midst of my house.

<span id="an_100:3">100:3</span> I did not set before my eyes any unjust
thing: I hated the workers of iniquities.

<span id="an_100:4">100:4</span> The perverse heart did not cleave to
me: and the malignant, that turned aside from me, I would not know.

<span id="an_100:5">100:5</span> The man that in private detracted his
neighbour, him did I persecute. With him that had a proud eye, and an
unsatiable heart, I would not eat.

<span id="an_100:6">100:6</span> My eyes were upon the faithful of the
earth, to sit with me: the man that walked in the perfect way, he served
me.

<span id="an_100:7">100:7</span> He that worketh pride shall not dwell
in the midst of my house: he that speaketh unjust things did not prosper
before my eyes.

<span id="an_100:8">100:8</span> In the morning I put to death all the
wicked of the land: that I might cut off all the workers of iniquity
from the city of the Lord.

<span id="an_101:1">101:1</span> The prayer of the poor man, when he was
anxious, and poured out his supplication before the Lord.

<span id="an_101:2">101:2</span> Hear, O Lord, my prayer: and let my cry
come to thee.

<span id="an_101:3">101:3</span> Turn not away thy face from me: in the
day when I am in trouble, incline thy ear to me. In what day soever I
shall call upon thee, hear me speedily.

<span id="an_101:4">101:4</span> For my days are vanished like smoke:
and my bones are grown dry like fuel for the fire.

<span id="an_101:5">101:5</span> I am smitten as grass, and my heart is
withered: because I forgot to eat my bread.

<span id="an_101:6">101:6</span> Through the voice of my groaning, my
bone hath cleaved to my flesh.

<span id="an_101:7">101:7</span> I am become like to a pelican of the
wilderness: I am like a night raven in the house.

<span id="an_101:8">101:8</span> I have watched, and am become as a
sparrow all alone on the housetop.

<span id="an_101:9">101:9</span> All the day long my enemies reproached
me: and they that praised me did swear against me.

<span id="an_101:10">101:10</span> For I did eat ashes like bread, and
mingled my drink with weeping.

<span id="an_101:11">101:11</span> Because of thy anger and indignation:
for having lifted me up thou hast thrown me down.

<span id="an_101:12">101:12</span> My days have declined like a shadow,
and I am withered like grass.

<span id="an_101:13">101:13</span> But thou, O Lord, endurest for ever:
and thy memorial to all generations.

<span id="an_101:14">101:14</span> Thou shalt arise and have mercy on
Sion: for it is time to have mercy on it, for the time is come.

<span id="an_101:15">101:15</span> For the stones thereof have pleased
thy servants: and they shall have pity on the earth thereof.

<span id="an_101:16">101:16</span> And the Gentiles shall fear thy name,
O Lord, and all the kings of the earth thy glory.

<span id="an_101:17">101:17</span> For the Lord hath built up Sion: and
he shall be seen in his glory.

<span id="an_101:18">101:18</span> He hath had regard to the prayer of
the humble: and he hath not despised their petition.

<span id="an_101:19">101:19</span> Let these things be written unto
another generation: and the people that shall be created shall praise
the Lord:

<span id="an_101:20">101:20</span> Because he hath looked forth from his
high sanctuary: from heaven the Lord hath looked upon the earth.

<span id="an_101:21">101:21</span> That he might hear the groans of them
that are in fetters: that he might release the children of the slain:

<span id="an_101:22">101:22</span> That they may declare the name of the
Lord in Sion: and his praise in Jerusalem;

<span id="an_101:23">101:23</span> When the people assemble together,
and kings, to serve the Lord.

<span id="an_101:24">101:24</span> He answered him in the way of his
strength: Declare unto me the fewness of my days.

<span id="an_101:25">101:25</span> Call me not away in the midst of my
days: thy years are unto generation and generation.

<span id="an_101:26">101:26</span> In the beginning, O Lord, thou
foundedst the earth: end the heavens are the works of thy hands.

<span id="an_101:27">101:27</span> They shall perish but thou remainest:
and all of them shall grow old like a garment: And as a vesture thou
shalt change them, and they shall be changed.

<span id="an_101:28">101:28</span> But thou art always the selfsame, and
thy years shall not fail.

<span id="an_101:29">101:29</span> The children of thy servants shall
continue: and their seed shall be directed for ever.

<span id="an_102:1">102:1</span> For David himself. Bless the Lord, O my
soul: and let all that is within me bless his holy name.

<span id="an_102:2">102:2</span> Bless the Lord, O my soul, and never
forget all he hath done for thee.

<span id="an_102:3">102:3</span> Who forgiveth all thy iniquities: who
healeth all thy diseases.

<span id="an_102:4">102:4</span> Who redeemeth thy life from
destruction: who crowneth thee with mercy and compassion.

<span id="an_102:5">102:5</span> Who satisfieth thy desire with good
things: thy youth shall be renewed like the eagle's.

<span id="an_102:6">102:6</span> The Lord doth mercies, and judgment for
all that suffer wrong.

<span id="an_102:7">102:7</span> He hath made his ways known to Moses:
his wills to the children of Israel.

<span id="an_102:8">102:8</span> The ford is compassionate and merciful:
longsuffering and plenteous in mercy.

<span id="an_102:9">102:9</span> He will not always be angry: nor will
he threaten for ever.

<span id="an_102:10">102:10</span> He hath not dealt with us according
to our sins: nor rewarded us according to our iniquities.

<span id="an_102:11">102:11</span> For according to the height of the
heaven above the earth: he hath strengthened his mercy towards them that
fear him.

<span id="an_102:12">102:12</span> As far as the east is from the west,
so far hath he removed our iniquities from us.

<span id="an_102:13">102:13</span> As a father hath compassion on his
children, so hath the Lord compassion on them that fear him:

<span id="an_102:14">102:14</span> for he knoweth our frame. He
remembereth that we are dust:

<span id="an_102:15">102:15</span> man's days are as grass, as the
flower of the field so shall he flourish.

<span id="an_102:16">102:16</span> For the spirit shall pass in him, and
he shall not be: and he shall know his place no more.

<span id="an_102:17">102:17</span> But the mercy of the Lord is from
eternity and unto eternity upon them that fear him: And his justice unto
children's children,

<span id="an_102:18">102:18</span> to such as keep his covenant, And are
mindful of his commandments to do them.

<span id="an_102:19">102:19</span> The Lord hath prepared his throne in
heaven: and his kingdom shall rule over all.

<span id="an_102:20">102:20</span> Bless the Lord, all ye his angels:
you that are mighty in strength, and execute his word, hearkening to the
voice of his orders.

<span id="an_102:21">102:21</span> Bless the Lord, all ye his hosts: you
ministers of his that do his will.

<span id="an_102:22">102:22</span> Bless the Lord, all his works: in
every place of his dominion, O my soul, bless thou the Lord.

<span id="an_103:1">103:1</span> For David himself. Bless the Lord, O my
soul: O Lord my God, thou art exceedingly great. Thou hast put on praise
and beauty:

<span id="an_103:2">103:2</span> and art clothed with light as with a
garment. Who stretchest out the heaven like a pavilion:

<span id="an_103:3">103:3</span> who coverest the higher rooms thereof
with water. Who makest the clouds thy chariot: who walkest upon the
wings of the winds.

<span id="an_103:4">103:4</span> Who makest thy angels spirits: and thy
ministers a burning fire.

<span id="an_103:5">103:5</span> Who hast founded the earth upon its own
bases: it shall not be moved for ever and ever.

<span id="an_103:6">103:6</span> The deep like a garment is its
clothing: above the mountains shall the waters stand.

<span id="an_103:7">103:7</span> At thy rebuke they shall flee: at the
voice of thy thunder they shall fear.

<span id="an_103:8">103:8</span> The mountains ascend, and the plains
descend into the place which thou hast founded for them.

<span id="an_103:9">103:9</span> Thou hast set a bound which they shall
not pass over; neither shall they return to cover the earth.

<span id="an_103:10">103:10</span> Thou sendest forth springs in the
vales: between the midst of the hills the waters shall pass.

<span id="an_103:11">103:11</span> All the beasts of the field shall
drink: the wild asses shall expect in their thirst.

<span id="an_103:12">103:12</span> Over them the birds of the air shall
dwell: from the midst of the rocks they shall give forth their voices.

<span id="an_103:13">103:13</span> Thou waterest the hills from thy
upper rooms: the earth shall be filled with the fruit of thy works:

<span id="an_103:14">103:14</span> Bringing forth grass for cattle, and
herb for the service of men. That thou mayst bring bread out of the
earth:

<span id="an_103:15">103:15</span> and that wine may cheer the heart of
man. That he may make the face cheerful with oil: and that bread may
strengthen man's heart.

<span id="an_103:16">103:16</span> The trees of the field shall be
filled, and the cedars of Libanus which he hath planted:

<span id="an_103:17">103:17</span> there the sparrows shall make their
nests. The highest of them is the house of the heron.

<span id="an_103:18">103:18</span> The high hills are a refuge for the
harts, the rock for the irchins.

<span id="an_103:19">103:19</span> He hath made the moon for seasons:
the sun knoweth his going down.

<span id="an_103:20">103:20</span> Thou hast appointed darkness, and it
is night: in it shall all the beasts of the woods go about:

<span id="an_103:21">103:21</span> The young lions roaring after their
prey, and seeking their meat from God.

<span id="an_103:22">103:22</span> The sun ariseth, and they are
gathered together: and they shall lie down in their dens.

<span id="an_103:23">103:23</span> Man shall go forth to his work, and
to his labour until the evening.

<span id="an_103:24">103:24</span> How great are thy works, O Lord? thou
hast made all things in wisdom: the earth is filled with thy riches.

<span id="an_103:25">103:25</span> So is this great sea, which
stretcheth wide its arms: there are creeping things without number:
Creatures little and great.

<span id="an_103:26">103:26</span> There the ships shall go. This sea
dragon which thou hast formed to play therein.

<span id="an_103:27">103:27</span> All expect of thee that thou give
them food in season.

<span id="an_103:28">103:28</span> What thou givest to them they shall
gather up: when thou openest thy hand, they shall all be filled with
good.

<span id="an_103:29">103:29</span> But if thou turnest away thy face,
they shall be troubled: thou shalt take away their breath, and they
shall fail, and shall return to their dust.

<span id="an_103:30">103:30</span> Thou shalt send forth thy spirit, and
they shall be created: and thou shalt renew the face of the earth.

<span id="an_103:31">103:31</span> May the glory of the Lord endure for
ever: the Lord shall rejoice in his works.

<span id="an_103:32">103:32</span> He looketh upon the earth, and maketh
it tremble: he toucheth the mountains, and they smoke.

<span id="an_103:33">103:33</span> I will sing to the Lord as long as I
live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.

<span id="an_103:34">103:34</span> Let my speech be acceptable to him:
but I will take delight in the Lord.

<span id="an_103:35">103:35</span> Let sinners be consumed out of the
earth, and the unjust, so that they be no more: O my soul, bless thou
the Lord.

<span id="an_104:1">104:1</span> Alleluia. Give glory to the Lord, and
call upon his name: declare his deeds among the Gentiles.

<span id="an_104:2">104:2</span> Sing to him, yea sing praises to him:
relate all his wondrous works.

<span id="an_104:3">104:3</span> Glory ye in his holy name: let the
heart of them rejoice that seek the Lord.

<span id="an_104:4">104:4</span> Seek ye the Lord, and be strengthened:
seek his face evermore.

<span id="an_104:5">104:5</span> Remember his marvellous works which he
hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth.

<span id="an_104:6">104:6</span> O ye seed of Abraham his servant; ye
sons of Jacob his chosen.

<span id="an_104:7">104:7</span> He is the Lord our God: his judgments
are in all the earth.

<span id="an_104:8">104:8</span> He hath remembered his covenant for
ever: the word which he commanded to a thousand generations.

<span id="an_104:9">104:9</span> Which he made to Abraham; and his oath
to Isaac:

<span id="an_104:10">104:10</span> And he appointed the same to Jacob
for a law, and to Israel for an everlasting testament:

<span id="an_104:11">104:11</span> Saying: To thee will I give the land
of Chanaan, the lot of your inheritance.

<span id="an_104:12">104:12</span> When they were but a small number:
yea very few, and sojourners therein:

<span id="an_104:13">104:13</span> And they passed from nation to
nation, and from one kingdom to another people.

<span id="an_104:14">104:14</span> He suffered no man to hurt them: and
he reproved kings for their sakes.

<span id="an_104:15">104:15</span> Touch ye not my anointed: and do no
evil to my prophets.

<span id="an_104:16">104:16</span> And he called a famine upon the land:
and he broke in pieces all the support of bread.

<span id="an_104:17">104:17</span> He sent a man before them: Joseph,
who was sold for a slave.

<span id="an_104:18">104:18</span> They humbled his feet in fetters: the
iron pierced his soul,

<span id="an_104:19">104:19</span> until his word came. The word of the
Lord inflamed him.

<span id="an_104:20">104:20</span> The king sent, and he released him:
the ruler of the people, and he set him at liberty.

<span id="an_104:21">104:21</span> He made him master of his house, and
ruler of all his possession.

<span id="an_104:22">104:22</span> That he might instruct his princes as
himself, and teach his ancients wisdom.

<span id="an_104:23">104:23</span> And Israel went into Egypt: and Jacob
was a sojourner in the land of Cham.

<span id="an_104:24">104:24</span> And he increased his people
exceedingly: and strengthened them over their enemies,

<span id="an_104:25">104:25</span> He turned their heart to hate his
people: and to deal deceitfully with his servants.

<span id="an_104:26">104:26</span> He sent Moses his servant: Aaron the
man whom he had chosen.

<span id="an_104:27">104:27</span> He gave them power to shew his signs,
and his wonders in the land of Cham.

<span id="an_104:28">104:28</span> He sent darkness, and made it
obscure: and grieved not his words.

<span id="an_104:29">104:29</span> He turned their waters into blood,
and destroyed their fish.

<span id="an_104:30">104:30</span> Their land brought forth frogs, in
the inner chambers of their kings.

<span id="an_104:31">104:31</span> He spoke, and there came divers sorts
of flies and sciniphs in all their coasts.

<span id="an_104:32">104:32</span> He gave them hail for rain, a burning
fire in the land.

<span id="an_104:33">104:33</span> And he destroyed their vineyards and
their fig trees: and he broke in pieces the trees of their coasts.

<span id="an_104:34">104:34</span> He spoke, and the locust came, and
the bruchus, of which there was no number.

<span id="an_104:35">104:35</span> And they devoured all the grass in
their land, and consumed all the fruit of their ground.

<span id="an_104:36">104:36</span> And he slew all the firstborn in
their land: the firstfruits of all their labour.

<span id="an_104:37">104:37</span> And he brought them out with silver
and gold: and there was not among their tribes one that was feeble.

<span id="an_104:38">104:38</span> Egypt was glad when they departed:
for the fear of them lay upon them.

<span id="an_104:39">104:39</span> He spread a cloud for their
protection, and fire to give them light in the night.

<span id="an_104:40">104:40</span> They asked, and the quail came: and
he filled them with the bread of heaven.

<span id="an_104:41">104:41</span> He opened the rock, and waters
flowed: rivers ran down in the dry land.

<span id="an_104:42">104:42</span> Because he remembered his holy word,
which he had spoken to his servant Abraham.

<span id="an_104:43">104:43</span> And he brought forth his people with
joy, and his chosen with gladness.

<span id="an_104:44">104:44</span> And he gave them the lands of the
Gentiles: and they possessed the labours of the people:

<span id="an_104:45">104:45</span> That they might observe his
justifications, and seek after his law.

<span id="an_105:1">105:1</span> Alleluia. Give glory to the Lord, for
he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_105:2">105:2</span> Who shall declare the powers of the
Lord? who shall set forth all his praises?

<span id="an_105:3">105:3</span> Blessed are they that keep judgment,
and do justice at all times.

<span id="an_105:4">105:4</span> Remember us, O Lord, in the favour of
thy people: visit us with thy salvation.

<span id="an_105:5">105:5</span> That we may see the good of thy chosen,
that we may rejoice in the joy of thy nation: that thou mayst be praised
with thy inheritance.

<span id="an_105:6">105:6</span> We have sinned with our fathers: we
have acted unjustly, we have wrought iniquity.

<span id="an_105:7">105:7</span> Our fathers understood not thy wonders
in Egypt: they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies: And they
provoked to wrath going up to the sea, even the Red Sea.

<span id="an_105:8">105:8</span> And he saved them for his own name's
sake: that he might make his power known.

<span id="an_105:9">105:9</span> And he rebuked the Red Sea, and it was
dried up: and he led them through the depths, as in a wilderness.

<span id="an_105:10">105:10</span> And he saved them from the hand of
them that hated them: and he redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.

<span id="an_105:11">105:11</span> And the water covered them that
afflicted them: there was not one of them left.

<span id="an_105:12">105:12</span> And they believed his words: and they
sang his praises.

<span id="an_105:13">105:13</span> They had quickly done, they forgot
his works: and they waited not for his counsels.

<span id="an_105:14">105:14</span> And they coveted their desire in the
desert: and they tempted God in the place without water.

<span id="an_105:15">105:15</span> And he gave them their request: and
sent fulness into their souls.

<span id="an_105:16">105:16</span> And they provoked Moses in the camp,
Aaron the holy one of the Lord.

<span id="an_105:17">105:17</span> The earth opened and swallowed up
Dathan: and covered the congregation of Abiron.

<span id="an_105:18">105:18</span> And a fire was kindled in their
congregation: the flame burned the wicked.

<span id="an_105:19">105:19</span> They made also a calf in Horeb: and
they adored the graven thing.

<span id="an_105:20">105:20</span> And they changed their glory into the
likeness of a calf that eateth grass.

<span id="an_105:21">105:21</span> They forgot God, who saved them, who
had done great things in Egypt,

<span id="an_105:22">105:22</span> wondrous works in the land of Cham:
terrible things in the Red Sea.

<span id="an_105:23">105:23</span> And he said that he would destroy
them: had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach: To turn
away his wrath, lest he should destroy them.

<span id="an_105:24">105:24</span> And they set at nought the desirable
land. They believed not his word,

<span id="an_105:25">105:25</span> and they murmured in their tents:
they hearkened not to the voice of the Lord.

<span id="an_105:26">105:26</span> And he lifted up his hand over them:
to overthrow them in the desert;

<span id="an_105:27">105:27</span> And to cast down their seed among the
nations, and to scatter them in the countries.

<span id="an_105:28">105:28</span> They also were initiated to
Beelphegor: and ate the sacrifices of the dead.

<span id="an_105:29">105:29</span> And they provoked him with their
inventions: and destruction was multiplied among them.

<span id="an_105:30">105:30</span> Then Phinees stood up, and pacified
him: and the slaughter ceased.

<span id="an_105:31">105:31</span> And it was reputed to him unto
justice, to generation and generation for evermore.

<span id="an_105:32">105:32</span> They provoked him also at the waters
of contradiction: and Moses was afflicted for their sakes:

<span id="an_105:33">105:33</span> because they exasperated his spirit.
And he distinguished with his lips.

<span id="an_105:34">105:34</span> They did not destroy the nations of
which the Lord spoke unto them.

<span id="an_105:35">105:35</span> And they were mingled among the
heathens, and learned their works:

<span id="an_105:36">105:36</span> and served their idols, and it became
a stumblingblock to them.

<span id="an_105:37">105:37</span> And they sacrificed their sons, and
their daughters to devils.

<span id="an_105:38">105:38</span> And they shed innocent blood: the
blood of their sons and of their daughters which they sacrificed to the
idols of Chanaan. And the land was polluted with blood,

<span id="an_105:39">105:39</span> and was defiled with their works: and
they went aside after their own inventions.

<span id="an_105:40">105:40</span> And the Lord was exceedingly angry
with his people: and he abhorred his inheritance.

<span id="an_105:41">105:41</span> And he delivered them into the hands
of the nations: and they that hated them had dominion over them.

<span id="an_105:42">105:42</span> And their enemies afflicted them: and
they were humbled under their hands:

<span id="an_105:43">105:43</span> many times did he deliver them. But
they provoked him with their counsel: and they were brought low by their
iniquities.

<span id="an_105:44">105:44</span> And he saw when they were in
tribulation: and he heard their prayer.

<span id="an_105:45">105:45</span> And he was mindful of his covenant:
and repented according to the multitude of his mercies.

<span id="an_105:46">105:46</span> And he gave them unto mercies, in the
sight of all those that had made them captives.

<span id="an_105:47">105:47</span> Save us, O Lord, our God: and gather
us from among nations: That we may give thanks to thy holy name, and may
glory in thy praise.

<span id="an_105:48">105:48</span> Blessed be the Lord the God of
Israel, from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say: So
be it, so be it.

<span id="an_106:1">106:1</span> Give glory to the Lord, for he is good:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_106:2">106:2</span> Let them say so that have been redeemed
by the Lord, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy: and
gathered out of the countries.

<span id="an_106:3">106:3</span> From the rising and the setting of the
sun, from the north and from the sea.

<span id="an_106:4">106:4</span> They wandered in a wilderness, in a
place without water: they found not the way of a city for their
habitation.

<span id="an_106:5">106:5</span> They were hungry and thirsty: their
soul fainted in them.

<span id="an_106:6">106:6</span> And they cried to the Lord in their
tribulation: and he delivered them out of their distresses.

<span id="an_106:7">106:7</span> And he led them into the right way:
that they might go to a city of habitation.

<span id="an_106:8">106:8</span> Let the mercies of the Lord give glory
to him: and his wonderful works to the children of men.

<span id="an_106:9">106:9</span> For he hath satisfied the empty soul,
and hath filled the hungry soul with good things.

<span id="an_106:10">106:10</span> Such as sat in darkness and in the
shadow of death: bound in want and in iron.

<span id="an_106:11">106:11</span> Because they had exasperated the
words of God: and provoked the counsel of the most High:

<span id="an_106:12">106:12</span> And their heart was humbled with
labours: they were weakened, and their was none to help them.

<span id="an_106:13">106:13</span> Then they cried to the Lord in their
affliction: and he delivered them out of their distresses.

<span id="an_106:14">106:14</span> And he brought them out of darkness,
and the shadow of death; and broke their bonds in sunder.

<span id="an_106:15">106:15</span> Let the mercies of the Lord give
glory to him, and his wonderful works to the children of men.

<span id="an_106:16">106:16</span> Because he hath broken gates of
brass, and burst the iron bars.

<span id="an_106:17">106:17</span> He took them out of the way of their
iniquity: for they were brought low for their injustices.

<span id="an_106:18">106:18</span> Their soul abhorred all manner of
meat: and they drew nigh even to the gates of death.

<span id="an_106:19">106:19</span> And they cried to the Lord in their
affliction: and he delivered them out of their distresses.

<span id="an_106:20">106:20</span> He sent his word, and healed them:
and delivered them from their destructions.

<span id="an_106:21">106:21</span> Let the mercies of the Lord give
glory to him: and his wonderful works to the children of men.

<span id="an_106:22">106:22</span> And let them sacrifice the sacrifice
of praise: and declare his works with joy.

<span id="an_106:23">106:23</span> They that go down to the sea in
ships, doing business in the great waters:

<span id="an_106:24">106:24</span> These have seen the works of the
Lord, and his wonders in the deep.

<span id="an_106:25">106:25</span> He said the word, and there arose a
storm of wind: and the waves thereof were lifted up.

<span id="an_106:26">106:26</span> They mount up to the heavens, and
they go down to the depths: their soul pined away with evils.

<span id="an_106:27">106:27</span> They were troubled, and reeled like a
drunken man; and all their wisdom was swallowed up.

<span id="an_106:28">106:28</span> And they cried to the Lord in their
affliction: and he brought them out of their distresses.

<span id="an_106:29">106:29</span> And he turned the storm into a
breeze: and its waves were still.

<span id="an_106:30">106:30</span> And they rejoiced because they were
still: and he brought them to the haven which they wished for.

<span id="an_106:31">106:31</span> Let the mercies of the Lord give
glory to him, and his wonderful works to the children of men.

<span id="an_106:32">106:32</span> And let them exalt him in the church
of the people: and praise him in the chair of the ancients.

<span id="an_106:33">106:33</span> He hath turned rivers into a
wilderness: and the sources of water into dry ground:

<span id="an_106:34">106:34</span> A fruitful land into barrenness, for
the wickedness of them that dwell therein.

<span id="an_106:35">106:35</span> He hath turned a wilderness into
pools of water, and a dry land into water springs.

<span id="an_106:36">106:36</span> And hath placed there the hungry; and
they made a city for their habitation.

<span id="an_106:37">106:37</span> And they sowed fields, and planted
vineyards: and they yielded fruit of birth.

<span id="an_106:38">106:38</span> And he blessed them, and they were
multiplied exceedingly: and their cattle he suffered not to decrease.

<span id="an_106:39">106:39</span> Then they were brought to be few: and
they were afflicted through the trouble of evils and sorrow.

<span id="an_106:40">106:40</span> Contempt was poured forth upon their
princes: and he caused them to wander where there was no passing, and
out of the way.

<span id="an_106:41">106:41</span> And he helped the poor out of
poverty: and made him families like a flock of sheep.

<span id="an_106:42">106:42</span> The just shall see, and shall
rejoice, and all iniquity shall stop their mouth.

<span id="an_106:43">106:43</span> Who is wise, and will keep these
things: and will understand the mercies of the Lord?

<span id="an_107:1">107:1</span> A canticle of a psalm for David
himself.

<span id="an_107:2">107:2</span> My heart is ready, O God, my heart is
ready: I will sing, and will give praise, with my glory.

<span id="an_107:3">107:3</span> Arise, my glory; arise, psaltery and
harp: I will arise in the morning early.

<span id="an_107:4">107:4</span> I will praise thee, O Lord, among the
people: and I will sing unto thee among the populations.

<span id="an_107:5">107:5</span> For thy mercy is great above the
heavens: and thy truth even unto the clouds.

<span id="an_107:6">107:6</span> Be thou exalted, O God, above the
heavens, and thy glory over all the earth:

<span id="an_107:7">107:7</span> that thy beloved may be delivered. Save
with thy right hand and hear me.

<span id="an_107:8">107:8</span> God hath spoken in his holiness. I will
rejoice, and I will divide Sichem and I will mete out the vale of
tabernacles.

<span id="an_107:9">107:9</span> Galaad is mine, and Manasses is mine
and Ephraim the protection of my head. Juda is my king:

<span id="an_107:10">107:10</span> Moab the pot of my hope. Over Edom I
will stretch out my shoe: the aliens are become my friends.

<span id="an_107:11">107:11</span> Who will bring me into the strong
city? who will lead me into Edom?

<span id="an_107:12">107:12</span> Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast
us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our armies?

<span id="an_107:13">107:13</span> O grant us help from trouble: for
