vain is the help of man.

<span id="an_107:14">107:14</span> Through God we shall do mightily: and
he will bring our enemies to nothing.

<span id="an_108:1">108:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David.

<span id="an_108:2">108:2</span> O God, be not thou silent in thy
praise: for the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful man
is opened against me.

<span id="an_108:3">108:3</span> They have spoken against with deceitful
tongues; and they have compassed me about with words of hatred; and have
fought against me without cause.

<span id="an_108:4">108:4</span> Instead of making me a return of love,
they detracted me: but I gave myself to prayer.

<span id="an_108:5">108:5</span> And they repaid me evil for good: and
hatred for my love.

<span id="an_108:6">108:6</span> Set thou the sinner over him: and may
the devil stand at his right hand.

<span id="an_108:7">108:7</span> When he is judged, may he go out
condemned; and may his prayer be turned to sin.

<span id="an_108:8">108:8</span> May his days be few: and his bishopric
let another take.

<span id="an_108:9">108:9</span> May his children be fatherless, and his
wife a widow.

<span id="an_108:10">108:10</span> Let his children be carried about
vagabonds, and beg; and let them be cast out of their dwellings.

<span id="an_108:11">108:11</span> May the userer search all his
substance: and let strangers plunder his labours.

<span id="an_108:12">108:12</span> May there be none to help him: nor
none to pity his fatherless offspring.

<span id="an_108:13">108:13</span> May his posterity be cut off; in one
generation may his name be blotted out.

<span id="an_108:14">108:14</span> May the iniquity of his fathers be
remembered in the sight of the Lord: and let not the sin of his mother
be blotted out.

<span id="an_108:15">108:15</span> May they be before the lord
continually, and let the memory of them perish from the earth:

<span id="an_108:16">108:16</span> because he remembered not to show
mercy,

<span id="an_108:17">108:17</span> But persecuted the poor man and the
beggar; and the broken in heart, to put him to death.

<span id="an_108:18">108:18</span> And he loved cursing, and it shall
come unto him: and he would not have blessing, and it shall be far from
him. And he put on cursing, like a garment: and it went in like water
into his entrails, and like oil in his bones.

<span id="an_108:19">108:19</span> May it be unto him like a garment
which covereth him; and like a girdle with which he is girded
continually.

<span id="an_108:20">108:20</span> This is the work of them who detract
me before the Lord; and who speak evils against my soul.

<span id="an_108:21">108:21</span> But thou, O Lord, do with for thy
names sake: because thy mercy is sweet. Do thou deliver me.

<span id="an_108:22">108:22</span> for I am poor and needy, and my heart
is troubled within me.

<span id="an_108:23">108:23</span> I am taken away like the shadow when
it declineth: and I am shaken off as locusts.

<span id="an_108:24">108:24</span> My knees are weakened through
fasting: and my flesh is changed for oil.

<span id="an_108:25">108:25</span> And I am become a reproach to them:
they saw me and they shaked their heads,

<span id="an_108:26">108:26</span> Help me, O Lord my God; save me
according to thy mercy.

<span id="an_108:27">108:27</span> And let them know that this is thy
hand: and that thou, O Lord, hast done it.

<span id="an_108:28">108:28</span> They will curse and thou will bless:
let them that rise up against me be confounded: but thy servant shall
rejoice.

<span id="an_108:29">108:29</span> Let them that detract me be clothed
with shame: and let them be covered with the their confusion as with a
double cloak.

<span id="an_108:30">108:30</span> I will give great thanks to the Lord
with my mouth: and in the midst of many I will praise him.

<span id="an_108:31">108:31</span> Because he hath stood at the right
hand of the poor, to save my soul from persecutors

<span id="an_109:1">109:1</span> The Lord said to my Lord: Sit thou at
my right hand: Until I make thy enemies thy footstool.

<span id="an_109:2">109:2</span> The Lord will send forth the sceptre of
thy power out of Sion: rule thou in the midst of thy enemies.

<span id="an_109:3">109:3</span> With thee is the principality in the
day of thy strength: in the brightness of the saints: from the womb
before the day star I begot thee.

<span id="an_109:4">109:4</span> The Lord hath sworn, and he will not
repent: Thou art a priest for ever according to the order of
Melchisedech.

<span id="an_109:5">109:5</span> The Lord at thy right hand hath broken
kings in the day of his wrath.

<span id="an_109:6">109:6</span> He shall judge among nations, he shall
fill ruins: he shall crush the heads in the land of the many.

<span id="an_109:7">109:7</span> He shall drink of the torrent in the
way: therefore shall he lift up the head.

<span id="an_110:1">110:1</span> I will praise thee, O Lord, with my
whole heart; in the council of the just: and in the congregation.

<span id="an_110:2">110:2</span> Great are the works of the Lord: sought
out according to all his wills

<span id="an_110:3">110:3</span> His work is praise and magnificence:
and his justice continueth for ever and ever.

<span id="an_110:4">110:4</span> He hath made a remembrance of his
wonderful works, being a merciful and gracious Lord:

<span id="an_110:5">110:5</span> he hath given food to them that fear
him. He will be mindful for ever of his covenant:

<span id="an_110:6">110:6</span> he will shew forth to his people the
power of his works.

<span id="an_110:7">110:7</span> That he may give them the inheritance
of the Gentiles: the works of his hands are truth and judgment.

<span id="an_110:8">110:8</span> All his commandments are faithful:
confirmed for ever and ever, made in truth and equity.

<span id="an_110:9">110:9</span> He hath sent redemption to his people:
he hath commanded his covenant for ever. Holy and terrible is his name:

<span id="an_110:10">110:10</span> the fear of the Lord is the beginning
of wisdom. A good understanding to all that do it: his praise continueth
for ever and ever.

<span id="an_111:1">111:1</span> Blessed is the man that feareth the
Lord: he shall delight exceedingly in his commandments.

<span id="an_111:2">111:2</span> His seed shall be mighty upon earth:
the generation of the righteous shall be blessed.

<span id="an_111:3">111:3</span> Glory and wealth shall be in his house:
and his justice remaineth for ever and ever.

<span id="an_111:4">111:4</span> To the righteous a light is risen up in
darkness: he is merciful, and compassionate and just.

<span id="an_111:5">111:5</span> Acceptable is the man that showeth
mercy and lendeth: he shall order his words with judgment:

<span id="an_111:6">111:6</span> because he shall not be moved for ever.

<span id="an_111:7">111:7</span> The just shall be in everlasting
remembrance: he shall not hear the evil hearing. His heart is ready to
hope in the Lord:

<span id="an_111:8">111:8</span> his heart is strengthened, he shall not
be moved until he look over his enemies.

<span id="an_111:9">111:9</span> He hath distributed, he hath given to
the poor: his justice remaineth for ever and ever: his horn shall be
exalted in glory.

<span id="an_111:10">111:10</span> The wicked shall see, and shall be
angry, he shall gnash with his teeth and pine away: the desire of the
wicked shall perish.

<span id="an_112:1">112:1</span> Praise the Lord, ye children: praise ye
the name of the Lord.

<span id="an_112:2">112:2</span> Blessed be the name of the Lord, from
henceforth now and for ever.

<span id="an_112:3">112:3</span> From the rising of the sun unto the
going down of the same, the name of the Lord is worthy of praise.

<span id="an_112:4">112:4</span> The Lord is high above all nations; and
his glory above the heavens.

<span id="an_112:5">112:5</span> Who is as the Lord our God, who
dwelleth on high:

<span id="an_112:6">112:6</span> and looketh down on the low things in
heaven and in earth?

<span id="an_112:7">112:7</span> Raising up the needy from the earth,
and lifting up the poor out of the dunghill::

<span id="an_112:8">112:8</span> That he may place him with princes,
with the princes of his people.

<span id="an_112:9">112:9</span> Who maketh a barren woman to dwell in a
house, the joyful mother of children.

<span id="an_113:1">113:1</span> When Israel went out of Egypt, the
house of Jacob from a barbarous people:

<span id="an_113:2">113:2</span> Judea made his sanctuary, Israel his
dominion.

<span id="an_113:3">113:3</span> The sea saw and fled: Jordan was turned
back.

<span id="an_113:4">113:4</span> The mountains skipped like rams, and
the hills like the lambs of the flock.

<span id="an_113:5">113:5</span> What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou
didst flee: and thou, O Jordan, that thou wast turned back?

<span id="an_113:6">113:6</span> Ye mountains, that ye skipped like
rams, and ye hills, like lambs of the flock?

<span id="an_113:7">113:7</span> At the presence of the Lord the earth
was moved, at the presence of the God of Jacob:

<span id="an_113:8">113:8</span> Who turned the rock into pools of
water, and the stony hill into fountains of waters.

<span id="an_113:9">113:9</span> Not to us, O Lord, not to us; but to
thy name give glory.

<span id="an_113:10">113:10</span> For thy mercy, and for thy truth's
sake: lest the gentiles should say: Where is their God?

<span id="an_113:11">113:11</span> But our God is in heaven: he hath
done all things whatsoever he would.

<span id="an_113:12">113:12</span> The idols of the gentiles are silver
and gold, the works of the hands of men.

<span id="an_113:13">113:13</span> They have mouths and speak not: they
have eyes and see not.

<span id="an_113:14">113:14</span> They have ears and hear not: they
have noses and smell not.

<span id="an_113:15">113:15</span> They have hands and feel not: they
have feet and walk not: neither shall they cry out through their throat.

<span id="an_113:16">113:16</span> Let them that make them become like
unto them: and all such as trust in them.

<span id="an_113:17">113:17</span> The house of Israel hath hoped in the
Lord: he is their helper and their protector.

<span id="an_113:18">113:18</span> The house of Aaron hath hoped in the
Lord: he is their helper and their protector.

<span id="an_113:19">113:19</span> They that fear the Lord hath hoped in
the Lord: he is their helper and their protector.

<span id="an_113:20">113:20</span> The Lord hath been mindful of us, and
hath blessed us. He hath blessed the house of Israel: he hath blessed
the house of Aaron.

<span id="an_113:21">113:21</span> He hath blessed all that fear the
Lord, both little and great.

<span id="an_113:22">113:22</span> May the Lord add blessings upon you:
upon you, and upon your children.

<span id="an_113:23">113:23</span> Blessed be you of the Lord, who made
heaven and earth.

<span id="an_113:24">113:24</span> The heaven of heaven is the Lord's:
but the earth he has given to the children of men.

<span id="an_113:25">113:25</span> The dead shall not praise thee, O
Lord: nor any of them that go down to hell.

<span id="an_113:26">113:26</span> But we that live bless the Lord: from
this time now and for ever.

<span id="an_114:1">114:1</span> I have loved, because the Lord will
hear the voice of my prayer.

<span id="an_114:2">114:2</span> Because he hath inclined his ear unto
me: and in my days I will call upon him.

<span id="an_114:3">114:3</span> The sorrows of death have encompassed
me: and the perils of hell have found me. I met with trouble and sorrow:

<span id="an_114:4">114:4</span> and I called upon the name of the Lord.
O Lord, deliver my soul.

<span id="an_114:5">114:5</span> The Lord is merciful and just, and our
God sheweth mercy.

<span id="an_114:6">114:6</span> The Lord is the keeper of little ones:
I was little and he delivered me.

<span id="an_114:7">114:7</span> Turn, O my soul, into thy rest: for the
Lord hath been bountiful to thee.

<span id="an_114:8">114:8</span> For he hath delivered my soul from
death: my eyes from tears, my feet from falling.

<span id="an_114:9">114:9</span> I will please the Lord in the land of
the living.

<span id="an_115:10">115:10</span> I have believed, therefore have I
spoken; but I have been humbled exceedingly.

<span id="an_115:11">115:11</span> I said in my excess: Every man is a
liar.

<span id="an_115:12">115:12</span> What shall I render to the Lord, for
all the things he hath rendered unto me?

<span id="an_115:13">115:13</span> I will take the chalice of salvation;
and I will call upon the name of the Lord.

<span id="an_115:14">115:14</span> I will pay my vows to the Lord before
all his people:

<span id="an_115:15">115:15</span> precious in the sight of the Lord is
the death of his saints.

<span id="an_115:16">115:16</span> O Lord, for I am thy servant: I am
thy servant, and the son of thy handmaid. Thou hast broken my bonds:

<span id="an_115:17">115:17</span> I will sacrifice to thee the
sacrifice of praise, and I will call upon the name of the Lord.

<span id="an_115:18">115:18</span> I will pay my vows to the Lord in the
sight of all his people:

<span id="an_115:19">115:19</span> in the courts of the house of the
Lord, in the midst of thee, O Jerusalem.

<span id="an_116:1">116:1</span> O praise the Lord, all ye nations:
praise him, all ye people.

<span id="an_116:2">116:2</span> For his mercy is confirmed upon us: and
the truth of the Lord remaineth for ever.

<span id="an_117:1">117:1</span> Give praise to Lord, for he is good:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_117:2">117:2</span> Let Israel now say that he is good:
that his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_117:3">117:3</span> Let the house of Aaron now say, that
his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_117:4">117:4</span> Let them that fear the Lord now say,
that his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_117:5">117:5</span> In my trouble I called upon the Lord:
and the Lord heard me, and enlarged me.

<span id="an_117:6">117:6</span> The Lord is my helper, I will not fear
what man can do unto me.

<span id="an_117:7">117:7</span> The Lord is my helper: and I will look
over my enemies.

<span id="an_117:8">117:8</span> It is good to confide in the Lord,
rather than to have confidence in man.

<span id="an_117:9">117:9</span> It is good to trust in the Lord, rather
than to trust in princes.

<span id="an_117:10">117:10</span> All nations compassed me about; and
in the name of the Lord I have been revenged on them.

<span id="an_117:11">117:11</span> Surrounding me they compassed me
about: and in the name of the Lord I have been revenged on them.

<span id="an_117:12">117:12</span> They surrounded me like bees, and
they burned like fire among thorns: and in the name of the Lord I was
revenged on them

<span id="an_117:13">117:13</span> Being pushed I was overturned that I
might fall: but the Lord supported me.

<span id="an_117:14">117:14</span> The Lord is my strength and my
praise: and he is become my salvation.

<span id="an_117:15">117:15</span> The voice of rejoicing and of
salvation is in the tabernacles of the just.

<span id="an_117:16">117:16</span> The right hand of the Lord hath
wrought strength: the right hand of the Lord hath exulted me: the right
hand of the Lord hath wrought strength.

<span id="an_117:17">117:17</span> I shall not die, but live: and shall
declare the works of the Lord.

<span id="an_117:18">117:18</span> The Lord chastising hath chastised
me: but he hath not delivered me over to death.

<span id="an_117:19">117:19</span> Open ye to me the gates of justice: I
will go into them, and give praise to the Lord.

<span id="an_117:20">117:20</span> This is the gate of the Lord, the
just shall enter into it.

<span id="an_117:21">117:21</span> I will give glory to thee because
thou hast heard me: and art become my salvation.

<span id="an_117:22">117:22</span> The stone which the builders
rejected; the same is become the head of the corner.

<span id="an_117:23">117:23</span> This is the Lord's doing: and it is
wonderful in our eyes.

<span id="an_117:24">117:24</span> This is the day which the Lord hath
made: let us be glad and rejoice therein.

<span id="an_117:25">117:25</span> O Lord, save me: O Lord, give good
success.

<span id="an_117:26">117:26</span> Blessed be he that cometh in the name
Lord. We have blessed you out of the house of the Lord.

<span id="an_117:27">117:27</span> The Lord is God, and he hath shone
upon us. Appoint a solemn day, with shady boughs, even to the horn of
the alter.

<span id="an_117:28">117:28</span> Thou art my God, and I will praise
thee: thou art my God, and I will exalt thee. I will praise thee,
because thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation.

<span id="an_117:29">117:29</span> O praise ye the Lord, for he is good:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_118:1">118:1</span> \[ALEPH\] Blessed are the undefiled in
the way, who walk in the law of the Lord.

<span id="an_118:2">118:2</span> Blessed are they who search his
testimonies: that seek him with their whole heart.

<span id="an_118:3">118:3</span> For they that work iniquity, have not
walked in his ways.

<span id="an_118:4">118:4</span> Thou hast commanded thy commandments to
be kept most diligently.

<span id="an_118:5">118:5</span> O! that my ways may be directed to keep
thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:6">118:6</span> Then shall I not be confounded, when I
shall look into all thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:7">118:7</span> I will praise thee with uprightness of
heart, when I shall have learned the judgments of thy justice.

<span id="an_118:8">118:8</span> I will keep thy justifications: O! do
not thou utterly forsake me.

<span id="an_118:9">118:9</span> \[BETH\] By what doth a young man
correct his way? by observing thy words.

<span id="an_118:10">118:10</span> With my whole heart have I sought
after thee: let me not stray from thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:11">118:11</span> Thy words have I hidden in my heart,
that I may not sin against thee.

<span id="an_118:12">118:12</span> Blessed art thou, O Lord: teach me
thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:13">118:13</span> With my lips I have pronounced all
the judgments of thy mouth.

<span id="an_118:14">118:14</span> I have been delighted in the way of
thy testimonies, as in all riches.

<span id="an_118:15">118:15</span> I will meditate on thy commandments:
and I will consider thy ways.

<span id="an_118:16">118:16</span> I will think of thy justifications: I
will not forget thy words.

<span id="an_118:17">118:17</span> \[GIMEL\] Give bountifully to thy
servant, enliven me: and I shall keep thy words.

<span id="an_118:18">118:18</span> Open thou my eyes: and I will
consider the wondrous things of thy law.

<span id="an_118:19">118:19</span> I am a sojourner on the earth: hide
not thy commandments from me.

<span id="an_118:20">118:20</span> My soul hath coveted to long for thy
justifications, at all times.

<span id="an_118:21">118:21</span> Thou hast rebuked the proud: they are
cursed who decline from thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:22">118:22</span> Remove from reproach and contempt:
because I have sought after thy testimonies.

<span id="an_118:23">118:23</span> For princes sat, and spoke against
me: but thy servant was employed in thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:24">118:24</span> For thy testimonies are my
meditation: and thy justifications my counsel.

<span id="an_118:25">118:25</span> \[DALETH\] My soul hath cleaved to
the pavement: quicken thou me according to thy word.

<span id="an_118:26">118:26</span> I have declared my ways, and thou
hast heard me: tech me thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:27">118:27</span> Make me to understand the way of thy
justifications: and I shall be exercised in thy wondrous works.

<span id="an_118:28">118:28</span> My soul hath slumbered through
heaviness: strengthen thou me in thy words.

<span id="an_118:29">118:29</span> Remove from me the way of iniquity:
and out of thy law have mercy on me.

<span id="an_118:30">118:30</span> I have chosen the way of truth: thy
judgments I have not forgotten.

<span id="an_118:31">118:31</span> I have stuck to thy testimonies, O
Lord: put me not to shame.

<span id="an_118:32">118:32</span> I have run the way of thy
commandments, when thou didst enlarge my heart.

<span id="an_118:33">118:33</span> \[HE\] Set before me for a law the
way of thy justifications, O Lord: and I will always seek after it.

<span id="an_118:34">118:34</span> Give me understanding, and I will
search thy law ; and I will keep it with my whole heart.

<span id="an_118:35">118:35</span> Lead me into the path of thy
commandments; for this same I have desired.

<span id="an_118:36">118:36</span> Incline my heart into thy testimonies
and not to covetousness.

<span id="an_118:37">118:37</span> Turn away my eyes that they may not
behold vanity: quicken me in thy way.

<span id="an_118:38">118:38</span> Establish thy word to thy servant, in
thy fear.

<span id="an_118:39">118:39</span> Turn away my reproach, which I have
apprehended: for thy judgments are delightful.

<span id="an_118:40">118:40</span> Behold I have longed after thy
precepts: quicken me in thy justice.

<span id="an_118:41">118:41</span> \[VAU\] Let thy mercy also come upon
me, O Lord: thy salvation according to thy word.

<span id="an_118:42">118:42</span> So shall I answer them that reproach
me in any thing; that I have trusted in thy words.

<span id="an_118:43">118:43</span> And take not thou the word of truth
utterly out of my mouth: for in thy words have I hoped exceedingly.

<span id="an_118:44">118:44</span> So shall I always keep thy law, for
ever and ever.

<span id="an_118:45">118:45</span> And I walked at large: because I have
sought after thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:46">118:46</span> And I spoke of thy testimonies before
kings: and I was not ashamed.

<span id="an_118:47">118:47</span> I meditated also on thy commandments,
which I loved.

<span id="an_118:48">118:48</span> And I lifted up my hands to thy
commandments, which I loved: and I was exercised in thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:49">118:49</span> \[ZAIN\] Be thou mindful of thy word
to thy servant, in which thou hast given me hope.

<span id="an_118:50">118:50</span> This hath comforted me in my
humiliation: because thy word hath enlivened me.

<span id="an_118:51">118:51</span> The proud did iniquitously
altogether: but I declined not from thy law.

<span id="an_118:52">118:52</span> I remembered, O Lord, thy judgments
of old: and I was comforted.

<span id="an_118:53">118:53</span> A fainting hath taken hold of me,
because of the wicked that forsake thy law.

<span id="an_118:54">118:54</span> Thy justifications were the subject
of my song, in the place of my pilgrimage.

<span id="an_118:55">118:55</span> In the night I have remembered thy
name, O Lord: and have kept thy law.

<span id="an_118:56">118:56</span> This happened to me: because I sought
after thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:57">118:57</span> \[HETH\] O Lord, my portion, I have
said, I would keep the law.

<span id="an_118:58">118:58</span> I entreated thy face with all my
heart: have mercy on me according to thy word.

<span id="an_118:59">118:59</span> I have thought on my ways: and turned
my feet unto thy testimonies.

<span id="an_118:60">118:60</span> I am ready, and am not troubled: that
I may keep thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:61">118:61</span> The cords of the wicked have
encompassed me: but I have not forgotten thy law.

<span id="an_118:62">118:62</span> I rose at midnight to give praise to
thee; for the judgments of thy justification.

<span id="an_118:63">118:63</span> I am a partaker with all them that
fear thee, and that keep thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:64">118:64</span> The earth, O Lord, is full of thy
mercy: teach me thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:65">118:65</span> \[TETH\] Thou hast done well with thy
servant, O Lord, according to thy word.

<span id="an_118:66">118:66</span> Teach me goodness and discipline and
knowledge; for I have believed thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:67">118:67</span> Before I was humbled I offended;
therefore have I kept thy word.

<span id="an_118:68">118:68</span> Thou art good; and in thy goodness
teach me thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:69">118:69</span> The iniquity of the proud hath been
multiplied over me: but I will seek thy commandments with my whole
heart.

<span id="an_118:70">118:70</span> Their heart is curdled like milk: but
I have meditated on thy law.

<span id="an_118:71">118:71</span> It is good for me that thou hast
humbled me, that I may learn thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:72">118:72</span> The law of thy mouth is good to me,
above thousands of gold and silver.

<span id="an_118:73">118:73</span> \[JOD\] Thy hands have made me and
formed me: give me understanding, and I will learn thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:74">118:74</span> They that fear thee shall see me, and
shall be glad: because I have greatly hoped in thy words.

<span id="an_118:75">118:75</span> I know, O Lord, that thy judgments
are equity: and in thy truth thou hast humbled me.

<span id="an_118:76">118:76</span> O! let thy mercy be for my comfort,
according to thy word unto thy servant.

<span id="an_118:77">118:77</span> Let thy tender mercies come unto me,
and I shall live: for thy law is my meditation.

<span id="an_118:78">118:78</span> Let the proud be ashamed, because
they have done unjustly towards me: but I will be employed in thy
commandments.

<span id="an_118:79">118:79</span> Let them that fear thee turn to me"
and they that know thy testimonies.

<span id="an_118:80">118:80</span> Let my heart be undefiled in thy
justifications, that I may not be confounded.

<span id="an_118:81">118:81</span> \[CAPH\] My soul hath fainted after
thy salvation: and in thy word I have very much hoped.

<span id="an_118:82">118:82</span> My eyes have failed for thy word,
saying: When wilt thou comfort me?

<span id="an_118:83">118:83</span> For I am become like a bottle in the
frost: I have not forgotten thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:84">118:84</span> How many are the days of thy servant:
when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me?

<span id="an_118:85">118:85</span> The wicked have told me fables: but
not as thy law.

<span id="an_118:86">118:86</span> All thy statutes are truth: they have
persecuted me unjustly, do thou help me.

<span id="an_118:87">118:87</span> They had almost made an end of me
upon earth: but I have not forsaken thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:88">118:88</span> Quicken thou me according to thy
mercy: and I shall keep the testimonies of thy mouth.

<span id="an_118:89">118:89</span> \[LAMED\] For ever, O Lord, thy word
standeth firm in heaven.

<span id="an_118:90">118:90</span> Thy truth unto all generations: thou
hast founded the earth, and it continueth.

<span id="an_118:91">118:91</span> By thy ordinance the day goeth on:
for all things serve thee.

<span id="an_118:92">118:92</span> Unless thy law had been my
meditation, I had then perhaps perished in my abjection.

<span id="an_118:93">118:93</span> Thy justifications I will never
forget: for by them thou hast given me life.

<span id="an_118:94">118:94</span> I am thine, save thou me: for I have
sought thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:95">118:95</span> The wicked have waited for me to
destroy me: but I have understood thy testimonies.

<span id="an_118:96">118:96</span> I have seen an end to all
persecution: thy commandment is exceeding broad.

<span id="an_118:97">118:97</span> \[MEM\] O how have I loved thy law, O
Lord! it is my meditation all the day.

<span id="an_118:98">118:98</span> Through thy commandment, thou hast
made me wiser than my enemies: for it is ever with me.

<span id="an_118:99">118:99</span> I have understood more than all my
teachers: because thy testimonies are my meditation.

<span id="an_118:100">118:100</span> I have had understanding above
ancients: because I have sought thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:101">118:101</span> I have restrained my feet from
every evil way: that I may keep thy words.

<span id="an_118:102">118:102</span> I have not declined from thy
judgments, because thou hast set me a law.

<span id="an_118:103">118:103</span> How sweet are thy words to my
palate! more than honey to my mouth.

<span id="an_118:104">118:104</span> By thy commandments I have had
understanding: therefore have I hated every way of iniquity.

<span id="an_118:105">118:105</span> \[NUN\] Thy word is a lamp to my
feet, and a light to my paths.

<span id="an_118:106">118:106</span> I have sworn and am determined to
keep the judgments of thy justice.

<span id="an_118:107">118:107</span> I have been humbled, O Lord,
exceedingly: quicken thou me according to thy word.

<span id="an_118:108">118:108</span> The free offerings of my mouth make
acceptable, O Lord: and teach me thy judgments.

<span id="an_118:109">118:109</span> My soul is continually in my hands:
and I have not forgotten thy law.

<span id="an_118:110">118:110</span> Sinners have laid a snare for me:
but I have not erred from thy precepts.

<span id="an_118:111">118:111</span> I have purchased thy testimonies
for an inheritance for ever: because they are a joy to my heart.

<span id="an_118:112">118:112</span> I have inclined my heart to do thy
justifications for ever, for the reward.

<span id="an_118:113">118:113</span> \[SAMECH\] I have hated the unjust:
and have loved thy law.

<span id="an_118:114">118:114</span> Thou art my helper and my
protector: and in thy word I have greatly hoped.

<span id="an_118:115">118:115</span> Depart from me, ye malignant: and I
will search the commandments of my God.

<span id="an_118:116">118:116</span> Uphold me according to thy word,
and I shall live: and let me not be confounded in my expectation.

<span id="an_118:117">118:117</span> Help me, and I shall be saved: and
I will meditate always on thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:118">118:118</span> Thou hast despised all them that
fall off from thy judgments; for their thought is unjust.

<span id="an_118:119">118:119</span> I have accounted all the sinners of
the earth prevaricators: therefore have I loved thy testimonies.

<span id="an_118:120">118:120</span> Pierce thou my flesh with thy fear:
for I am afraid of thy judgments.

<span id="an_118:121">118:121</span> \[AIN\] I have done judgment and
justice: give me not up to them that slander me.

<span id="an_118:122">118:122</span> Uphold thy servant unto good: let
not the proud calumniate me.

<span id="an_118:123">118:123</span> My eyes have fainted after thy
salvation: and for the word of thy justice.

<span id="an_118:124">118:124</span> Deal with thy servant according to
thy mercy: and teach me thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:125">118:125</span> I am thy servant: give me
understanding that I may know thy testimonies.

<span id="an_118:126">118:126</span> It is time, O Lord, to do: they
have dissipated thy law.

<span id="an_118:127">118:127</span> Therefore have I loved thy
commandments above gold and the topaz.

<span id="an_118:128">118:128</span> Therefore was I directed to all thy
commandments: I have hated all wicked ways.

<span id="an_118:129">118:129</span> \[PHE\] Thy testimonies are
wonderful: therefore my soul hath sought them.

<span id="an_118:130">118:130</span> The declaration of thy words giveth
light: and giveth understanding to little ones.

<span id="an_118:131">118:131</span> I opened my mouth and panted:
because I longed for thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:132">118:132</span> Look thou upon me, and have mercy
on me, according to the judgment of them that love thy name.

<span id="an_118:133">118:133</span> Direct my steps according to thy
word: and let no iniquity have dominion over me.

<span id="an_118:134">118:134</span> Redeem me from the calumnies of
men: that I may keep thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:135">118:135</span> Make thy face to shine upon thy
servant: and teach me thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:136">118:136</span> My eyes have sent forth springs of
water: because they have not kept thy law.

<span id="an_118:137">118:137</span> \[SADE\] Thou art just, O Lord: and
thy judgment is right.

<span id="an_118:138">118:138</span> Thou hast commanded justice thy
testimonies: and thy truth exceedingly.

<span id="an_118:139">118:139</span> My zeal hath made me pine away:
because my enemies forgot thy words.

<span id="an_118:140">118:140</span> Thy word is exceedingly refined:
and thy servant hath loved it.

<span id="an_118:141">118:141</span> I am very young and despised; but I
forgot not thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:142">118:142</span> Thy justice is justice for ever:
and thy law is the truth.

<span id="an_118:143">118:143</span> Trouble and anguish have found me:
thy commandments are my meditation.

<span id="an_118:144">118:144</span> Thy testimonies are justice for
ever: give me understanding, and I shall live.

<span id="an_118:145">118:145</span> \[COPH\] I cried with my whole
heart, hear me, O Lord: I will seek thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:146">118:146</span> I cried unto thee, save me: that I
may keep thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:147">118:147</span> I prevented the dawning of the day,
and cried: because in thy words I very much hoped.

<span id="an_118:148">118:148</span> My eyes to thee have prevented the
morning: that I might meditate on thy words.

<span id="an_118:149">118:149</span> Hear thou my voice, O Lord,
according to thy mercy: and quicken me according to thy mercy.

<span id="an_118:150">118:150</span> They that persecute me have drawn
nigh to iniquity; but they are gone far off from the law.

<span id="an_118:151">118:151</span> Thou art near, O Lord: and all thy
ways are truth.

<span id="an_118:152">118:152</span> I have known from the beginning
concerning thy testimonies: that thou hast founded them for ever.

<span id="an_118:153">118:153</span> \[RES\] See my humiliation and
deliver me: for I have not forgotten the law.

<span id="an_118:154">118:154</span> Judge my judgment and redeem me:
quicken thou me for thy word's sake.

<span id="an_118:155">118:155</span> Salvation is far from sinners;
because they have not sought thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:156">118:156</span> Many, O Lord, are thy mercies:
quicken me according to thy judgment.

<span id="an_118:157">118:157</span> Many are they that persecute me,
and afflict me; but I have not declined from thy testimonies.

<span id="an_118:158">118:158</span> I beheld the transgressors, and I
pined away; because they kept not thy word.

<span id="an_118:159">118:159</span> Behold I have loved thy
commandments, O Lord; quicken me thou in thy mercy.

<span id="an_118:160">118:160</span> The beginning of thy words is
truth: all the judgments of thy justice are for ever.

<span id="an_118:161">118:161</span> \[SIN\] Princes have persecuted me
without cause: and my heart hath been in awe of thy words.

<span id="an_118:162">118:162</span> I will rejoice at thy words, as one
that hath found great spoil.

<span id="an_118:163">118:163</span> I have hated and abhorred iniquity;
but I have loved thy law.

<span id="an_118:164">118:164</span> Seven times a day I have given
praise to thee, for the judgments of thy justice.

<span id="an_118:165">118:165</span> Much peace have they that love thy
law, and to them there is no stumbling block

<span id="an_118:166">118:166</span> I looked to thy salvation, O Lord:
and I loved thy commandments.

<span id="an_118:167">118:167</span> My soul hath kept thy testimonies:
and hath loved them exceedingly.

<span id="an_118:168">118:168</span> I have kept thy commandments and
thy testimonies: because all my ways are in thy sight.

<span id="an_118:169">118:169</span> \[TAU\] Let my supplication, O
Lord, come near in thy sight: give me understanding according to thy
word.

<span id="an_118:170">118:170</span> Let my request come in before thee;
deliver thou me according to thy word.

<span id="an_118:171">118:171</span> My lips shall utter a hymn, when
thou shalt teach me thy justifications.

<span id="an_118:172">118:172</span> My tongue shall pronounce thy word:
because all thy commandments are justice.

<span id="an_118:173">118:173</span> Let thy hand be with me to save me;
for I have chosen thy precepts.

<span id="an_118:174">118:174</span> I have longed for thy salvation, O
Lord; and thy law is my meditation.

<span id="an_118:175">118:175</span> My soul shall live and shall praise
thee: and thy judgments shall help me.

<span id="an_118:176">118:176</span> I have gone astray like a sheep
that is lost: seek thy servant, because I have not forgotten thy
commandments.

<span id="an_119:1">119:1</span> In my trouble I cried to the Lord: and
he heard me.

<span id="an_119:2">119:2</span> O Lord, deliver my soul from wicked
lips, and a deceitful tongue.

<span id="an_119:3">119:3</span> What shall be given to thee, or what
shall be added to thee, to a deceitful tongue.

<span id="an_119:4">119:4</span> The sharp arrows of the mighty, with
coals that lay waste.

<span id="an_119:5">119:5</span> Woe is me, that my sojourning is
prolonged! I have dwelt with the inhabitants of cedar:

<span id="an_119:6">119:6</span> my soul hath been long a sojourner.

<span id="an_119:7">119:7</span> With them that hate peace I was
peaceable: when I spoke to them they fought against me without cause.

<span id="an_120:1">120:1</span> I have lifted up my eyes to the
mountains, from whence help shall come to me.

<span id="an_120:2">120:2</span> My help is from the Lord, who made
heaven and earth.

<span id="an_120:3">120:3</span> May he not suffer thy foot to be moved:
neither let him slumber that keepeth thee.

<span id="an_120:4">120:4</span> Behold he shall neither slumber nor
sleep, that keepeth Israel.

<span id="an_120:5">120:5</span> The Lord is thy keeper, the Lord is thy
protection upon thy right hand.

<span id="an_120:6">120:6</span> The sun shall not burn thee by day: nor
the moon by night.

<span id="an_120:7">120:7</span> The Lord keepeth thee from all evil:
may the Lord keep thy soul.

<span id="an_120:8">120:8</span> May the Lord keep thy going in and thy
going out; from henceforth now and for ever.

<span id="an_121:1">121:1</span> I rejoiced at the things that were said
to me: We shall go into the house of the Lord.

<span id="an_121:2">121:2</span> Our feet were standing in thy courts, O
Jerusalem.

<span id="an_121:3">121:3</span> Jerusalem, which is built as a city,
which is compact together.

<span id="an_121:4">121:4</span> For thither did the tribes go up, the
tribes of the Lord: the testimony of Israel, to praise the name of the
Lord.

<span id="an_121:5">121:5</span> Because their seats have sat in
judgment, seats upon the house of David.

<span id="an_121:6">121:6</span> Pray ye for the things that are for the
peace of Jerusalem: and abundance for them that love thee.

<span id="an_121:7">121:7</span> Let peace be in thy strength: and
abundance in thy towers.

<span id="an_121:8">121:8</span> For the sake of my brethren, and of my
neighbours, I spoke peace of thee.

<span id="an_121:9">121:9</span> Because of the house of the Lord our
God, I have sought good things for thee.

<span id="an_122:1">122:1</span> To thee have I lifted up my eyes, who
dwellest in heaven.

<span id="an_122:2">122:2</span> Behold as the eyes of the servants are
on the hands of their masters, As the eyes of the handmaid are on the
hands of her mistress: so are our eyes unto the Lord our God, until he
have mercy on us.

<span id="an_122:3">122:3</span> Have mercy on us, O Lord, have mercy on
us: for we are greatly filled with contempt.

<span id="an_122:4">122:4</span> For our soul is greatly filled: we are
a reproach to the rich, and contempt to the proud.

<span id="an_123:1">123:1</span> If it had not been that the Lord was
with us, let Israel now say:

<span id="an_123:2">123:2</span> If it had not been that the Lord was
with us, When men rose up against us

<span id="an_123:3">123:3</span> perhaps they had swallowed us up alive.
When their fury was enkindled against us,

<span id="an_123:4">123:4</span> perhaps the waters had swallowed us up.

<span id="an_123:5">123:5</span> Our soul hath passed through a torrent:
perhaps our soul had passed through a water insupportable.

<span id="an_123:6">123:6</span> Blessed be the Lord, who hath not given
us to be a prey to their teeth.

<span id="an_123:7">123:7</span> Our soul hath been delivered as a
sparrow out of the snare of the followers. The snare is broken, and we
are delivered.

<span id="an_123:8">123:8</span> Our help is in the name of the Lord,
who made heaven and earth.

<span id="an_124:1">124:1</span> They that trust in the Lord shall be as
mount Sion: he shall not be moved for ever that dwelleth

<span id="an_124:2">124:2</span> in Jerusalem. Mountains are round about
it: so the Lord is round about his people from henceforth now and for
ever.

<span id="an_124:3">124:3</span> For the Lord will not leave the rod of
sinners upon the lot of the just: that the just may not stretch forth
their hands to iniquity.

<span id="an_124:4">124:4</span> Do good, O Lord, to those that are
good, and to the upright of heart.

<span id="an_124:5">124:5</span> But such as turn aside into bonds, the
Lord shall lead out with the workers of iniquity: peace upon Israel.

<span id="an_125:1">125:1</span> When the lord brought back the
captivity of Sion, we became like men comforted.

<span id="an_125:2">125:2</span> Then was our mouth filled with
gladness; and our tongue with joy. Then shall they say among the
Gentiles: The Lord hath done great things for them.

<span id="an_125:3">125:3</span> The Lord hath done great things for us:
we are become joyful.

<span id="an_125:4">125:4</span> Turn again our captivity, O Lord, as a
stream in the south.

<span id="an_125:5">125:5</span> They that sow in tears shall reap in
joy.

<span id="an_125:6">125:6</span> Going they went and wept, casting their
seeds.

<span id="an_125:7">125:7</span> But coming they shall come with
joyfulness, carrying their sheaves.

<span id="an_126:1">126:1</span> Unless the Lord build the house, they
labour in vain that build it. Unless the Lord keep the city, he watcheth
in vain that keepeth it.

<span id="an_126:2">126:2</span> It is vain for you to rise before
light, rise ye after you have sitten, you that eat the bread of sorrow.
When he shall give sleep to his beloved,

<span id="an_126:3">126:3</span> behold the inheritance of the Lord are
children: the reward, the fruit of the womb.

<span id="an_126:4">126:4</span> As arrows in the hand of the mighty, so
the children of them that have been shaken.

<span id="an_126:5">126:5</span> Blessed is the man that hath filled the
desire with them; he shall not be confounded when he shall speak to his
enemies in the gate.

<span id="an_127:1">127:1</span> Blessed are all they that fear the
Lord: that walk in his ways.

<span id="an_127:2">127:2</span> For thou shalt eat the labours of thy
hands: blessed art thou, and it shall be well with thee.

<span id="an_127:3">127:3</span> Thy wife as a fruitful vine, on the
sides of thy house. Thy children as olive plants, round about thy table.

<span id="an_127:4">127:4</span> Behold, thus shall the man be blessed
that feareth the Lord.

<span id="an_127:5">127:5</span> May the Lord bless thee out of Sion:
and mayest thou see the good things of Jerusalem all the days of thy
life.

<span id="an_127:6">127:6</span> And mayest thou see thy children's
children, peace upon Israel.

<span id="an_128:1">128:1</span> Often have they fought against me from
my youth, let Israel now say.

<span id="an_128:2">128:2</span> Often have they fought against me from
my youth: but they could not prevail over me.

<span id="an_128:3">128:3</span> The wicked have wrought upon my back:
they have lengthened their iniquity.

<span id="an_128:4">128:4</span> The Lord who is just will cut the necks
of sinners:

<span id="an_128:5">128:5</span> let them all be confounded and turned
back that hate Sion.

<span id="an_128:6">128:6</span> Let them be as grass on the tops of
houses: which withered before it be plucked up:

<span id="an_128:7">128:7</span> Wherewith the mower filleth not his
hand: nor he that gathereth sheaves his bosom.

<span id="an_128:8">128:8</span> And they that have passed by have not
said: The blessing of the Lord be upon you: we have blessed you in the
name of the Lord.

<span id="an_129:1">129:1</span> Out of the depths I have cried to thee,
O Lord:

<span id="an_129:2">129:2</span> Lord, hear my voice. Let thy ears be
attentive to the voice of my supplication.

<span id="an_129:3">129:3</span> If thou, O Lord, wilt mark iniquities:
Lord, who shall stand it.

<span id="an_129:4">129:4</span> For with thee there is merciful
forgiveness: and by reason of thy law, I have waited for thee, O Lord.
My soul hath relied on his word:

<span id="an_129:5">129:5</span> my soul hath hoped in the Lord.

<span id="an_129:6">129:6</span> From the morning watch even until
night, let Israel hope in the Lord.

<span id="an_129:7">129:7</span> Because with the Lord there is mercy:
and with him plentiful redemption.

<span id="an_129:8">129:8</span> And he shall redeem Israel from all his
iniquities.

<span id="an_130:1">130:1</span> Lord, my heart is not exalted: nor are
my eyes lofty. Neither have I walked in great matters, nor in wonderful
things above me.

<span id="an_130:2">130:2</span> If I was not humbly minded, but exalted
my soul: As a child that is weaned is towards his mother, so reward in
my soul.

<span id="an_130:3">130:3</span> Let Israel hope in the Lord, from
henceforth now and for ever.

<span id="an_131:1">131:1</span> O Lord, remember David, and all his
meekness.

<span id="an_131:2">131:2</span> How he swore to the Lord, he vowed a
vow to the God of Jacob:

<span id="an_131:3">131:3</span> If I shall enter into the tabernacle of
my house: if I shall go up into the bed wherein I lie:

<span id="an_131:4">131:4</span> If I shall give sleep to my eyes, or
slumber to my eyelids,

<span id="an_131:5">131:5</span> Or rest to my temples: until I find out
a place for the Lord, a tabernacle for the God of Jacob.

<span id="an_131:6">131:6</span> Behold we have heard of it in Ephrata:
we have found it in the fields of the wood.

<span id="an_131:7">131:7</span> We will go into his tabernacle: We will
adore in the place where his feet stood.

<span id="an_131:8">131:8</span> Arise, O Lord, into thy resting place:
thou and the ark, which thou hast sanctified.

<span id="an_131:9">131:9</span> Let thy priests be clothed with
justice: and let thy saints rejoice.

<span id="an_131:10">131:10</span> For thy servant David's sake, turn
not away the face of thy anointed.

<span id="an_131:11">131:11</span> The Lord hath sworn truth to David,
and he will not make it void: of the fruit of thy womb I will set upon
thy throne.

<span id="an_131:12">131:12</span> If thy children will keep thy
covenant, and these my testimonies which I shall teach them: Their
children also for evermore shall sit upon thy throne.

<span id="an_131:13">131:13</span> For the Lord hath chosen Sion: he
hath chosen it for his dwelling.

<span id="an_131:14">131:14</span> This is my rest for ever and ever:
here will I dwell, for I have chosen it.

<span id="an_131:15">131:15</span> Blessing, I will bless her widow: I
will satisfy her poor with bread.

<span id="an_131:16">131:16</span> I will clothe her priests with
salvation: and her saints shall rejoice with exceeding great joy.

<span id="an_131:17">131:17</span> There will I bring forth a horn to
David: I have prepared a lamp for my anointed.

<span id="an_131:18">131:18</span> His enemies I will clothe with
confusion: but upon him will my sanctification flourish.

<span id="an_132:1">132:1</span> Behold how good and how pleasant it is
for brethren to dwell in unity.

<span id="an_132:2">132:2</span> Like the precious ointment on the head,
that ran down upon the beard, the beard of Aaron, Which ran down to the
skirt of his garment:

<span id="an_132:3">132:3</span> as the dew of Hermon, which descendeth
upon mount Sion. For there the Lord hath commandeth blessing, and life
for evermore.

<span id="an_133:1">133:1</span> Behold now bless ye the Lord, all ye
servants of the Lord: Who stand in the house of the Lord, in the courts
of the house of our God.

<span id="an_133:2">133:2</span> In the nights lift up your hands to the
holy places, and bless ye the Lord.

<span id="an_133:3">133:3</span> May the Lord out of Sion bless thee, he
that made heaven and earth.

<span id="an_134:1">134:1</span> Praise ye the name of the Lord: O you
his servants, praise the Lord:

<span id="an_134:2">134:2</span> You that stand in the house of the
Lord, in the courts of the house of our God.

<span id="an_134:3">134:3</span> Praise ye the Lord, for the Lord is
good: sing ye to his name, for it is sweet.

<span id="an_134:4">134:4</span> For the Lord hath chosen Jacob unto
himself: Israel for his own possession.

<span id="an_134:5">134:5</span> For I have known that the Lord is
great, and our God is above all gods.

<span id="an_134:6">134:6</span> Whatsoever the Lord hath pleased he
hath done, in heaven, in earth, in the sea, and in all the deeps.

<span id="an_134:7">134:7</span> He bringeth up clouds from the end of
the earth: he hath made lightnings for the rain. He bringeth forth winds
out of his stores:

<span id="an_134:8">134:8</span> He slew the firstborn of Egypt from man
even unto beast.

<span id="an_134:9">134:9</span> He sent forth signs and wonders in the
midst of thee, O Egypt: upon Pharao, and upon all his servants.

<span id="an_134:10">134:10</span> He smote many nations, and slew
mighty kings:

<span id="an_134:11">134:11</span> Sehon king of the Amorrhites, and Og
king of Basan, and all the kingdoms of Chanaan.

<span id="an_134:12">134:12</span> And gave their land for an
inheritance, for an inheritance to his people Israel.

<span id="an_134:13">134:13</span> Thy name, O Lord, is for ever: thy
memorial, O Lord, unto all generations.

<span id="an_134:14">134:14</span> For the Lord will judge his people,
and will be entreated in favour of his servants.

<span id="an_134:15">134:15</span> The idols of the Gentiles are silver
and gold, the works of men's hands.

<span id="an_134:16">134:16</span> They have a mouth, but they speak
not: they have eyes, but they see not.

<span id="an_134:17">134:17</span> They have ears, but they hear not:
neither is there any breath in their mouths.

<span id="an_134:18">134:18</span> Let them that make them be like to
them: and every one that trusteth in them.

<span id="an_134:19">134:19</span> Bless the Lord, O house of Israel:
bless the Lord, O house of Aaron.

<span id="an_134:20">134:20</span> Bless the Lord, O house of Levi: you
that fear the Lord, bless the Lord.

<span id="an_134:21">134:21</span> Blessed be the Lord out of Sion, who
dwelleth in Jerusalem.

<span id="an_135:1">135:1</span> Praise the Lord, for he is good: for
his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:2">135:2</span> Praise ye the God of gods: for his
mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:3">135:3</span> Praise ye the Lord of lords: for his
mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:4">135:4</span> Who alone doth great wonders: for his
mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:5">135:5</span> Who made the heavens in understanding:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:6">135:6</span> Who established the earth above the
waters: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:7">135:7</span> Who made the great lights: for his
mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:8">135:8</span> The sun to rule over the day: for his
mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:9">135:9</span> The moon and the stars to rule the
night: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:10">135:10</span> Who smote Egypt with their firstborn:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:11">135:11</span> Who brought Israel from among them:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:12">135:12</span> With a mighty hand and a stretched
out arm: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:13">135:13</span> Who divided the Red Sea into parts:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:14">135:14</span> And brought out Israel through the
midst thereof: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:15">135:15</span> And overthrew Pharao and his host in
the Red Sea: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:16">135:16</span> Who led his people through the
desert: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:17">135:17</span> Who smote great kings: for his mercy
endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:18">135:18</span> And slew strong kings: for his mercy
endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:19">135:19</span> Sehon king of the Amorrhites: for his
mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:20">135:20</span> And Og king of Basan: for his mercy
endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:21">135:21</span> And he gave their land for an
inheritance: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:22">135:22</span> For an inheritance to his servant
Israel: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:23">135:23</span> For he was mindful of us in our
affliction: for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:24">135:24</span> And he redeemed us from our enemies:
for his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:25">135:25</span> Who giveth food to all flesh: for his
mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:26">135:26</span> Give glory to the God of heaven: for
his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_135:27">135:27</span> Give glory to the Lord of lords: for
his mercy endureth for ever.

<span id="an_136:1">136:1</span> Upon the rivers of Babylon, there we
sat and wept: when we remembered Sion:

<span id="an_136:2">136:2</span> On the willows in the midst thereof we
hung up our instruments.

<span id="an_136:3">136:3</span> For there they that led us into
captivity required of us the words of songs. And they that carried us
away, said: Sing ye to us a hymn of the songs of Sion.

<span id="an_136:4">136:4</span> How shall we sing the song of the Lord
in a strange land?

<span id="an_136:5">136:5</span> If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my
right hand be forgotten.

<span id="an_136:6">136:6</span> Let my tongue cleave to my jaws, if I
do not remember thee: If I make not Jerusalem the beginning of my joy.

<span id="an_136:7">136:7</span> Remember, O Lord, the children of Edom,
in the day of Jerusalem: Who say: Rase it, rase it, even to the
foundation thereof.

<span id="an_136:8">136:8</span> O daughter of Babylon, miserable:
blessed shall he be who shall repay thee thy payment which thou hast
paid us.

<span id="an_136:9">136:9</span> Blessed be he that shall take and dash
thy little ones against the rock.

<span id="an_137:1">137:1</span> I will praise thee, O lord, with my
whole heart: for thou hast heard the words of my mouth. I will sing
praise to thee in the sight of his angels:

<span id="an_137:2">137:2</span> I will worship towards thy holy temple,
and I will give glory to thy name. For thy mercy, and for thy truth: for
thou hast magnified thy holy name above all.

<span id="an_137:3">137:3</span> In what day soever I shall call upon
thee, hear me: thou shall multiply strength in my soul.

<span id="an_137:4">137:4</span> May all the kings of the earth give
glory to thee: for they have heard all the words of thy mouth.

<span id="an_137:5">137:5</span> And let them sing in the ways of the
Lord: for great is the glory of the Lord.

<span id="an_137:6">137:6</span> For the Lord is high, and looketh on
the low: and the high he knoweth afar off.

<span id="an_137:7">137:7</span> If I shall walk in the midst of
tribulation, thou wilt quicken me: and thou hast stretched forth thy
hand against the wrath of my enemies: and thy right hand hath saved me.

<span id="an_137:8">137:8</span> The Lord will repay for me: thy mercy,
O Lord, endureth for ever: O despise not the work of thy hands.

<span id="an_138:1">138:1</span> Lord, thou hast proved me, and known
me:

<span id="an_138:2">138:2</span> thou hast know my sitting down, and my
rising up.

<span id="an_138:3">138:3</span> Thou hast understood my thoughts afar
off: my path and my line thou hast searched out.

<span id="an_138:4">138:4</span> And thou hast foreseen all my ways: for
there is no speech in my tongue.

<span id="an_138:5">138:5</span> Behold, O Lord, thou hast known all
things, the last and those of old: thou hast formed me, and hast laid
thy hand upon me.

<span id="an_138:6">138:6</span> Thy knowledge is become wonderful to
me: it is high, and I cannot reach to it.

<span id="an_138:7">138:7</span> Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or
whither shall I flee from thy face?

<span id="an_138:8">138:8</span> If I ascend into heaven, thou art
there: if I descend into hell, thou art present.

<span id="an_138:9">138:9</span> If I take my wings early in the
morning, and dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea:

<span id="an_138:10">138:10</span> Even there also shall thy hand lead
me: and thy right hand shall hold me.

<span id="an_138:11">138:11</span> And I said: Perhaps darkness shall
cover me: and night shall be my light in my pleasures.

<span id="an_138:12">138:12</span> But darkness shall not be dark to
thee, and night shall be light as day: the darkness thereof, and the
light thereof are alike to thee.

<span id="an_138:13">138:13</span> For thou hast possessed my reins:
thou hast protected me from my mother's womb.

<span id="an_138:14">138:14</span> I will praise thee, for thou art
fearfully magnified: wonderful are thy works, and my soul knoweth right
well.

<span id="an_138:15">138:15</span> My bone is not hidden from thee,
which thou hast made in secret: and my substance in the lower parts of
the earth.

<span id="an_138:16">138:16</span> Thy eyes did see my imperfect being,
and in thy book all shall be written: days shall be formed, and no one
in them.

<span id="an_138:17">138:17</span> But to me thy friends, O God, are
made exceedingly honourable: their principality is exceedingly
strengthened.

<span id="an_138:18">138:18</span> I will number them, and they shall be
multiplied above the sand: I rose up and am still with thee.

<span id="an_138:19">138:19</span> If thou wilt kill the wicked, O God:
ye men of blood, depart from me:

<span id="an_138:20">138:20</span> Because you say in thought: They
shall receive thy cities in vain.

<span id="an_138:21">138:21</span> Have I not hated them, O Lord, that
hated thee: and pine away because of thy enemies?

<span id="an_138:22">138:22</span> I have hated them with a perfect
hatred: and they are become enemies to me.

<span id="an_138:23">138:23</span> Prove me, O God, and know my heart:
examine me, and know my paths.

<span id="an_138:24">138:24</span> And see if there be in me the way of
iniquity: and lead me in the eternal way.

<span id="an_139:1">139:1</span> Unto the end, a psalm for David.

<span id="an_139:2">139:2</span> Deliver me, O Lord, from the evil man:
rescue me from the unjust man.

<span id="an_139:3">139:3</span> Who have devised iniquities in their
hearts: all the day long they designed battles.

<span id="an_139:4">139:4</span> They have sharpened their tongues like
a serpent: the venom of saps is under their lips.

<span id="an_139:5">139:5</span> Keep me, O Lord, from the hand of the
wicked: and from unjust men deliver me. Who have proposed to supplant my
steps.

<span id="an_139:6">139:6</span> the proud have hidden a net for me. And
they have stretched out cords for a snare: they have laid for me a
stumblingblock by the wayside.

<span id="an_139:7">139:7</span> I said to the Lord: Thou art my God:
hear, O Lord, the voice of my supplication.

<span id="an_139:8">139:8</span> O Lord, Lord, the strength of my
salvation: thou hast overshadowed my head in the day of battle.

<span id="an_139:9">139:9</span> Give me not up, O Lord, from my desire
to the wicked: they have plotted against me; do not thou forsake me,
lest they should triumph.

<span id="an_139:10">139:10</span> The head of them compassing me about:
the labour of their lips shall overwhelm them.

<span id="an_139:11">139:11</span> Burning coals shall fall upon them;
thou wilt cast them down into the fire: in miseries they shall not be
able to stand.

<span id="an_139:12">139:12</span> A man full of tongue shall not be
established in the earth: evil shall catch the unjust man unto
destruction.

<span id="an_139:13">139:13</span> I know that the Lord will do justice
to the needy, and will revenge the poor.

<span id="an_139:14">139:14</span> But as for the just, they shall give
glory to thy name: and the upright shall dwell with thy countenance.

<span id="an_140:1">140:1</span> I have cried to the, O Lord, hear me:
hearken to my voice, when I cry to thee.

<span id="an_140:2">140:2</span> Let my prayer be directed as incense in
thy sight; the lifting up of my hands, as evening sacrifice.

<span id="an_140:3">140:3</span> Set a watch, O Lord, before my mouth:
and a door round about my lips.

<span id="an_140:4">140:4</span> Incline not my heart to evil words; to
make excuses in sins. With men that work iniquity: and I will not
communicate with the choicest of them.

<span id="an_140:5">140:5</span> The just shall correct me in mercy, and
shall reprove me: but let not the oil of the sinner fatten my head. For
my prayer also shall still be against the things with which they are
well pleased:

<span id="an_140:6">140:6</span> their judges falling upon the rock have
been swallowed up. They shall hear my words, for they have prevailed:

<span id="an_140:7">140:7</span> as when the thickness of the earth is
broken up upon the ground: Our bones are scattered by the side of hell.

<span id="an_140:8">140:8</span> But o to thee, O Lord, Lord, are my
eyes: in thee have I put my trust, take not away my soul.

<span id="an_140:9">140:9</span> Keep me from the snare, which they have
laid for me, and from the stumblingblocks of them that work iniquity.

<span id="an_140:10">140:10</span> The wicked shall fall in his net: I
am alone until I pass.

<span id="an_141:1">141:1</span> Of understanding for David. A prayer
when he was in the cave. \[1 Kings 24\].

<span id="an_141:2">141:2</span> I cried to the Lord with my voice: with
my voice I made supplication to the Lord.

<span id="an_141:3">141:3</span> In his sight I pour out my prayer, and
before him I declare my trouble:

<span id="an_141:4">141:4</span> When my spirit failed me, then thou
newest my paths.

<span id="an_141:5">141:5</span> I looked on my right hand, and beheld,
and there was no one that would know me. Flight hath failed me: and
there is no one that hath regard to my soul.

<span id="an_141:6">141:6</span> I cried to thee, O Lord: I said: Thou
art my hope, my portion in the land of the living.

<span id="an_141:7">141:7</span> Attend to my supplication: for I am
brought very low. Deliver me from my persecutors; for they are stronger
than I.

<span id="an_141:8">141:8</span> Bring my soul out of prison, that I may
praise thy name: the just wait for me, until thou reward me.

<span id="an_142:1">142:1</span> Hear, O Lord, my prayer: give ear to my
supplication in thy truth: hear me in thy justice.

<span id="an_142:2">142:2</span> And enter not into judgment with thy
servant: for in thy sight no man living shall be justified.

<span id="an_142:3">142:3</span> For the enemy hath persecuted my soul:
he hath brought down my life to the earth. He hath made me to dwell in
darkness as those that have been dead of old:

<span id="an_142:4">142:4</span> and my spirit is in anguish within me:
my heart within me is troubled.

<span id="an_142:5">142:5</span> I remembered the days of old, I
meditated on all thy works: I meditated upon the works of thy hands.

<span id="an_142:6">142:6</span> I stretched forth my hands to thee: my
soul is as earth without water unto thee.

<span id="an_142:7">142:7</span> Hear me speedily, O Lord: my spirit
hath fainted away. Turn not away thy face from me, lest I be like unto
them that go down into the pit.

<span id="an_142:8">142:8</span> Cause me to hear thy mercy in the
morning; for in thee have I hoped. Make the way known to me, wherein I
should walk: for I have lifted up my soul to thee.

<span id="an_142:9">142:9</span> Deliver me from my enemies, O Lord, to
thee have I fled:

<span id="an_142:10">142:10</span> teach me to do thy will, for thou art
my God. Thy good spirit shall lead me into the right land:

<span id="an_142:11">142:11</span> for thy name's sake, O Lord, thou
wilt quicken me in thy justice. Thou wilt bring my soul out of trouble:

<span id="an_142:12">142:12</span> and in thy mercy thou wilt destroy my
enemies. And thou wilt cut off all them that afflict my soul: for I am
thy servant.

<span id="an_143:1">143:1</span> Blessed be the Lord my God, who
teacheth my hands to fight, and my fingers to war.

<span id="an_143:2">143:2</span> My mercy, and my refuge: my support,
and my deliverer: My protector, and I have hoped in him: who subdueth my
people under me.

<span id="an_143:3">143:3</span> Lord, what is man, that thou art made
known to him? or the son of man, that thou makest account of him?

<span id="an_143:4">143:4</span> Man is like to vanity: his days pass
away like a shadow.

<span id="an_143:5">143:5</span> Lord, bow down thy heavens and descend:
touch the mountains and they shall smoke.

<span id="an_143:6">143:6</span> Send forth lightning, and thou shalt
scatter them: shoot out thy arrows, and thou shalt trouble them.

<span id="an_143:7">143:7</span> Put forth thy hand from on high, take
me out, and deliver me from many waters: from the hand of strange
children:

<span id="an_143:8">143:8</span> Whose mouth hath spoken vanity: and
their right hand is the right hand of iniquity.

<span id="an_143:9">143:9</span> To thee, O God, I will sing a new
canticle: on the psaltery and an instrument of ten strings I will sing
praises to thee.

<span id="an_143:10">143:10</span> Who givest salvation to kings: who
hast redeemed thy servant David from the malicious sword:

<span id="an_143:11">143:11</span> Deliver me, And rescue me out of the
hand of strange children; whose mouth hath spoken vanity: and their
right hand is the right hand of iniquity:

<span id="an_143:12">143:12</span> Whose sons are as new plants in their
youth: Their daughters decked out, adorned round about after the
similitude of a temple:

<span id="an_143:13">143:13</span> Their storehouses full, flowing out
of this into that. Their sheep fruitful in young, abounding in their
goings forth:

<span id="an_143:14">143:14</span> their oxen fat. There is no breach of
wall, nor passage, nor crying out in their streets.

<span id="an_143:15">143:15</span> They have called the people happy,
that hath these things: but happy is that people whose God is the Lord.

<span id="an_144:1">144:1</span> I will extol thee, O God my king: and I
will bless thy name for ever; yea, for ever and ever.

<span id="an_144:2">144:2</span> Every day I will bless thee: and I will
praise thy name for ever; yea, for ever and ever.

<span id="an_144:3">144:3</span> Great is the Lord, and greatly to be
praised: and of his greatness there is no end.

<span id="an_144:4">144:4</span> Generation and generation shall praise
thy works: and they shall declare thy power.

<span id="an_144:5">144:5</span> They shall speak of the magnificence of
the glory of thy holiness: and shall tell thy wondrous works.

<span id="an_144:6">144:6</span> And they shall speak of the might of
thy terrible acts: and shall declare thy greatness.

<span id="an_144:7">144:7</span> They shall publish the memory of the
abundance of thy sweetness: and shall rejoice in thy justice.

<span id="an_144:8">144:8</span> The Lord is gracious and merciful:
patient and plenteous in mercy.

<span id="an_144:9">144:9</span> The Lord is sweet to all: and his
tender mercies are over all his works.

<span id="an_144:10">144:10</span> Let all thy works, O lord, praise
thee: and let thy saints bless thee.

<span id="an_144:11">144:11</span> They shall speak of the glory of thy
kingdom: and shall tell of thy power:

<span id="an_144:12">144:12</span> To make thy might known to the sons
of men: and the glory of the magnificence of thy kingdom.

<span id="an_144:13">144:13</span> Thy kingdom is a kingdom of all ages:
and thy dominion endureth throughout all generations.

<span id="an_144:14">144:14</span> The Lord lifteth up all that fall:
and setteth up all that are cast down.

<span id="an_144:15">144:15</span> The eyes of all hope in thee, O Lord:
and thou givest them meat in due season.

<span id="an_144:16">144:16</span> Thou openest thy hand, and fillest
with blessing every living creature.

<span id="an_144:17">144:17</span> The Lord is just in all his ways: and
holy in all his works.

<span id="an_144:18">144:18</span> The Lord is nigh unto all them that
call upon him: to all that call upon him in truth.

<span id="an_144:19">144:19</span> He will do the will of them that fear
him: and he will hear their prayer, and save them.

<span id="an_144:20">144:20</span> The Lord keepeth all them that love
him; but all the wicked he will destroy.

<span id="an_144:21">144:21</span> My mouth shall speak the praise of
the Lord: and let all flesh bless thy holy name for ever; yea, for ever
and ever.

<span id="an_145:1">145:1</span> Alleluia, of Aggeus and Zacharias.

<span id="an_145:2">145:2</span> Praise the Lord, O my soul, in my life
I will praise the Lord: I will sing to my God as long as I shall be. Put
not your trust in princes:

<span id="an_145:3">145:3</span> in the children of men, in whom there
is no salvation.

<span id="an_145:4">145:4</span> His spirit shall go forth, and he shall
return into his earth: in that day all their thoughts shall perish.

<span id="an_145:5">145:5</span> Blessed is he who hath the God of Jacob
for his helper, whose hope is in the Lord his God:

<span id="an_145:6">145:6</span> who made heaven and earth, the sea, and
all things that are in them.

<span id="an_145:7">145:7</span> Who keepeth truth for ever: who
executeth judgment for them that suffer wrong: who giveth food to the
hungry. The Lord looseth them that are fettered:

<span id="an_145:8">145:8</span> the Lord enlighteneth the blind. The
Lord lifteth up them that are cast down: the Lord loveth the just.

<span id="an_145:9">145:9</span> The Lord keepeth the strangers, he will
support the fatherless and the widow: and the ways of sinners he will
destroy.

<span id="an_145:10">145:10</span> The Lord shall reign for ever: thy
God, O Sion, unto generation and generation.

<span id="an_146:1">146:1</span> Praise ye the Lord, because psalm is
good: to our God be joyful and comely praise.

<span id="an_146:2">146:2</span> The Lord buildeth up Jerusalem: he will
gather together the dispersed of Israel.

<span id="an_146:3">146:3</span> Who healeth the broken of heart, and
bindeth up their bruises.

<span id="an_146:4">146:4</span> Who telleth the number of the stars:
and calleth them all by their names.

<span id="an_146:5">146:5</span> Great is our Lord, and great is his
power: and of his wisdom there is no number.

<span id="an_146:6">146:6</span> The Lord lifteth up the meek, and
bringeth the wicked down even to the ground.

<span id="an_146:7">146:7</span> Sing ye to the Lord with praise: sing
to our God upon the harp.

<span id="an_146:8">146:8</span> Who covereth the heaven with clouds,
and prepareth rain for the earth. Who maketh grass to grow on the
mountains, and herbs for the service of men.

<span id="an_146:9">146:9</span> Who giveth to beasts their food: and to
the young ravens that call upon him.

<span id="an_146:10">146:10</span> He shall not delight in the strength
of the horse: nor take pleasure in the legs of a man.

<span id="an_146:11">146:11</span> The Lord taketh pleasure in them that
fear him: and in them that hope in his mercy.

<span id="an_147:12">147:12</span> Praise the Lord, O Jerusalem: praise
thy God, O Sion.

<span id="an_147:13">147:13</span> Because he hath strengthened the
bolts of thy gates, he hath blessed thy children within thee.

<span id="an_147:14">147:14</span> Who hath placed peace in thy borders:
and filleth thee with the fat of corn.

<span id="an_147:15">147:15</span> Who sendeth forth his speech to the
earth: his word runneth swiftly.

<span id="an_147:16">147:16</span> Who giveth snow like wool: scattereth
mists like ashes.

<span id="an_147:17">147:17</span> He sendeth his crystal like morsels:
who shall stand before the face of his cold?

<span id="an_147:18">147:18</span> He shall send out his word, and shall
melt them: his wind shall blow, and the waters shall run.

<span id="an_147:19">147:19</span> Who declareth his word to Jacob: his
justices and his judgments to Israel.

<span id="an_147:20">147:20</span> He hath not done in like manner to
every nation: and his judgments he hath not made manifest to them.
Alleluia.

<span id="an_148:1">148:1</span> Praise ye the Lord from the heavens:
praise ye him in the high places.

<span id="an_148:2">148:2</span> Praise ye him , all his angels: praise
ye him, all his hosts.

<span id="an_148:3">148:3</span> Praise ye him, O sun and moon: praise
him, all ye stars and light.

<span id="an_148:4">148:4</span> Praise him, ye heavens of heavens: and
let all the waters that are above the heavens

<span id="an_148:5">148:5</span> praise the name of the Lord. For he
spoke, and they were made: he commanded, and they were created.

<span id="an_148:6">148:6</span> He hath established them for ever, and
for ages of ages: he hath made a decree, and it shall not pass away.

<span id="an_148:7">148:7</span> Praise the Lord from the earth, ye
dragons, and all ye deeps:

<span id="an_148:8">148:8</span> Fire, hail, snow, ice, stormy winds
which fulfil his word:

<span id="an_148:9">148:9</span> Mountains and all hills, fruitful trees
and all cedars:

<span id="an_148:10">148:10</span> Beasts and all cattle: serpents and
feathered fowls:

<span id="an_148:11">148:11</span> Kings of the earth and all people:
princes and all judges of the earth:

<span id="an_148:12">148:12</span> Young men and maidens: let the old
with the younger, praise the name of the Lord:

<span id="an_148:13">148:13</span> for his name alone is exalted.

<span id="an_148:14">148:14</span> The praise of him is above heaven and
earth: and he hath exalted the horn of his people. A hymn to all his
saints: to the children of Israel, a people approaching to him.
Alleluia.

<span id="an_149:1">149:1</span> Sing ye to the Lord a new canticle: let
his praise be in the church of the saints.

<span id="an_149:2">149:2</span> Let Israel rejoice in him that made
him: and let the children of Sion be joyful in their king.

<span id="an_149:3">149:3</span> Let them praise his name in choir: let
them sing to him with the timbrel and the psaltery.

<span id="an_149:4">149:4</span> For the Lord is well pleased with his
people: and he will exalt the meek unto salvation.

<span id="an_149:5">149:5</span> The saints shall rejoice in glory: they
shall be joyful in their beds.

<span id="an_149:6">149:6</span> The high praise of God shall be in
their mouth: and two-edged swords in their hands:

<span id="an_149:7">149:7</span> To execute vengeance upon the nations,
chastisements among the people:

<span id="an_149:8">149:8</span> To bind their kings with fetters, and
their nobles with manacles of iron.

<span id="an_149:9">149:9</span> To execute upon them the judgment that
is written: this glory is to all his saints. Alleluia.

<span id="an_150:1">150:1</span> Praise ye the Lord in his holy places:
praise ye him in the firmament of his power.

<span id="an_150:2">150:2</span> Praise ye him for his mighty acts:
praise ye him according to the multitude of his greatness.

<span id="an_150:3">150:3</span> Praise him with sound of trumpet:
praise him with psaltery and harp.

<span id="an_150:4">150:4</span> Praise him with timbrel and choir:
praise him with strings and organs.

<span id="an_150:5">150:5</span> Praise him on high sounding cymbals:
praise him on cymbals of joy: let every spirit praise the Lord.
Alleluia.
